::hangnum
1806\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthī assarathe datvā, nāriyo ca alaṅkatā;
::

::gathalast
Esa vessantaro rājā, samhā raṭṭhā nirajjati.
::

::hangnum
1807\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāsi yaṃ bhiṃsanakaṃ, tadāsi lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahādāne padinnamhi, medanī sampakampatha.
::

::hangnum
1808\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāsi yaṃ bhiṃsanakaṃ, tadāsi lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ pañjalikato rājā, samhā raṭṭhā nirajjatī’’ti.
::

Tattha **sivikaññā**ti bhikkhave, phussatiyā paridevitasaddaṃ sutvā sabbāpi sañjayassa sivirañño itthiyo samāgatā hutvā pakkanduṃ parideviṃsu. **Vessantaranivesane**ti tattha itthīnaṃ pakkanditasaddaṃ sutvā vessantarassapi nivesane tatheva pakkanditvā dvīsu rājakulesu keci sakabhāvena saṇṭhātuṃ asakkontā vātavegena sampamathitā sālā viya patitvā parivattantā parideviṃsu. **Tato ratyā vivasāne**ti bhikkhave, tato tassā rattiyā accayena sūriye uggate dānaveyyāvatikā ‘‘dānaṃ paṭiyādita’’nti rañño ārocayiṃsu. Atha vessantaro rājā pātova nhatvā sabbālaṅkārappaṭimaṇḍito sādurasabhojanaṃ bhuñjitvā mahājanaparivuto sattasatakaṃ mahādānaṃ dātuṃ dānaggaṃ upāgami.

**Dethā**ti {pb:V:7.0259} tattha gantvā saṭṭhisahassaamacce āṇāpento evamāha. **Vāruṇi**nti ‘‘majjadānaṃ nāma nipphala’’nti jānāti, evaṃ santepi ‘‘surāsoṇḍā dānaggaṃ patvā ‘vessantarassa dānagge suraṃ na labhimhā’ti vattuṃ mā labhantū’’ti dāpesi. **Vanibbake**ti vanibbakajanesu kañci ekampi mā viheṭhayittha. **Paṭipūjitā**ti mayā pūjitā hutvā yathā maṃ thomayamānā gacchanti{pb:P:6.0504}, tathā tumhe karothāti vadati.

Iti so suvaṇṇālaṅkārānaṃ suvaṇṇadhajānaṃ hemajālappaṭicchannānaṃ hatthīnaṃ sattasatāni ca, tathārūpānaññeva assānaṃ sattasatāni ca, sīhacammādīhi parikkhittānaṃ nānāratanavicitrānaṃ suvaṇṇadhajānaṃ rathānaṃ sattasatāni, sabbālaṅkārappaṭimaṇḍitānaṃ uttamarūpadharānaṃ khattiyakaññādīnaṃ itthīnaṃ sattasatāni, suvinītānaṃ susikkhitānaṃ dāsānaṃ sattasatāni, tathā {pb:M:7.0272} dāsīnaṃ sattasatāni, varausabhajeṭṭhakānaṃ kuṇḍopadohinīnaṃ dhenūnaṃ sattasatāni, aparimāṇāni pānabhojanānīti sattasatakaṃ mahādānaṃ adāsi. Tasmiṃ evaṃ dānaṃ dadamāne jetuttaranagaravāsino khattiyabrāhmaṇavessasuddādayo ‘‘sāmi, vessantara siviraṭṭhavāsino taṃ ‘dānaṃ detī’ti pabbājenti, tvaṃ puna dānameva desī’’ti parideviṃsu. Tena vuttaṃ –

::hangnum
1809\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athettha vattatī saddo, tumulo bheravo mahā;
::

::gathalast
Dānena taṃ nīharanti, puna dānaṃ adā tuva’’nti.
::

Dānapaṭiggāhakā pana dānaṃ gahetvā ‘‘idāni kira vessantaro rājā amhe anāthe katvā araññaṃ pavisissati, ito paṭṭhāya kassa santikaṃ gamissāmā’’ti chinnapādā viya patantā āvattantā parivattantā mahāsaddena parideviṃsu. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1810\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te su mattā kilantāva, sampatanti vanibbakā;
::

::gathalast
Nikkhamante mahārāje, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane’’ti.
::

Tattha **te su mattā**ti **su**-kāro nipātamatto, te vanibbakāti attho. **Mattā kilantāvā**ti mattā viya kilantā viya ca hutvā. **Sampatantī**ti parivattitvā bhūmiyaṃ patanti. **Acchecchuṃ vatā**ti chindiṃsu, **vatā**ti nipātamattaṃ. **Yathā**ti yena kāraṇena. **Atiyakkhā**ti bhūtavijjā ikkhaṇikāpi. **Vassavarā**ti uddhaṭabījā orodhapālakā. **Vacanatthenā**ti vacanakāraṇena. **Samhā raṭṭhā nirajjatī**ti attano raṭṭhā niggacchati. **Gāmaṇīyehī**ti hatthācariyehi. **Ājānīyevā**ti jātisampanne{pb:V:7.0260}. **Gāmaṇīyehī**ti assācariyehi. **Illiyācāpadhāribhī**ti illiyañca cāpañca dhārentehi. **Dīpe athopi veyyagghe**ti dīpicammabyagghacammaparikkhitte. **Ekamekā rathe ṭhitā**ti so kira ekamekaṃ itthiratanaṃ rathe ṭhapetvā aṭṭhaaṭṭhavaṇṇadāsīhi parivutaṃ katvā adāsi.

**Nikkharajjūhī**ti suvaṇṇasuttamayehi pāmaṅgehi. **Āḷārapamhā**ti visālakkhigaṇḍā. **Hasulā**ti mhitapubbaṅgamakathā. **Susaññā**ti sussoṇiyo. **Tanumajjhimā**ti {pb:M:7.0273} karatalamiva tanumajjhimabhāgā. Tadā pana devatāyo jambudīpatale rājūnaṃ ‘‘vessantaro rājā mahādānaṃ detī’’ti ārocayiṃsu, tasmā te khattiyā devatānubhāvenāgantvā tā gaṇhitvā pakkamiṃsu. **Kaṃsupadhāraṇā**ti idha **kaṃsa**nti rajatassa nāmaṃ, rajatamayena khīrapaṭicchanabhājanena saddhiññeva adāsīti attho. **Padinnamhī**ti dīyamāne. **Sampakampathā**ti dānatejena kampittha. **Yaṃ pañjalikato**ti yaṃ so vessantaro rājā mahādānaṃ datvā añjaliṃ paggayha attano dānaṃ namassamāno ‘‘sabbaññutaññāṇassa me idaṃ paccayo hotū’’ti pañjalikato ahosi, tadāpi bhīsanakameva ahosi, tasmiṃ khaṇe pathavī kampitthāti attho. **Nirajjatī**ti evaṃ katvā niggacchatiyeva, na koci naṃ nivāretīti attho.

Apica {pb:P:6.0505} kho tassa dānaṃ dadantasseva sāyaṃ ahosi. So attano nivesanameva gantvā ‘‘mātāpitaro vanditvā sve gamissāmī’’ti cintetvā alaṅkatarathena mātāpitūnaṃ vasanaṭṭhānaṃ gato. Maddīdevīpi ‘‘ahaṃ sāminā saddhiṃ gantvā mātāpitaro anujānāpessāmī’’ti teneva saddhiṃ gatā. Mahāsatto pitaraṃ vanditvā attano gamanabhāvaṃ kathesi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1811\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āmantayittha rājānaṃ, sañjayaṃ dhamminaṃ varaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Avaruddhasi maṃ deva, vaṅkaṃ gacchāmi pabbataṃ.
::

::hangnum
1812\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye hi keci mahārāja, bhūtā ye ca bhavissare;
::

::gathalast
Atittāyeva kāmehi, gacchanti yamasādhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1813\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāhaṃ sake abhissasiṃ, yajamāno sake pure;
::

::gathalast
Sivīnaṃ vacanatthena, samhā raṭṭhā nirajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1814\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aghaṃ {pb:V:7.0261} taṃ paṭisevissaṃ, vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe;
::

::gatha2
Khaggadīpinisevite, ahaṃ puññāni karomi;
::

::gathalast
Tumhe paṅkamhi sīdathā’’ti.
::

Tattha **dhamminaṃ vara**nti dhammikarājūnaṃ antare uttamaṃ. **Avaruddhasī**ti raṭṭhā nīharasi. **Bhūtā**ti atītā. **Bhavissare**ti ye ca anāgate bhavissanti{pb:M:7.0274}, paccuppanne ca nibbattā. **Yamasādhana**nti yamarañño āṇāpavattiṭṭhānaṃ. **Svāhaṃ sake abhissasi**nti so ahaṃ attano nagaravāsinoyeva pīḷesiṃ. Kiṃ karonto? **Yajamāno sake pure**ti. Pāḷiyaṃ pana ‘‘so aha’’nti likhitaṃ. **Nirajjaha**nti nikkhanto ahaṃ. **Aghaṃ ta**nti yaṃ araññe vasantena paṭisevitabbaṃ dukkhaṃ, taṃ paṭisevissāmi. **Paṅkamhī**ti tumhe pana kāmapaṅkamhi sīdathāti vadati.

Iti mahāsatto imāhi catūhi gāthāhi pitarā saddhiṃ kathetvā mātu santikaṃ gantvā vanditvā pabbajjaṃ anujānāpento evamāha –

::hangnum
1815\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anujānāhi maṃ amma, pabbajjā mama ruccati;
::

::gatha2
Svāhaṃ sake abhissasiṃ, yajamāno sake pure;
::

::gathalast
Sivīnaṃ vacanatthena, samhā raṭṭhā nirajjahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1816\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aghaṃ {pb:P:6.0506} taṃ paṭisevissaṃ, vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe;
::

::gatha2
Khaggadīpinisevite, ahaṃ puññāni karomi;
::

::gathalast
Tumhe paṅkamhi sīdathā’’ti.
::

Taṃ sutvā phussatī āha –

::hangnum
1817\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anujānāmi taṃ putta, pabbajjā te samijjhatu;
::

::gatha2
Ayañca maddī kalyāṇī, susaññā tanumajjhimā;
::

Acchataṃ saha puttehi, kiṃ araññe karissatī’’ti.

Tattha **samijjhatū**ti jhānena samiddhā hotu. **Acchata**nti acchatu, idheva hotūti vadati.

Vessantaro {pb:V:7.0262} āha –

::hangnum
1818\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ akāmā dāsimpi, araññaṃ netumussahe;
::

::gathalast
Sace icchati anvetu, sace nicchati acchatū’’ti.
::

Tattha **akāmā**ti amma, kiṃ nāmetaṃ kathetha, ahaṃ anicchāya dāsimpi netuṃ na ussahāmīti.

Tato puttassa kathaṃ sutvā rājā suṇhaṃ yācituṃ paṭipajji. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1819\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:M:7.0275} suṇhaṃ mahārājā, yācituṃ paṭipajjatha;
::

::gathalast
Mā candanasamācāre, rajojallaṃ adhārayi.
::

::hangnum
1820\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā kāsiyāni dhāretvā, kusacīraṃ adhārayi;
::

::gathalast
Dukkho vāso araññasmiṃ, mā hi tvaṃ lakkhaṇe gamī’’ti.
::

Tattha **paṭipajjathā**ti bhikkhave, puttassa kathaṃ sutvā rājā suṇhaṃ yācituṃ paṭipajji. **Candanasamācāre**ti lohitacandanena parikiṇṇasarīre. **Mā hi tvaṃ lakkhaṇe gamī**ti subhalakkhaṇena samannāgate mā tvaṃ araññaṃ gamīti.

::hangnum
1821\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamabravi rājaputtī, maddī sabbaṅgasobhanā;
::

::gathalast
Nāhaṃ taṃ sukhamiccheyyaṃ, yaṃ me vessantaraṃ vinā’’ti.
::

Tattha **tamabravī**ti taṃ sasuraṃ abravi.

::hangnum
1822\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamabravi mahārājā, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano;
::

::gathalast
Iṅgha maddi nisāmehi, vane ye honti dussahā.
::

::hangnum
1823\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahū {pb:V:7.0263} kīṭā paṭaṅgā ca, makasā madhumakkhikā;
::

::gathalast
Tepi taṃ tattha hiṃ seyyuṃ, taṃ te dukkhataraṃ siyā.
::

::hangnum
1824\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Apare {pb:P:6.0507} passa santāpe, nadīnupanisevite;
::

::gathalast
Sappā ajagarā nāma, avisā te mahabbalā.
::

::hangnum
1825\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te manussaṃ migaṃ vāpi, api māsannamāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parikkhipitvā bhogehi, vasamānenti attano.
::

::hangnum
1826\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññepi kaṇhajaṭino, acchā nāma aghammigā;
::

::gathalast
Na tehi puriso diṭṭho, rukkhamāruyha muccati.
::

::hangnum
1827\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅghaṭṭayantā siṅgāni, tikkhaggātippahārino;
::

::gathalast
Mahiṃsā vicarantettha, nadiṃ sotumbaraṃ pati.
::

::hangnum
1828\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvā migānaṃ yūthānaṃ, gavaṃ sañcarataṃ vane;
::

::gathalast
Dhenuva vacchagiddhāva, kathaṃ maddi karissasi.
::

::hangnum
1829\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Disvā {pb:M:7.0276} sampatite ghore, dumaggesu plavaṅgame;
::

::gathalast
Akhettaññāya te maddi, bhavissate mahabbhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1830\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yā tvaṃ sivāya sutvāna, muhuṃ uttasayī pure;
::

::gathalast
Sā tvaṃ vaṅkamanuppattā, kathaṃ maddi karissasi.
::

::hangnum
1831\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ṭhite majjhanhike kāle, sannisinnesu pakkhisu;
::

::gathalast
Saṇateva brahāraññaṃ, tattha kiṃ gantumicchasī’’ti.
::

Tattha **tamabravī**ti taṃ suṇhaṃ abravi. **Apare passa santāpe**ti aññepi santāpe bhayajanake pekkha. **Nadīnupanisevite**ti nadīnaṃ upanisevite āsannaṭṭhāne, nadīkūle vasanteti attho. **Avisā**ti nibbisā. **Api māsanna**nti āsannaṃ attano sarīrasamphassaṃ āgatanti attho. **Aghammigā**ti {pb:V:7.0264} aghakarā migā, dukkhāvahā migāti attho. **Nadiṃ sotumbaraṃ patī**ti sotumbarāya nāma nadiyā tīre. **Yūthāna**nti yūthāni, ayameva vā pāṭho. **Dhenuva vacchagiddhāvā**ti tava dārake apassantī vacchagiddhā dhenu viya kathaṃ karissasi. **Va**-kāro panettha nipātamattova. **Sampatite**ti sampatante. **Ghore**ti bhīsanake virūpe. **Plavaṅgame**ti makkaṭe. **Akhettaññāyā**ti araññabhūmiakusalatāya. **Bhavissate**ti bhavissati. **Sivāya sutvānā**ti siṅgāliyā saddaṃ sutvā. **Muhu**nti punappunaṃ. **Uttasayī**ti uttasasi. **Saṇatevā**ti nadati viya saṇantaṃ viya bhavissati.

::hangnum
1832\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamabravi rājaputtī, maddī sabbaṅgasobhanā;
::

::gatha2
Yāni etāni akkhāsi, vane paṭibhayāni me;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāni abhisambhossaṃ, gacchaññeva rathesabha.
::

::hangnum
1833\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāsaṃ {pb:P:6.0508} kusaṃ poṭakilaṃ, usiraṃ muñcapabbajaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Urasā panudahissāmi, nassa hessāmi dunnayā.
::

::hangnum
1834\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahūhi vata cariyāhi, kumārī vindate patiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Udarassuparodhena, gohanuveṭhanena ca.
::

::hangnum
1835\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aggissa {pb:M:7.0277} pāricariyāya, udakummujjanena ca;
::

::gathalast
Vedhabyaṃ kaṭukaṃ loke, gacchaññeva rathesabha.
::

::hangnum
1836\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Apissā hoti appatto, ucchiṭṭhamapi bhuñjituṃ;
::

::gatha2
Yo naṃ hatthe gahetvāna, akāmaṃ parikaḍḍhati;
::

::gathalast
Vedhabyaṃ kaṭukaṃ loke, gacchaññeva rathesabha.
::

::hangnum
1837\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kesaggahaṇamukkhepā, bhūmyā ca parisumbhanā;
::

::gatha2
Datvā ca no pakkamati, bahuṃ dukkhaṃ anappakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vedhabyaṃ kaṭukaṃ loke, gacchaññeva rathesabha.
::

::hangnum
1838\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sukkacchavī {pb:V:7.0265} vedhaverā, datvā subhagamānino;
::

::gatha2
Akāmaṃ parikaḍḍhanti, ulūkaññeva vāyasā;
::

::gathalast
Vedhabyaṃ kaṭukaṃ loke, gacchaññeva rathesabha.
::

::hangnum
1839\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Api ñātikule phīte, kaṃsapajjotane vasaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Nevātivākyaṃ na labhe, bhātūhi sakhinīhipi;
::

::gathalast
Vedhabyaṃ kaṭukaṃ loke, gacchaññeva rathesabha.
::

::hangnum
1840\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Naggā nadī anudakā, naggaṃ raṭṭhaṃ arājakaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Itthīpi vidhavā naggā, yassāpi dasa bhātaro;
::

::gathalast
Vedhabyaṃ kaṭukaṃ loke, gacchaññeva rathesabha.
::

::hangnum
1841\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhajo rathassa paññāṇaṃ, dhūmo paññāṇamaggino;
::

::gatha2
Rājā raṭṭhassa paññāṇaṃ, bhattā paññāṇamitthiyā;
::

::gathalast
Vedhabyaṃ kaṭukaṃ loke, gacchaññeva rathesabha.
::

::hangnum
1842\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yā daliddī daliddassa, aḍḍhā aḍḍhassa kittimā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ ve devā pasaṃsanti, dukkarañhi karoti sā.
::

::hangnum
1843\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāmikaṃ anubandhissaṃ, sadā kāsāyavāsinī;
::

::gathalast
Pathabyāpi abhijjantyā, vedhabyaṃ kaṭukitthiyā.
::

::hangnum
1844\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Api sāgarapariyantaṃ, bahuvittadharaṃ mahiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānāratanaparipūraṃ, nicche vessantaraṃ vinā.
::

::hangnum
1845\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ {pb:M:7.0278} nu tāsaṃ hadayaṃ, sukharā vata itthiyo;
::

::gathalast
Yā sāmike dukkhitamhi, sukhamicchanti attano.
::

::hangnum
1846\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nikkhamante mahārāje, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ anubandhissaṃ, sabbakāmadado hi me’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:V:7.0266} **tamabravī**ti bhikkhave, maddī rañño vacanaṃ sutvā taṃ rājānaṃ abravi. **Abhisambhossa**nti sahissāmi adhivāsessāmi. **Poṭakila**nti poṭakilatiṇaṃ. **Panudahissāmī**ti dvedhā katvā vessantarassa purato gamissāmi. **Udarassuparodhenā**ti upavāsena khudādhivāsena. **Gohanuveṭhanena cā**ti visālakaṭiyo onatapassā ca itthiyo sāmikaṃ labhantīti {pb:P:6.0509} katvā gohanunā kaṭiphalakaṃ koṭṭāpetvā veṭhanena ca passāni onāmetvā kumārikā patiṃ labhati. **Kaṭuka**nti asātaṃ. **Gacchaññevā**ti gamissāmiyeva.

**Apissā hoti appatto**ti tassā vidhavāya ucchiṭṭhakampi bhuñjituṃ ananucchavikova. **Yo na**nti yo nīcajacco taṃ vidhavaṃ anicchamānaññeva hatthe gahetvā kaḍḍhati. **Kesaggahaṇamukkhepā, bhūmyā ca parisumbhanā**ti asāmikaṃ itthiṃ hatthapādehi kesaggahaṇaṃ, ukkhepā, bhūmiyaṃ pātananti etāni avamaññanāni katvā atikkamanti. **Datvā cā**ti asāmikāya itthiyā evarūpaṃ bahuṃ anappakaṃ dukkhaṃ parapuriso datvā ca **no pakkamati** nirāsaṅko olokentova tiṭṭhati.

**Sukkacchavī**ti nhānīyacuṇṇena uṭṭhāpitacchavivaṇṇā. **Vedhaverā**ti vidhavitthikāmā purisā. **Datvā**ti kiñcideva appamattakaṃ dhanaṃ datvā. **Subhagamānino**ti mayaṃ subhagāti maññamānā. **Akāma**nti taṃ vidhavaṃ asāmikaṃ akāmaṃ. **Ulūkaññeva vāyasā**ti kākā viyaulūkaṃ parikaḍḍhanti. **Kaṃsapajjotane**ti suvaṇṇabhājanābhāya pajjotante. **Vasa**nti evarūpepi ñātikule vasamānā. **Nevātivākyaṃ na labhe**ti ‘‘ayaṃ itthī nissāmikā, yāvajīvaṃ amhākaññeva bhāro jāto’’tiādīni vacanāni vadantehi bhātūhipi sakhinīhipi ativākyaṃ garahavacanaṃ neva na labhati. **Paññāṇa**nti pākaṭabhāvakāraṇaṃ.

**Yā** {pb:M:7.0279} **daliddī daliddassā**ti deva, kittisampannā yā itthī attano sāmikassa daliddassa dukkhappattakāle sayampi daliddī samānā dukkhāva hoti, tassa aḍḍhakāle teneva saddhiṃ aḍḍhā sukhappattā hoti, taṃ ve devā pasaṃsanti. Abhijjantyāti abhijjantiyā. Sacepi hi itthiyā sakalapathavī na bhijjati, tāya sakalāya pathaviyā sāva issarā hoti, tathāpi vedhabyaṃ kaṭukamevāti attho. Sukharā vata itthiyoti suṭṭhu kharā vata itthiyo.

::hangnum
1847\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamabravi {pb:V:7.0267} mahārājā, maddiṃ sabbaṅgasobhanaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Ime te daharā puttā, jālī kaṇhājinā cubho;
::

::gathalast
Nikkhippa lakkhaṇe gaccha, mayaṃ te posayāmase’’ti.
::

Tattha **jālī kaṇhājinā cubho**ti jālī ca kaṇhājinā cāti ubho. **Nikkhippā**ti ime nikkhipitvā gacchāhīti.

::hangnum
1848\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamabravi rājaputtī, maddī sabbaṅgasobhanā;
::

::gatha2
Piyā me puttakā deva, jālī kaṇhājinā cubho;
::

::gathalast
Tyamhaṃ tattha ramessanti, araññe jīvasokina’’nti.
::

Tattha **tyamha**nti te dārakā amhākaṃ tattha araññe. **Jīvasokina**nti avigatasokānaṃ hadayaṃ ramayissantīti attho.

::hangnum
1849\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamabravi {pb:P:6.0510} mahārājā, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano;
::

::gatha2
Sālīnaṃ odanaṃ bhutvā, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rukkhaphalāni bhuñjantā, kathaṃ kāhanti dārakā.
::

::hangnum
1850\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhutvā satapale kaṃse, sovaṇṇe satarājike;
::

::gathalast
Rukkhapattesu bhuñjantā, kathaṃ kāhanti dārakā.
::

::hangnum
1851\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāsiyāni ca dhāretvā, khomakoṭumbarāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Kusacīrāni dhārentā, kathaṃ kāhanti dārakā.
::

::hangnum
1852\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vayhāhi pariyāyitvā, sivikāya rathena ca;
::

::gathalast
Pattikā paridhāvantā, kathaṃ kāhanti dārakā.
::

::hangnum
1853\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kūṭāgāre {pb:M:7.0280} sayitvāna, nivāte phusitaggaḷe;
::

::gathalast
Sayantā rukkhamūlasmiṃ, kathaṃ kāhanti dārakā.
::

::hangnum
1854\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pallaṅkesu {pb:V:7.0268} sayitvāna, gonake cittasanthate;
::

::gathalast
Sayantā tiṇasanthāre, kathaṃ kāhanti dārakā.
::

::hangnum
1855\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gandhakena vilimpitvā, agarucandanena ca;
::

::gathalast
Rajojallāni dhārentā, kathaṃ kāhanti dārakā.
::

::hangnum
1856\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cāmaramorahatthehi, bījitaṅgā sukhedhitā;
::

::gathalast
Phuṭṭhā ḍaṃsehi makasehi, kathaṃ kāhanti dārakā’’ti.
::

Tattha **palasate kaṃse**ti palasatena katāya kañcanapātiyā. **Gonake cittasanthate**ti mahāpiṭṭhiyaṃ kāḷakojave ceva vicittake santhare ca. **Cāmaramorahatthehī**ti cāmarehi ceva morahatthehi ca bījitaṅgā.

Evaṃ tesaṃ sallapantānaññeva ratti vibhāyi, sūriyo uggañchi. Mahāsattassa catusindhavayuttaṃ alaṅkatarathaṃ ānetvā rājadvāre ṭhapayiṃsu. Maddīpi sassusasure vanditvā sesitthiyo apaloketvā dve putte ādāya vessantarato paṭhamataraṃ gantvā rathe aṭṭhāsi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1857\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamabravi rājaputtī, maddī sabbaṅgasobhanā;
::

::gatha2
Mā deva paridevesi, mā ca tvaṃ vimano ahu;
::

::gathalast
Yathā mayaṃ bhavissāma, tathā hessanti dārakā.
::

::hangnum
1858\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna pakkāmi, maddī sabbaṅgasobhanā;
::

::gathalast
Sivimaggena anvesi, putte ādāya lakkhaṇā’’ti.
::

Tattha **sivimaggenā**ti sivirañño gantabbamaggena. **Anvesī**ti taṃ agamāsi, pāsādā otaritvā rathaṃ abhiruhīti attho.

::hangnum
1859\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:P:6.0511} vessantaro rājā, dānaṃ datvāna khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Pitu mātu ca vanditvā, katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1860\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catuvāhiṃ {pb:V:7.0269}{pb:M:7.0281} rathaṃ yuttaṃ, sīghamāruyha sandanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ādāya puttadārañca, vaṅkaṃ pāyāsi pabbata’’nti.
::

Tattha **tato**ti bhikkhave, tassā maddiyā rathaṃ abhiruhitvā ṭhitakāle. **Datvā**ti hiyyo dānaṃ datvā. **Katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇa**nti padakkhiṇañca katvā. **Na**nti nipātamattaṃ.

::hangnum
1861\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato vessantaro rājā, yenāsi bahuko jano;
::

::gathalast
Āmanta kho taṃ gacchāma, arogā hontu ñātayo’’ti.
::

Tassattho – bhikkhave, tato vessantaro rājā yattha ‘‘vessantaraṃ rājānaṃ passissāmā’’ti bahuko jano ṭhito āsi, tattha rathaṃ pesetvā mahājanaṃ āpucchanto ‘‘āmanta kho taṃ gacchāma, arogā hontu ñātayo’’ti āha. Tattha **ta**nti nipātamattaṃ. Bhikkhave, tato vessantaro rājā ñātake āha – ‘‘tumhe āmantetvā mayaṃ gacchāma, tumhe sukhitā hotha nidukkhā’’ti.

Evaṃ mahāsatto mahājanaṃ āmantetvā ‘‘appamattā hotha, dānādīni puññāni karothā’’ti tesaṃ ovaditvā pakkāmi. Gacchante pana bodhisatte mātā ‘‘putto me dānavittako dānaṃ detū’’ti ābharaṇehi saddhiṃ sattaratanapūrāni sakaṭāni ubhosu passesu pesesi. Sopi attano kāyāruḷhameva ābharaṇabhaṇḍaṃ omuñcitvā sampattayācakānaṃ aṭṭhārasa vāre datvā avasesaṃ sabbaṃ adāsi. So nagarā nikkhamitvā ca nivattitvā oloketukāmo ahosi. Athassa manaṃ paṭicca rathappamāṇaṭṭhāne mahāpathavī bhijjitvā kulālacakkaṃ viya parivattitvā rathaṃ nagarābhimukhaṃ akāsi. So mātāpitūnaṃ vasanaṭṭhānaṃ olokesi. Tena kāraṇena pathavīkampo ahosi. Tena vuttaṃ –

::gatha2
‘‘Nikkhamitvāna nagarā, nivattitvā vilokite;
::

::gathalast
Tadāpi pathavī kampi, sineruvanavaṭaṃsakā’’ti. (cariyā. 1.93);
::

Sayaṃ {pb:M:7.0282} pana oloketvā maddimpi olokāpetuṃ gāthamāha –

::hangnum
1862\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iṅgha {pb:V:7.0270} maddi nisāmehi, rammarūpaṃva dissati;
::

::gathalast
Āvāsaṃ siviseṭṭhassa, pettikaṃ bhavanaṃ mamā’’ti.
::

Tattha **nisāmehī**ti olokehi.

Atha {pb:P:6.0512} mahāsatto sahajāte saṭṭhisahassaamacce ca sesajanañca nivattāpetvā rathaṃ pājento maddiṃ āha – ‘‘bhadde, sace pacchato yācakā āgacchanti, upadhāreyyāsī’’ti. Sāpi olokentī nisīdi. Athassa sattasatakaṃ mahādānaṃ sampāpuṇituṃ asakkontā cattāro brāhmaṇā nagaraṃ āgantvā ‘‘kuhiṃ vessantaro rājā’’ti pucchitvā ‘‘dānaṃ datvā gato’’ti vutte ‘‘kiñci gahetvā gato’’ti pucchitvā ‘‘rathena gato’’ti sutvā ‘‘asse naṃ yācissāmā’’ti anubandhiṃsu. Atha maddī te āgacchante disvā ‘‘yācakā āgacchanti, devā’’ti ārocesi. Mahāsatto rathaṃ ṭhapesi. Te āgantvā asse yāciṃsu. Mahāsatto asse adāsi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1863\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ brāhmaṇā anvagamuṃ, te naṃ asse ayācisuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yācito paṭipādesi, catunnaṃ caturo haye’’ti.
::

Assesu pana dinnesu rathadhuraṃ ākāseyeva aṭṭhāsi. Atha brāhmaṇesu gatamattesuyeva cattāro devaputtā rohiccamigavaṇṇena āgantvā rathadhuraṃ sampaṭicchitvā agamaṃsu. Mahāsatto tesaṃ devaputtabhāvaṃ ñatvā imaṃ gāthamāha –

::hangnum
1864\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iṅgha maddi nisāmehi, cittarūpaṃva dissati;
::

::gathalast
Migarohiccavaṇṇena, dakkhiṇassā vahanti ma’’nti.
::

Tattha **dakkhiṇassā**ti susikkhitā assā viya maṃ vahanti.

Atha naṃ evaṃ gacchantaṃ aparo brāhmaṇo āgantvā rathaṃ yāci. Mahāsatto puttadāraṃ otāretvā tassa rathaṃ adāsi. Rathe pana dinne devaputtā antaradhāyiṃsu. Rathassa dinnabhāvaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1865\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athettha {pb:V:7.0271}{pb:M:7.0283} pañcamo āgā, so taṃ rathamayācatha;
::

::gathalast
Tassa taṃ yācitodāsi, na cassupahato mano.
::

::hangnum
1866\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato vessantaro rājā, oropetvā sakaṃ janaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Assāsayi assarathaṃ, brāhmaṇassa dhanesino’’ti.
::

Tattha **athetthā**ti atha tasmiṃ vane. **Na cassupahato mano**ti na cassa mano olīno. **Assāsayī**ti paritosento niyyādesi.

Tato {pb:P:6.0513} paṭṭhāya pana te sabbepi pattikāva ahesuṃ. Atha mahāsatto maddiṃ avoca –

::hangnum
1867\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tvaṃ maddi kaṇhaṃ gaṇhāhi, lahu esā kaniṭṭhikā;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ jāliṃ gahessāmi, garuko bhātiko hi so’’ti.
::

Evañca pana vatvā ubhopi khattiyā dve dārake aṅkenādāya pakkamiṃsu. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1868\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājā kumāramādāya, rājaputtī ca dārikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sammodamānā pakkāmuṃ, aññamaññaṃ piyaṃvadā’’ti.
::

::centre
Dānakaṇḍavaṇṇanā niṭṭhitā.
::

::centre
Vanapavesanakaṇḍavaṇṇanā
::

Te paṭipathaṃ āgacchante manusse disvā ‘‘kuhiṃ vaṅkapabbato’’ti pucchanti. Manussā ‘‘dūre’’ti vadanti. Tena vuttaṃ –

::hangnum
1869\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadi keci manujā enti, anumagge paṭipathe;
::

::gathalast
Maggaṃ te paṭipucchāma, ‘kuhiṃ vaṅkatapabbato’.
::

::hangnum
1870\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te {pb:V:7.0272} tattha amhe passitvā, kalunaṃ paridevayuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dukkhaṃ te paṭivedenti, dūre vaṅkatapabbato’’ti.
::

Maggassa ubhosu passesu vividhaphaladhārino rukkhe disvā dārakā kandanti. Mahāsattassānubhāvena phaladhārino rukkhā onamitvā hatthasamphassaṃ {pb:M:7.0284} āgacchanti. Tato supakkaphalāphalāni uccinitvā tesaṃ deti. Taṃ disvā maddī acchariyaṃ pavedesi. Tena vuttaṃ –

::hangnum
1871\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadi passanti pavane, dārakā phaline dume;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ phalānaṃ hetumhi, uparodanti dārakā.
::

::hangnum
1872\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rodante dārake disvā, ubbiddhā vipulā dumā;
::

::gathalast
Sayamevonamitvāna, upagacchanti dārake.
::

::hangnum
1873\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ accherakaṃ disvā, abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sādhukāraṃ pavattesi, maddī sabbaṅgasobhanā.
::

::hangnum
1874\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accheraṃ vata lokasmiṃ, abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vessantarassa tejena, sayamevonatā dumā’’ti.
::

Jetuttaranagarato {pb:P:6.0514} suvaṇṇagiritālo nāma pabbato pañca yojanāni, tato kontimārā nāma nadī pañca yojanāni, tato añcaragiri nāma pabbato pañca yojanāni, tato dunniviṭṭhabrāhmaṇagāmo nāma pañca yojanāni, tato mātulanagaraṃ dasa yojanāni. Iti taṃ maggaṃ jetuttaranagarato tiṃsayojanaṃ hoti. Devatā taṃ maggaṃ saṃkhipiṃsu. Te ekadivaseneva mātulanagaraṃ pāpuṇiṃsu. Tena vuttaṃ –

::hangnum
1875\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅkhipiṃsu pathaṃ yakkhā, anukampāya dārake;
::

::gathalast
Nikkhantadivaseneva, cetaraṭṭhaṃ upāgamu’’nti.
::

Upagacchantā {pb:V:7.0273} ca pana jetuttaranagarato pātarāsasamaye nikkhamitvā sāyanhasamaye cetaraṭṭhe mātulanagaraṃ pattā. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1876\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te gantvā dīghamaddhānaṃ, cetaraṭṭhaṃ upāgamuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Iddhaṃ phītaṃ janapadaṃ, bahumaṃsasurodana’’nti.
::

Tadā mātulanagare saṭṭhi khattiyasahassāni vasanti. Mahāsatto antonagaraṃ apavisitvā nagaradvāreyeva sālāyaṃ nisīdi. Athassa maddī {pb:M:7.0285} bodhisattassa pādesu rajaṃ puñchitvā pāde sambāhitvā ‘‘vessantarassa āgatabhāvaṃ jānāpessāmī’’ti sālāto nikkhamitvā tassa cakkhupathe sālādvāre aṭṭhāsi. Nagaraṃ pavisantiyo ca nikkhamantiyo ca itthiyo taṃ disvā parivāresuṃ. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1877\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cetiyo parivāriṃsu, disvā lakkhaṇamāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sukhumālī vata ayyā, pattikā paridhāvati.
::

::hangnum
1878\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vayhāhi pariyāyitvā, sivikāya rathena ca;
::

::gathalast
Sājja maddī araññasmiṃ, pattikā paridhāvatī’’ti.
::

Tattha **lakkhaṇamāgata**nti lakkhaṇasampannaṃ maddiṃ āgataṃ. **Paridhāvatī**ti evaṃ sukhumālī hutvā pattikāva vicarati. **Pariyāyitvā**ti jetuttaranagare vicaritvā. **Sivikāyā**ti suvaṇṇasivikāya.

Mahājano {pb:P:6.0515} maddiñca vessantarañca dve putte cassa anāthāgamanena āgate disvā gantvā rājūnaṃ ācikkhi. Saṭṭhisahassā rājāno rodantā paridevantā tassa santikaṃ āgamaṃsu. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1879\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ disvā cetapāmokkhā, rodamānā upāgamuṃ;
::

::gatha2
Kacci nu deva kusalaṃ, kacci deva anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kacci pitā arogo te, sivīnañca anāmayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1880\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko {pb:V:7.0274} te balaṃ mahārāja, ko nu te rathamaṇḍalaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Anassako arathako, dīghamaddhānamāgato;
::

::gathalast
Kaccāmittehi pakato, anuppattosimaṃ disa’’nti.
::

Tattha **disvā**ti dūratova passitvā. **Cetapāmokkhā**ti cetarājāno. **Upāgamu**nti upasaṅkamiṃsu. **Kusala**nti ārogyaṃ. **Anāmaya**nti niddukkhabhāvaṃ. **Ko te bala**nti kuhiṃ tava balakāyo. **Rathamaṇḍala**nti yenāsi rathena āgato, so kuhinti pucchanti. **Anassako**ti assavirahito. **Arathako**ti ayānako. **Dīghamaddhānamāgato**ti dīghamaggaṃ āgato. **Pakato**ti abhibhūto.

Atha {pb:M:7.0286} nesaṃ mahāsatto attano āgatakāraṇaṃ kathento āha –

::hangnum
1881\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kusalañceva me sammā, atho sammā anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atho pitā arogo me, sivīnañca anāmayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1882\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahañhi kuñjaraṃ dajjaṃ, īsādantaṃ urūḷhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khettaññuṃ sabbayuddhānaṃ, sabbasetaṃ gajuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1883\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṇḍukambalasañchannaṃ, pabhinnaṃ sattumaddanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dantiṃ savālabījaniṃ, setaṃ kelāsasādisaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1884\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sasetacchattaṃ saupādheyyaṃ, sāthabbanaṃ sahatthipaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aggayānaṃ rājavāhiṃ, brāhmaṇānaṃ adāsahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1885\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmiṃ me sivayo kuddhā, pitā cupahatomano;
::

::gatha2
Avaruddhasi maṃ rājā, vaṅkaṃ gacchāmi pabbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Okāsaṃ sammā jānātha, vane yattha vasāmase’’ti.
::

Tattha **tasmiṃ me**ti tasmiṃ kāraṇe mayhaṃ sivayo kuddhā. **Upahatomano**ti upahatacitto kuddhova {pb:V:7.0275} maṃ raṭṭhā pabbājesi. **Yatthā**ti yasmiṃ vane mayaṃ vaseyyāma, tattha vasanokāsaṃ jānāthāti.

Te rājāno āhaṃsu –

::hangnum
1886\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ {pb:P:6.0516} te mahārāja, atho te adurāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Issarosi anuppatto, yaṃ idhatthi pavedaya.
::

::hangnum
1887\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sākaṃ bhisaṃ madhuṃ maṃsaṃ, suddhaṃ sālīnamodanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paribhuñja mahārāja, pāhuno nosi āgato’’ti.
::

Tattha **pavedayā**ti kathehi, sabbaṃ paṭiyādetvā dassāma. **Bhisa**nti bhisamūlaṃ, yaṃkiñci kandajātaṃ vā.

Vessantaro āha –

::hangnum
1888\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭiggahitaṃ yaṃ dinnaṃ, sabbassa agghiyaṃ kataṃ;
::

::gatha2
Avaruddhasi maṃ rājā, vaṅkaṃ gacchāmi pabbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Okāsaṃ sammā jānātha, vane yattha vasāmase’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:M:7.0287} **paṭiggahita**nti sabbametaṃ tumhehi dinnaṃ mayā ca paṭiggahitameva hotu, sabbassa tumhehi mayhaṃ agghiyaṃ nivedanaṃ kataṃ. Rājā pana maṃ avaruddhasi raṭṭhā pabbājesi, tasmā vaṅkameva gamissāmi, tasmiṃ me araññe vasanaṭṭhānaṃ jānāthāti.

Te rājāno āhaṃsu –

::hangnum
1889\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idheva tāva acchassu, cetaraṭṭhe rathesabha;
::

::gathalast
Yāva cetā gamissanti, rañño santika yācituṃ.
::

::hangnum
1890\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nijjhāpetuṃ {pb:V:7.0276} mahārājaṃ, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Taṃ taṃ cetā purakkhatvā, patītā laddhapaccayā;
::

::gathalast
Parivāretvāna gacchanti, evaṃ jānāhi khattiyā’’ti.
::

Tattha **rañño santika yācitu**nti rañño santikaṃ yācanatthāya gamissanti. **Nijjhāpetu**nti tumhākaṃ niddosabhāvaṃ jānāpetuṃ. **Laddhapaccayā**ti laddhapatiṭṭhā. **Gacchantī**ti gamissanti.

Mahāsatto āha –

::hangnum
1891\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā vo ruccittha gamanaṃ, rañño santika yācituṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nijjhāpetuṃ mahārājaṃ, rājāpi tattha nissaro.
::

::hangnum
1892\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accuggatā hi sivayo, balaggā negamā ca ye;
::

::gathalast
Te vidhaṃsetumicchanti, rājānaṃ mama kāraṇā’’ti.
::

Tattha **tatthā**ti tasmiṃ mama niddosabhāvaṃ nijjhāpane rājāpi anissaro. **Accuggatā**ti atikuddhā. **Balaggā**ti balakāyā. **Vidhaṃsetu**nti rajjato nīharituṃ. **Rājāna**nti rājānampi.

Te {pb:P:6.0517} rājāno āhaṃsu –

::hangnum
1893\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace esā pavattettha, raṭṭhasmiṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhana;
::

::gathalast
Idheva rajjaṃ kārehi, cetehi parivārito.
::

::hangnum
1894\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iddhaṃ phītañcidaṃ raṭṭhaṃ, iddho janapado mahā;
::

::gathalast
Matiṃ karohi tvaṃ deva, rajjassa manusāsitu’’nti.
::

Tattha {pb:M:7.0288} **sace esā pavattetthā**ti sace etasmiṃ raṭṭhe esā pavatti. **Rajjassa manusāsitu**nti rajjaṃ samanusāsituṃ, ayameva vā pāṭho.

Vessantaro āha –

::hangnum
1895\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:7.0277} me chando mati atthi, rajjassa anusāsituṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pabbājitassa raṭṭhasmā, cetaputtā suṇātha me.
::

::hangnum
1896\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atuṭṭhā sivayo āsuṃ, balaggā negamā ca ye;
::

::gathalast
Pabbājitassa raṭṭhasmā, cetā rajjebhisecayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
1897\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asammodiyampi vo assa, accantaṃ mama kāraṇā;
::

::gathalast
Sivīhi bhaṇḍanaṃ cāpi, viggaho me na ruccati.
::

::hangnum
1898\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athassa bhaṇḍanaṃ ghoraṃ, sampahāro anappako;
::

::gathalast
Ekassa kāraṇā mayhaṃ, hiṃseyya bahuko jano.
::

::hangnum
1899\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭiggahitaṃ yaṃ dinnaṃ, sabbassa agghiyaṃ kataṃ;
::

::gatha2
Avaruddhasi maṃ rājā, vaṅkaṃ gacchāmi pabbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Okāsaṃ sammā jānātha, vane yattha vasāmase’’ti.
::

Tattha **cetā rajjebhisecayu**nti cetaraṭṭhavāsino kira vessantaraṃ rajje abhisiñciṃsūti tumhākampi te atuṭṭhā āsuṃ. **Asammodiya**nti asāmaggiyaṃ. **Assā**ti bhaveyya. **Athassā**ti atha mayhaṃ ekassa kāraṇā tumhākaṃ bhaṇḍanaṃ bhavissatīti.

Evaṃ mahāsatto anekapariyāyena yācitopi rajjaṃ na icchi. Athassa te cetarājāno mahantaṃ sakkāraṃ kariṃsu. So nagaraṃ pavisituṃ na icchi. Atha naṃ sālameva alaṅkaritvā sāṇiyā parikkhepaṃ katvā mahāsayanaṃ paññāpetvā sabbe ārakkhaṃ kariṃsu. So ekarattiṃ tehi saṅgahitārakkho sālāyaṃ sayitvā punadivase pātova nhatvā nānaggarasabhojanaṃ bhuñjitvā tehi parivuto nikkhami. Saṭṭhisahassā khattiyā tena saddhiṃ pannarasayojanamaggaṃ gantvā {pb:P:6.0518} vanadvāre ṭhatvā purato pannarasayojanamaggaṃ ācikkhantā āhaṃsu –

::hangnum
1900\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taggha {pb:M:7.0289} te mayamakkhāma, yathāpi kusalā tathā;
::

::gathalast
Rājisī yattha sammanti, āhutaggī samāhitā.
::

::hangnum
1901\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Esa {pb:V:7.0278} selo mahārāja, pabbato gandhamādano;
::

::gathalast
Yattha tvaṃ saha puttehi, saha bhariyāya cacchasi.
::

::hangnum
1902\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ cetā anusāsiṃsu, assunettā rudaṃmukhā;
::

::gathalast
Ito gaccha mahārāja, ujuṃ yenuttarāmukho.
::

::hangnum
1903\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha dakkhisi bhaddante, vepullaṃ nāma pabbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānādumagaṇākiṇṇaṃ, sītacchāyaṃ manoramaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1904\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamatikkamma bhaddante, atha dakkhisi āpagaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nadiṃ ketumatiṃ nāma, gambhīraṃ girigabbharaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1905\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puthulomamacchākiṇṇaṃ, supatitthaṃ mahodakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tattha nhatvā pivitvā ca, assāsetvā saputtake.
::

::hangnum
1906\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha dakkhisi bhaddante, nigrodhaṃ madhupipphalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rammake sikhare jātaṃ, sītacchāyaṃ manoramaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1907\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha dakkhisi bhaddante, nāḷikaṃ nāma pabbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānādijagaṇākiṇṇaṃ, selaṃ kimpurisāyutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1908\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa uttarapubbena, mucalindo nāma so saro;
::

::gathalast
Puṇḍarīkehi sañchanno, setasogandhikehi ca.
::

::hangnum
1909\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So vanaṃ meghasaṅkāsaṃ, dhuvaṃ haritasaddalaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Sīhovāmisapekkhīva, vanasaṇḍaṃ vigāhaya;
::

::gathalast
Puppharukkhehi sañchannaṃ, phalarukkhehi cūbhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1910\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha bindussarā vaggū, nānāvaṇṇā bahū dijā;
::

::gathalast
Kūjantamupakūjanti, utusaṃpupphite dume.
::

::hangnum
1911\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gantvā {pb:V:7.0279} girividuggānaṃ, nadīnaṃ pabhavāni ca;
::

::gathalast
So dakkhisi pokkharaṇiṃ, karañjakakudhāyutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1912\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puthulomamacchākiṇṇaṃ{pb:M:7.0290}, supatitthaṃ mahodakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samañca caturaṃsañca, sāduṃ appaṭigandhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1913\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassā uttarapubbena, paṇṇasālaṃ amāpaya;
::

::gathalast
Paṇṇasālaṃ amāpetvā, uñchācariyāya īhathā’’ti.
::

Tattha **rājisī**ti rājāno hutvā pabbajitā. **Samāhitā**ti ekaggacittā. **Esā**ti dakkhiṇahatthaṃ ukkhipitvā iminā pabbatapādena gacchathāti ācikkhantā vadanti. **Acchasī**ti {pb:P:6.0519} vasissasi. **Āpaga**nti udakavāhanadiāvaṭṭaṃ. **Girigabbhara**nti girīnaṃ kucchito pavattaṃ. **Madhupipphala**nti madhuraphalaṃ. **Rammake**ti ramaṇīye. **Kimpurisāyuta**nti kimpurisehi āyutaṃ parikiṇṇaṃ. **Setasogandhīkehi cā**ti nānappakārehi setuppalehi ceva sogandhikehi ca sañchanno. **Sīhovāmisapekkhīvā**ti āmisaṃ pekkhanto sīho viya.

**Bindussarā**ti sampiṇḍitassarā. **Vaggū**ti madhurassarā. **Kūjantamupakūjantī**ti paṭhamaṃ kūjamānaṃ pakkhiṃ pacchā upakūjanti. **Utusaṃpupphite dume**ti utusamaye pupphite dume nilīyitvā kūjantaṃ upakūjanti. **So dakkhisī**ti so tvaṃ passissasīti attho. **Karañjakakudhāyuta**nti karañjarukkhehi ca kakudharukkhehi ca samparikiṇṇaṃ. **Appaṭigandhiya**nti paṭikūlagandhavirahitaṃ madhurodakaparikiṇṇaṃnānappakārapadumuppalādīhi sañchannaṃ. **Paṇṇasālaṃ amāpayā**ti paṇṇasālaṃ māpeyyāsi. **Amāpetvā**ti māpetvā. **Uñchācariyāya īhathā**ti atha tumhe, deva, uñchācariyāya yāpentā appamattā īhatha, āraddhavīriyā hutvā vihareyyāthāti attho.

Evaṃ te rājāno tassa pannarasayojanamaggaṃ ācikkhitvā taṃ uyyojetvā vessantarassa antarāyabhayassa vinodanatthaṃ ‘‘mā kocideva paccāmitto okāsaṃ labheyyā’’ti cintetvā ekaṃ byattaṃ susikkhitaṃ cetaputtaṃ āmantetvā ‘‘tvaṃ gacchante ca āgacchante ca pariggaṇhāhī’’ti vanadvāre ārakkhaṇatthāya ṭhapetvā sakanagaraṃ gamiṃsu. Vessantaropi saputtadāro gandhamādanapabbataṃ patvā, taṃ divasaṃ tattha vasitvā tato uttarābhimukho vepullapabbatapādena gantvā, ketumatiyā nāma nadiyā tīre nisīditvā vanacarakena dinnaṃ madhumaṃsaṃ khāditvā tassa suvaṇṇasūciṃ datvā {pb:M:7.0291} tattha {pb:V:7.0280} nhatvā pivitvā paṭippassaddhadaratho nadito uttaritvā sānupabbatasikhare ṭhitassa nigrodhassa mūle thokaṃ nisīditvā nigrodhaphalāni khāditvā uṭṭhāya gacchanto nāḷikaṃ nāma pabbataṃ patvā taṃ pariharanto mucalindasaraṃ gantvā sarassa tīrena pubbuttarakaṇṇaṃ patvā, ekapadikamaggena vanaghaṭaṃ pavisitvā taṃ atikkamma girividuggānaṃ nadippabhavānaṃ purato caturaṃsapokkharaṇiṃ pāpuṇi.

Tasmiṃ khaṇe sakko āvajjento ‘‘mahāsatto himavantaṃ paviṭṭho’’ti ñatvā ‘‘tassa vasanaṭṭhānaṃ laddhuṃ vaṭṭatī’’ti cintetvā vissakammaṃ {pb:P:6.0520} pakkosāpetvā ‘‘gaccha, tāta, tvaṃ vaṅkapabbatakujhacchimhi ramaṇīye ṭhāne assamapadaṃ māpetvā ehī’’ti pesesi. So ‘‘sādhu, devā’’ti devalokato otaritvā tattha dve paṇṇasālāyo dve caṅkame rattiṭṭhānadivāṭṭhānāni ca māpetvā caṅkamakoṭiyaṃ tesu tesu ṭhānesu nānāphaladhare rukkhe ca kadalivanāni ca dassetvā sabbe pabbajitaparikkhāre paṭiyādetvā ‘‘ye keci pabbajitukāmā, te ime gaṇhantū’’ti akkharāni likhitvā amanusse ca bheravasadde migapakkhino ca paṭikkamāpetvā sakaṭṭhānameva gato.

Mahāsatto ekapadikamaggaṃ disvā ‘‘pabbajitānaṃ vasanaṭṭhānaṃ bhavissatī’’ti maddiñca putte ca assamapadadvāre ṭhapetvā assamapadaṃ pavisitvā akkharāni oloketvā ‘‘sakkenamhi diṭṭho’’ti ñatvā paṇṇasālaṃ pavisitvā khaggañca dhanuñca apanetvā sāṭake omuñcitvā rattavākacīraṃ nivāsetvā ajinacammaṃ aṃse katvā jaṭāmaṇḍalaṃ bandhitvā isivesaṃ gahetvā kattaradaṇḍaṃ ādāya paṇṇasālato nikkhamitvā pabbajitasiriṃ samubbahanto ‘‘aho sukhaṃ, aho sukhaṃ, pabbajjā me adhigatā’’ti udānaṃ udānetvā caṅkamaṃ āruyha aparāparaṃ caṅkamitvā paccekabuddhasadisena upasamena puttadārānaṃ santikaṃ agamāsi. Maddīpi mahāsattassa pādesu patitvā roditvā teneva saddhiṃ assamapadaṃ pavisitvā attano paṇṇasālaṃ gantvā isivesaṃ gaṇhi. Pacchā puttepi tāpasakumārake kariṃsu. Cattāro khattiyā vaṅkapabbatakucchimhi vasiṃsu. Atha maddī mahāsattaṃ varaṃ yāci ‘‘deva, tumhe phalāphalatthāya vanaṃ agantvā putte gahetvā idheva hotha, ahaṃ phalāphalaṃ āharissāmī’’ti. Tato paṭṭhāya sā araññato phalāphalāni āharitvā tayo jane paṭijaggati.

Bodhisattopi {pb:M:7.0292} taṃ varaṃ yāci ‘‘bhadde, maddi mayaṃ ito paṭṭhāya pabbajitā nāma, itthī ca nāma brahmacariyassa malaṃ, ito paṭṭhāya akāle mama santikaṃ mā āgacchāhī’’ti. Sā ‘‘sādhū’’ti sampaṭicchi. Mahāsattassa mettānubhāvena samantā tiyojane sabbe tiracchānāpi aññamaññaṃ {pb:V:7.0281} mettacittaṃ paṭilabhiṃsu. Maddīdevīpi pātova uṭṭhāya pānīyaparibhojanīyaṃ upaṭṭhāpetvā mukhodakaṃ āharitvā dantakaṭṭhaṃ datvā assamapadaṃ sammajjitvā dve putte pitu santike ṭhapetvā pacchikhaṇittiaṅkusahatthā araññaṃ {pb:P:6.0521} pavisitvā vanamūlaphalāphalāni ādāya pacchiṃ pūretvā sāyanhasamaye araññato āgantvā paṇṇasālāya phalāphalaṃ ṭhapetvā nhatvā putte nhāpesi. Atha cattāropi janā paṇṇasālādvāre nisīditvā phalāphalaṃ paribhuñjanti. Tato maddī putte gahetvā attano paṇṇasālaṃ pāvisi. Iminā niyāmena te pabbatakucchimhi satta māse vasiṃsūti.

::centre
Vanapavesanakaṇḍavaṇṇanā niṭṭhitā.
::

#### Jūjakapabbavaṇṇanā

Tadā kāliṅgaraṭṭhe dunniviṭṭhabrāhmaṇagāmavāsī jūjako nāma brāhmaṇo bhikkhācariyāya kahāpaṇasataṃ labhitvā ekasmiṃ brāhmaṇakule ṭhapetvā puna dhanapariyesanatthāya gato. Tasmiṃ cirāyante brāhmaṇakulā kahāpaṇasataṃ valañjetvā pacchā itarena āgantvā codiyamānā kahāpaṇe dātuṃ asakkontā amittatāpanaṃ nāma dhītaraṃ tassa adaṃsu. So taṃ ādāya kāliṅgaraṭṭhe dunniviṭṭhabrāhmaṇagāmaṃ gantvā vasi. Amittatāpanā sammā brāhmaṇaṃ paricarati. Atha aññe taruṇabrāhmaṇā tassā ācārasampattiṃ disvā ‘‘ayaṃ mahallakabrāhmaṇaṃ sammā paṭijaggati, tumhe pana amhesu kiṃ pamajjathā’’ti attano attano bhariyāyo tajjenti. Tā ‘‘imaṃ amittatāpanaṃ imamhā gāmā palāpessāmā’’ti nadītitthādīsu sannipatitvā taṃ paribhāsiṃsu. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1914\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahu vāsī kaliṅgesu, jūjako nāma brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Tassāsi daharā bhariyā, nāmenāmittatāpanā.
::

::hangnum
1915\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tā {pb:M:7.0293} naṃ tattha gatāvocuṃ, nadiṃ udakahāriyā;
::

::gathalast
Thiyo naṃ paribhāsiṃsu, samāgantvā kutūhalā.
::

::hangnum
1916\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amittā nūna te mātā, amitto nūna te pitā;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1917\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahitaṃ {pb:V:7.0282} vata te ñātī, mantayiṃsu rahogatā;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1918\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amittā vata te ñātī, mantayiṃsu rahogatā;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1919\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dukkaṭaṃ vata te ñātī, mantayiṃsu rahogatā;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1920\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāpakaṃ vata te ñātī, mantayiṃsu rahogatā;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1921\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amanāpaṃ vata te ñātī, mantayiṃsu rahogatā;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1922\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amanāpavāsaṃ {pb:P:6.0522} vasi, jiṇṇena patinā saha;
::

::gathalast
Yā tvaṃ vasasi jiṇṇassa, mataṃ te jīvitā varaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1923\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi nūna tuyhaṃ kalyāṇi, pitā mātā ca sobhane;
::

::gatha2
Aññaṃ bhattāraṃ vindiṃsu, ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1924\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duyiṭṭhaṃ te navamiyaṃ, akataṃ aggihuttakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ jiṇṇassa pādaṃsu, evaṃ dahariyaṃ satiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1925\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samaṇe brāhmaṇe nūna, brahmacariyaparāyaṇe;
::

::gatha2
Sā tvaṃ loke abhisapi, sīlavante bahussute;
::

::gathalast
Yā tvaṃ vasasi jiṇṇassa, evaṃ dahariyā satī.
::

::hangnum
1926\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:7.0283}{pb:M:7.0294} dukkhaṃ ahinā daṭṭhaṃ, na dukkhaṃ sattiyā hataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tañca dukkhañca tibbañca, yaṃ passe jiṇṇakaṃ patiṃ.
::

::hangnum
1927\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Natthi khiḍḍā natthi rati, jiṇṇena patinā saha;
::

::gathalast
Natthi ālāpasallāpo, jagghitampi na sobhati.
::

::hangnum
1928\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yadā ca daharo daharā, mantayanti rahogatā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesaṃ sokā nassanti, ye keci hadayassitā.
::

::hangnum
1929\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Daharā tvaṃ rūpavatī, purisānaṃbhipatthitā;
::

::gathalast
Gaccha ñātikule accha, kiṃ jiṇṇo ramayissatī’’ti.
::

Tattha **ahū**ti ahosi. **Vāsī kaliṅgesū**ti kāliṅgaraṭṭhesu dunniviṭṭhabrāhmaṇagāmavāsī. **Tā naṃ tattha gatāvocu**nti tattha gāme tā itthiyo nadītitthe udakahārikā hutvā gatā naṃ avocuṃ. **Thiyo naṃ paribhāsiṃsū**ti itthiyo na aññaṃ kiñci avocuṃ, atha kho naṃ paribhāsiṃsu. **Kutūhalā**ti kotūhalajātā viya hutvā. **Samāgantvā**ti samantā parikkhipitvā. **Dahariyaṃ sati**nti dahariṃ taruṇiṃ sobhaggappattaṃ samānaṃ. **Jiṇṇassā**ti jarājiṇṇassa gehe. **Duyiṭṭhaṃ te navamiya**nti tava navamiyaṃ yāgaṃ duyiṭṭhaṃ bhavissati, so te yāgapiṇḍo paṭhamaṃ mahallakakākena gahito bhavissati. ‘‘Duyiṭṭhā te navamiyā’’tipi pāṭho, navamiyā tayā duyiṭṭhā bhavissatīti attho. **Akataṃ aggihuttaka**nti aggijuhanampi tayā akataṃ bhavissati. **Abhisapī**ti samaṇabrāhmaṇe samitapāpe vā bāhitapāpe vā akkosi. Tassa te pāpassa idaṃ phalanti adhippāyeneva āhaṃsu. **Jagghitampi na sobhatī**ti khaṇḍadante vivaritvā hasantassa mahallakassa hasitampi na sobhati. **Sabbesaṃ sokā nassantī**ti sabbe etesaṃ sokā vinassanti. **Kiṃ jiṇṇo**ti ayaṃ jiṇṇo taṃ pañcahi kāmaguṇehi kathaṃ ramayissatīti.

Sā tāsaṃ santikā paribhāsaṃ labhitvā udakaghaṭaṃ ādāya rodamānā gharaṃ gantvā ‘‘kiṃ bhoti rodasī’’ti brāhmaṇena puṭṭhā tassa ārocentī imaṃ gāthamāha –

::hangnum
1930\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:P:6.0523}{pb:M:7.0295} te brāhmaṇa gacchāmi, nadiṃ udakahāriyā;
::

::gathalast
Thiyo maṃ paribhāsanti, tayā jiṇṇena brāhmaṇā’’ti.
::

Tassattho {pb:V:7.0284} – brāhmaṇa, tayā jiṇṇena maṃ itthiyo paribhāsanti, tasmā ito paṭṭhāya tava udakahārikā hutvā nadiṃ na gacchāmīti.

Jūjako āha –

::hangnum
1931\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā me tvaṃ akarā kammaṃ, mā me udakamāhari;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ udakamāhissaṃ, mā bhoti kupitā ahū’’ti.
::

Tattha **udakamāhissa**nti bhoti ahaṃ udakaṃ āharissāmi.

Brāhmaṇī āha –

::hangnum
1932\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ tamhi kule jātā, yaṃ tvaṃ udakamāhare;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ brāhmaṇa jānāhi, na te vacchāmahaṃ ghare.
::

::hangnum
1933\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace me dāsaṃ dāsiṃ vā, nānayissasi brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ brāhmaṇa jānāhi, na te vacchāmi santike’’ti.
::

Tattha **nāha**nti brāhmaṇa, yamhi kule sāmiko kammaṃ karoti, nāhaṃ tattha jātā. **Yaṃ tva**nti tasmā yaṃ udakaṃ tvaṃ āharissasi, na mayhaṃ tena attho.

Jūjako āha –

::hangnum
1934\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Natthi me sippaṭhānaṃ vā, dhanaṃ dhaññañca brāhmaṇi;
::

::gatha2
Kutohaṃ dāsaṃ dāsiṃ vā, ānayissāmi bhotiyā;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ bhotiṃ upaṭṭhissaṃ, mā bhoti kupitā ahū’’ti.
::

Brāhmaṇī āha –

::hangnum
1935\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ehi te ahamakkhissaṃ, yathā me vacanaṃ sutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Esa vessantaro rājā, vaṅke vasati pabbate.
::

::hangnum
1936\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ tvaṃ gantvāna yācassu, dāsaṃ dāsiñca brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
So te dassati yācito, dāsaṃ dāsiñca khattiyo’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:V:7.0285}{pb:M:7.0296} **ehi te ahamakkhissa**nti ahaṃ te ācikkhissāmi. Idaṃ sā devatādhiggahitā hutvā āha.

Jūjako āha –

::hangnum
1937\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jiṇṇohamasmi dubbalo, dīgho caddhā suduggamo;
::

::gatha2
Mā bhoti paridevesi, mā ca tvaṃ vimanā ahu;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ bhotiṃ upaṭṭhissaṃ, mā bhoti kupitā ahū’’ti.
::

Tattha **jiṇṇohamasmī**ti bhadde, ahaṃ jiṇṇo amhi, kathaṃ gamissāmīti.

Brāhmaṇī {pb:P:6.0524} āha –

::hangnum
1938\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā agantvā saṅgāmaṃ, ayuddhova parājito;
::

::gathalast
Evameva tuvaṃ brahme, agantvāva parājito.
::

::hangnum
1939\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace me dāsaṃ dāsiṃ vā, nānayissasi brāhmaṇa;
::

::gatha2
Evaṃ brāhmaṇa jānāhi, na te vacchāmahaṃ ghare;
::

::gathalast
Amanāpaṃ te karissāmi, taṃ te dukkhaṃ bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
1940\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nakkhatte utupubbesu, yadā maṃ dakkhisilaṅkataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aññehi saddhiṃ ramamānaṃ, taṃ te dukkhaṃ bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
1941\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adassanena mayhaṃ te, jiṇṇassa paridevato;
::

::gathalast
Bhiyyo vaṅkā ca palitā, bahū hessanti brāhmaṇā’’ti.
::

Tattha **amanāpaṃ te**ti vessantarassa santikaṃ gantvā dāsaṃ vā dāsiṃ vā anāharantassa tava aruccanakaṃ kammaṃ karissāmi. **Nakkhatte utupubbesū**ti nakkhattayogavasena vā channaṃ utūnaṃ tassa tassa pubbavasena vā pavattesu chaṇesu.

Taṃ sutvā brāhmaṇo bhīto ahosi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1942\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:V:7.0286} so brāhmaṇo bhīto, brāhmaṇiyā vasānugo;
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭito kāmarāgena, brāhmaṇiṃ etadabravi.
::

::hangnum
1943\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pātheyyaṃ {pb:M:7.0297} me karohi tvaṃ, saṃkulyā saguḷāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Madhupiṇḍikā ca sukatāyo, sattubhattañca brāhmaṇi.
::

::hangnum
1944\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ānayissaṃ methunake, ubho dāsakumārake;
::

::gathalast
Te taṃ paricarissanti, rattindivamatanditā’’ti.
::

Tattha **aṭṭito**ti upadduto pīḷito. **Saguḷāni cā**ti saguḷapūve ca. **Sattubhatta**nti baddhasattuabaddhasattuñceva puṭabhattañca. **Methunake**ti jātigottakulapadesehi sadise. **Dāsakumārake**ti tava dāsatthāya kumārake.

Sā khippaṃ pātheyyaṃ paṭiyādetvā brāhmaṇassa ārocesi. So gehe dubbalaṭṭhānaṃ thiraṃ katvā dvāraṃ saṅkharitvā araññā dārūni āharitvā ghaṭena udakaṃ āharitvā gehe sabbabhājanāni pūretvā tattheva tāpasavesaṃ gahetvā ‘‘bhadde, ito paṭṭhāya vikāle mā nikkhami, yāva mamāgamanā appamattā hohī’’ti ovaditvā upāhanaṃ āruyha pātheyyapasibbakaṃ aṃse laggetvā amittatāpanaṃ padakkhiṇaṃ katvā assupuṇṇehi nettehi roditvā pakkāmi. Tamatthaṃ {pb:P:6.0525} pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1945\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvā brahmabandhu, paṭimuñci upāhanā;
::

::gathalast
Tato so mantayitvāna, bhariyaṃ katvā padakkhiṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1946\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pakkāmi so ruṇṇamukho, brāhmaṇo sahitabbato;
::

::gathalast
Sivīnaṃ nagaraṃ phītaṃ, dāsapariyesanaṃ cara’’nti.
::

Tattha **ruṇṇamukho**ti rudaṃmukho. **Sahitabbato**ti samādinnavato, gahitatāpasavesoti attho. **Cara**nti dāsapariyesanaṃ caranto sivīnaṃ nagaraṃ ārabbha pakkāmi.

So {pb:V:7.0287} taṃ nagaraṃ gantvā sannipatitaṃ janaṃ ‘‘vessantaro kuhi’’nti pucchati. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1947\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So tattha gantvā avaca, ye tatthāsuṃ samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Kuhiṃ vessantaro rājā, kattha passemu khattiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1948\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te {pb:M:7.0298} janā taṃ avaciṃsu, ye tatthāsuṃ samāgatā;
::

::gatha2
Tumhehi brahme pakato, atidānena khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Pabbājito sakā raṭṭhā, vaṅke vasati pabbate.
::

::hangnum
1949\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tumhehi brahme pakato, atidānena khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Ādāya puttadārañca, vaṅke vasati pabbate’’ti.
::

Tattha **pakato**ti upadduto pīḷito attano nagare vasituṃ alabhitvā idāni vaṅkapabbate vasati.

Evaṃ ‘‘tumhe amhākaṃ rājānaṃ nāsetvā punapi āgatā idha tiṭṭhathā’’ti te leḍḍudaṇḍādihatthā brāhmaṇaṃ anubandhiṃsu. So devatādhiggahito hutvā vaṅkapabbatamaggameva gaṇhi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1950\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So codito brāhmaṇiyā, brāhmaṇo kāmagiddhimā;
::

::gatha2
Aghaṃ taṃ paṭisevittha, vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe;
::

::gathalast
Khaggadīpinisevite.
::

::hangnum
1951\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ādāya beḷuvaṃ daṇḍaṃ, aggihuttaṃ kamaṇḍaluṃ;
::

::gathalast
So pāvisi brahāraññaṃ, yattha assosi kāmadaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1952\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ paviṭṭhaṃ brahāraññaṃ, kokā naṃ parivārayuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vikkandi so vippanaṭṭho, dūre panthā apakkami.
::

::hangnum
1953\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:V:7.0288} so brāhmaṇo gantvā, bhogaluddho asaññato;
::

::gathalast
Vaṅkassorohaṇe naṭṭhe, imā gāthā abhāsathā’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:P:6.0526} **aghaṃ ta**nti taṃ mahājanena anubandhanadukkhañceva vanapariyogāhanadukkhañca. **Aggihutta**nti aggijuhanakaṭacchuṃ. **Kokā naṃ parivārayu**nti so hi araññaṃ pavisitvā vaṅkapabbatagāmimaggaṃ ajānanto maggamūḷho hutvā araññe vicari. Atha naṃ ārakkhaṇatthāya nisinnassa cetaputtassa sunakhā parivārayiṃsūti attho. **Vikkandi so**ti so ekarukkhaṃ āruyha mahantena ravena kandi. **Vippanaṭṭho**ti vinaṭṭhamaggo. **Dūre panthā**ti vaṅkapabbatagāmipanthato dūre pakkāmi. **Bhogaluddho**ti bhogaratto. **Asaññato**ti dussīlo. **Vaṅkassorohaṇe naṭṭhe**ti vaṅkapabbatassa gamanamagge vinaṭṭhe.

So {pb:M:7.0299} sunakhehi parivārito rukkhe nisinnova imā gāthā abhāsatha –

::hangnum
1954\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ko rājaputtaṃ nisabhaṃ, jayantamaparājitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhaye khemassa dātāraṃ, ko me vessantaraṃ vidū.
::

::hangnum
1955\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo yācataṃ patiṭṭhāsi, bhūtānaṃ dharaṇīriva;
::

::gathalast
Dharaṇūpamaṃ mahārājaṃ, ko me vessantaraṃ vidū.
::

::hangnum
1956\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo yācataṃ gatī āsi, savantīnaṃva sāgaro;
::

::gathalast
Sāgarūpamaṃ mahārājaṃ, ko me vessantaraṃ vidū.
::

::hangnum
1957\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kalyāṇatitthaṃ sucimaṃ, sītūdakaṃ manoramaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Puṇḍarīkehi sañchannaṃ, yuttaṃ kiñjakkhareṇunā;
::

::gathalast
Rahadūpamaṃ mahārājaṃ, ko me vessantaraṃ vidū.
::

::hangnum
1958\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assatthaṃva pathe jātaṃ, sītacchāyaṃ manoramaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Santānaṃ visametāraṃ, kilantānaṃ paṭiggahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tathūpamaṃ mahārājaṃ, ko me vessantaraṃ vidū.
::

::hangnum
1959\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nigrodhaṃva {pb:V:7.0289} pathe jātaṃ, sītacchāyaṃ manoramaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Santānaṃ visametāraṃ, kilantānaṃ paṭiggahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tathūpamaṃ mahārājaṃ, ko me vessantaraṃ vidū.
::

::hangnum
1960\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ambaṃ iva pathe jātaṃ, sītacchāyaṃ manoramaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Santānaṃ visametāraṃ, kilantānaṃ paṭiggahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tathūpamaṃ mahārājaṃ, ko me vessantaraṃ vidū.
::

::hangnum
1961\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sālaṃ iva pathe jātaṃ, sītacchāyaṃ manoramaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Santānaṃ visametāraṃ, kilantānaṃ paṭiggahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tathūpamaṃ mahārājaṃ, ko me vessantaraṃ vidū.
::

::hangnum
1962\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dumaṃ iva pathe jātaṃ, sītacchāyaṃ manoramaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Santānaṃ visametāraṃ, kilantānaṃ paṭiggahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tathūpamaṃ mahārājaṃ, ko me vessantaraṃ vidū.
::

::hangnum
1963\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evañca {pb:M:7.0300} me vilapato, paviṭṭhassa brahāvane;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ jānanti yo vajjā, nandiṃ so janaye mama.
::

::hangnum
1964\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evañca me vilapato, paviṭṭhassa brahāvane;
::

::gatha2
Ahaṃ jānanti yo vajjā, tāya so ekavācāya;
::

::gathalast
Pasave puññaṃ anappaka’’nti.
::

Tattha {pb:P:6.0527} **jayanta**nti maccheracittaṃ vijayantaṃ. **Ko me vessantaraṃ vidū**ti ko mayhaṃ vessantaraṃ ācikkheyyāti vadati. **Patiṭṭhāsī**ti patiṭṭhā āsi. **Santāna**nti parissantānaṃ. **Kilantāna**nti maggakilantānaṃ. **Paṭiggaha**nti paṭiggāhakaṃ patiṭṭhābhūtaṃ. **Ahaṃ jānanti yo vajjā**ti ahaṃ vessantarassa vasanaṭṭhānaṃ jānāmīti yo vadeyyāti attho.

Tassa taṃ paridevasaddaṃ sutvā ārakkhaṇatthāya ṭhapito cetaputto migaluddako hutvā araññe vicaranto ‘‘ayaṃ brāhmaṇo vessantarassa vasanaṭṭhānatthāya paridevati, na kho panesa dhammatāya {pb:V:7.0290} āgato, maddiṃ vā dārake vā yācissati, idheva naṃ māressāmī’’ti tassa santikaṃ gantvā ‘‘brāhmaṇa, na te jīvitaṃ dassāmī’’ti dhanuṃ āropetvā ākaḍḍhitvā tajjesi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
1965\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa ceto paṭissosi, araññe luddako caraṃ;
::

::gatha2
Tumhehi brahme pakato, atidānena khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Pabbājito sakā raṭṭhā, vaṅke vasati pabbate.
::

::hangnum
1966\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tumhehi brahme pakato, atidānena khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Ādāya puttadārañca, vaṅke vasati pabbate.
::

::hangnum
1967\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akiccakārī dummedho, raṭṭhā pavanamāgato;
::

::gathalast
Rājaputtaṃ gavesanto, bako macchamivodake.
::

::hangnum
1968\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa tyāhaṃ na dassāmi, jīvitaṃ idha brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Ayañhi te mayā nunno, saro pissati lohitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1969\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Siro te vajjhayitvāna, hadayaṃ chetvā sabandhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Panthasakuṇaṃ yajissāmi, tuyhaṃ maṃsena brāhmaṇa.
::

::hangnum
1970\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuyhaṃ {pb:M:7.0301} maṃsena medena, matthakena ca brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Āhutiṃ paggahessāmi, chetvāna hadayaṃ tava.
::

::hangnum
1971\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ me suyiṭṭhaṃ suhutaṃ, tuyhaṃ maṃsena brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Na ca tvaṃ rājaputtassa, bhariyaṃ putte ca nessasī’’ti.
::

Tattha **akiccakārī**ti tvaṃ akiccakārako. **Dummedho**ti nippañño. **Raṭṭhā pavanamāgato**ti raṭṭhato mahāraññaṃ āgato. **Saro pissatī**ti ayaṃ saro tava lohitaṃ pivissati. **Vajjhayitvānā**ti taṃ māretvā rukkhā patitassa te sīsaṃ tālaphalaṃ viya luñcitvā sabandhanaṃ hadayamaṃsaṃ {pb:V:7.0291} chinditvā panthadevatāya panthasakuṇaṃ nāma yajissāmi. **Na ca tva**nti evaṃ sante na tvaṃ rājaputtassa bhariyaṃ vā putte vā nessasīti.

So {pb:P:6.0528} tassa vacanaṃ sutvā maraṇabhayatajjito musāvādaṃ kathento āha –

::hangnum
1972\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avajjho brāhmaṇo dūto, cetaputta suṇohi me;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā hi dūtaṃ na hanti, esa dhammo sanantano.
::

::hangnum
1973\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nijjhattā sivayo sabbe, pitā naṃ daṭṭhumicchati;
::

::gathalast
Mātā ca dubbalā tassa, acirā cakkhūni jīyare.
::

::hangnum
1974\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesāhaṃ pahito dūto, cetaputta suṇohi me;
::

::gathalast
Rājaputtaṃ nayissāmi, yadi jānāsi saṃsa me’’ti.
::

Tattha **nijjhattā**ti saññattā. **Acirā cakkhūni jīyare**ti niccarodanena na cirasseva cakkhūni jīyissanti.

Tadā cetaputto ‘‘vessantaraṃ kira ānetuṃ āgato’’ti somanassappatto hutvā sunakhe bandhitvā ṭhapetvā brāhmaṇaṃ otāretvā sākhāsanthare nisīdāpetvā bhojanaṃ datvā imaṃ gāthamāha –

::hangnum
1975\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piyassa {pb:M:7.0302} me piyo dūto, puṇṇapattaṃ dadāmi te;
::

::gatha2
Imañca madhuno tumbaṃ, migasatthiñca brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Tañca te desamakkhissaṃ, yattha sammati kāmado’’ti.
::

Tattha **piyassa me**ti mama piyassa vessantarassa tvaṃ piyo dūto. **Puṇṇapatta**nti tava ajjhāsayapūraṇaṃ puṇṇapattaṃ dadāmīti.

::centre
Jūjakapabbavaṇṇanā niṭṭhitā.
::

#### Cūḷavanavaṇṇanā

Evaṃ {pb:V:7.0292} cetaputto brāhmaṇaṃ bhojetvā pātheyyatthāya tassa madhuno tumbañceva pakkamigasatthiñca datvā magge ṭhatvā dakkhiṇahatthaṃ ukkhipitvā mahāsattassa vasanokāsaṃ ācikkhanto āha –

::hangnum
1976\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Esa selo mahābrahme, pabbato gandhamādano;
::

::gathalast
Yattha vessantaro rājā, saha puttehi sammati.
::

::hangnum
1977\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhārento brāhmaṇavaṇṇaṃ, āsadañca masaṃ jaṭaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cammavāsī chamā seti, jātavedaṃ namassati.
::

::hangnum
1978\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ete nīlā padissanti, nānāphaladharā dumā;
::

::gathalast
Uggatā abbhakūṭāva, nīlā añjanapabbatā.
::

::hangnum
1979\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhavassakaṇṇā khadirā, sālā phandanamāluvā;
::

::gathalast
Sampavedhanti vātena, sakiṃ pītāva māṇavā.
::

::hangnum
1980\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upari dumapariyāyesu, saṅgītiyova suyyare;
::

::gathalast
Najjuhā kokilasaṅghā, sampatanti dumā dumaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1981\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avhayanteva {pb:P:6.0529} gacchantaṃ, sākhāpattasamīritā;
::

::gatha2
Ramayanteva āgantaṃ, modayanti nivāsinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yattha vessantaro rājā, saha puttehi sammati.
::

::hangnum
1982\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhārento {pb:M:7.0303} brāhmaṇavaṇṇaṃ, āsadañca masaṃ jaṭaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cammavāsī chamā seti, jātavedaṃ namassatī’’ti.
::

Tattha **gandhamādano**ti esa gandhamādanapabbato, etassa pādena uttarābhimukho gacchanto yattha sakkadattiye assamapade vessantaro rājā saha puttadārehi vasati, taṃ passissasīti attho. **Brāhmaṇavaṇṇa**nti seṭṭhapabbajitavesaṃ. **Āsadañca masaṃ jaṭa**nti ākaḍḍhitvā phalānaṃ gahaṇatthaṃ aṅkusañca {pb:V:7.0293} aggijuhanakaṭacchuñca jaṭāmaṇḍalañca dhārento. **Cammavāsī**ti ajinacammadharo. **Chamā setī**ti pathaviyaṃ paṇṇasanthare sayati. **Dhavassakaṇṇā khadirā**ti dhavā ca assakaṇṇā ca khadirā ca. **Sakiṃ pītāva māṇavā**ti ekavārameva pītā surāsoṇḍā viya. **Upari dumapariyāyesū**ti rukkhasākhāsu. **Saṅgītiyova suyyare**ti nānāsakuṇānaṃ vassantānaṃ saddā dibbasaṅgītiyo viya suyyare. **Najjuhā**ti najjuhasakuṇā. **Sampatantī**ti vikūjantā vicaranti. **Sākhāpattasamīritā**ti sākhānaṃ pattehi saṅghaṭṭitā hutvā vikūjantā sakuṇā, vātena samīritā pattasākhāyeva vā. **Āganta**nti āgacchantaṃ janaṃ. **Yatthā**ti yasmiṃ assame vessantaro vasati, tattha gantvā imaṃ assamapadasampattiṃ passissasīti.

Tato uttaripi assamapadaṃ vaṇṇento āha –

::hangnum
1983\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ambā kapitthā panasā, sālā jambū vibhītakā;
::

::gathalast
Harītakī āmalakā, assatthā badarāni ca.
::

::hangnum
1984\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cārutimbarukkhā cettha, nigrodhā ca kapitthanā;
::

::gathalast
Madhumadhukā thevanti, nīce pakkā cudumbarā.
::

::hangnum
1985\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pārevatā bhaveyyā ca, muddikā ca madhutthikā;
::

::gathalast
Madhuṃ anelakaṃ tattha, sakamādāya bhuñjare.
::

::hangnum
1986\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññettha pupphitā ambā, aññe tiṭṭhanti dovilā;
::

::gathalast
Aññe āmā ca pakkā ca, bhekavaṇṇā tadūbhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
1987\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athettha heṭṭhā puriso, ambapakkāni gaṇhati;
::

::gathalast
Āmāni ceva pakkāni, vaṇṇagandharasuttame.
::

::hangnum
1988\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ateva {pb:M:7.0304} me acchariyaṃ, hīṅkāro paṭibhāti maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Devānamiva āvāso, sobhati nandanūpamo.
::

::hangnum
1989\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vibhedikā {pb:V:7.0294} nāḷikerā, khajjurīnaṃ brahāvane;
::

::gatha2
Mālāva ganthitā ṭhanti, dhajaggāneva dissare;
::

::gathalast
Nānāvaṇṇehi pupphehi, nabhaṃ tārācitāmiva.
::

::hangnum
1990\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuṭajī {pb:P:6.0530} kuṭṭhatagarā, pāṭaliyo ca pupphitā;
::

::gathalast
Punnāgā giripunnāgā, koviḷārā ca pupphitā.
::

::hangnum
1991\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uddālakā somarukkhā, agaruphalliyā bahū;
::

::gathalast
Puttajīvā ca kakudhā, asanā cettha pupphitā.
::

::hangnum
1992\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuṭajā salaḷā nīpā, kosambā labujā dhavā;
::

::gathalast
Sālā ca pupphitā tattha, palālakhalasannibhā.
::

::hangnum
1993\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassāvidūre pokkharaṇī, bhūmibhāge manorame;
::

::gathalast
Padumuppalasañchannā, devānamiva nandane.
::

::hangnum
1994\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athettha puppharasamattā, kokilā mañjubhāṇikā;
::

::gathalast
Abhinādenti pavanaṃ, utusampupphite dume.
::

::hangnum
1995\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhassanti makarandehi, pokkhare pokkhare madhū;
::

::gatha2
Athettha vātā vāyanti, dakkhiṇā atha pacchimā;
::

::gathalast
Padumakiñjakkhareṇūhi, okiṇṇo hoti assamo.
::

::hangnum
1996\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Thūlā siṅghāṭakā cettha, saṃsādiyā pasādiyā;
::

::gatha2
Macchakacchapabyāviddhā, bahū cettha mupayānakā;
::

::gathalast
Madhuṃ bhisehi savati, khīrasappi muḷālibhi.
::

::hangnum
1997\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Surabhī taṃ vanaṃ vāti, nānāgandhasamoditaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Sammaddateva gandhena, pupphasākhāhi taṃ vanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhamarā pupphagandhena, samantā mabhināditā.
::

::hangnum
1998\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athettha {pb:V:7.0295} sakuṇā santi, nānāvaṇṇā bahū dijā;
::

::gathalast
Modanti saha bhariyāhi, aññamaññaṃ pakūjino.
::

::hangnum
1999\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nandikā {pb:M:7.0305} jīvaputtā ca, jīvaputtā piyā ca no;
::

::gathalast
Piyā puttā piyā nandā, dijā pokkharaṇīgharā.
::

::hangnum
2000\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mālāva ganthitā ṭhanti, dhajaggāneva dissare;
::

::gatha2
Nānāvaṇṇehi pupphehi, kusaleheva suganthitā;
::

::gathalast
Yattha vessantaro rājā, saha puttehi sammati.
::

::hangnum
2001\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhārento brāhmaṇavaṇṇaṃ, āsadañca masaṃ jaṭaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cammavāsī chamā seti, jātavedaṃ namassatī’’ti.
::

Tattha **cārutimbarukkhā**ti suvaṇṇatimbarukkhā. **Madhumadhukā**ti madhurasā madhukā. **Thevantī**ti virocanti. **Pārevatā**ti pārevatapādasadisā rukkhā. **Bhaveyyā**ti dīghaphalā kadaliyo. **Madhutthikā**ti madhuttheve paggharantiyo, madhuratāya vā madhutthevasadisā. **Sakamādāyā**ti taṃ sayameva gahetvā paribhuñjanti. **Dovilā**ti patitapupphapattā sañjāyamānaphalā. **Bhekavaṇṇā tadūbhaya**nti te ubhopi āmā ca pakkā ca maṇḍūkapiṭṭhivaṇṇāyeva. **Athettha heṭṭhā puriso**ti atha ettha assame tesaṃ ambānaṃ heṭṭhā ṭhitakova puriso ambaphalāni gaṇhāti, ārohaṇakiccaṃ {pb:P:6.0531} natthi. **Vaṇṇagandharasuttame**ti etehi vaṇṇādīhi uttamāni.

**Ateva me acchariya**nti ativiya me acchariyaṃ. **Hiṅkāro**ti hinti karaṇaṃ. **Vibhedikā**ti tālā. **Mālāva ganthitā**ti supupphitarukkhānaṃ upari ganthitā mālā viya pupphāni tiṭṭhanti. **Dhajaggāneva dissare**ti tāni rukkhāni alaṅkatadhajaggāni viya dissanti. **Kuṭajī kuṭṭhatagarā**ti kuṭaji nāmekā rukkhajāti kuṭṭhagacchā ca tagaragacchā ca. **Giripunnāgā**ti mahāpunnāgā. **Koviḷārā**ti koviḷārarukkhā nāma. **Uddālakā**ti uddālarukkhā. **Somarukkhā**ti pītapupphavaṇṇā rājarukkhā. **Phalliyā**ti phalliyarukkhā nāma. **Puttajīvā**ti mahānigrodhā. **Labujā**ti labujarukkhā nāma. **Palālakhalasannibhā**ti tesaṃ heṭṭhā paggharitapupphapuñjā palālakhalasannibhāti vadati.

**Pokkharaṇī**ti {pb:V:7.0296} caturassapokkharaṇī. **Nandane**ti nandanavane nandāpokkharaṇī viya. **Puppharasamattā**ti puppharasena mattā calitā. **Makarandehī**ti kiñjakkhehi. **Pokkhare** {pb:M:7.0306} **pokkhare**ti paduminipaṇṇe paduminipaṇṇe. Tesu hi kiñjakkhato reṇu bhassitvā pokkharamadhu nāma hoti. **Dakkhiṇā atha pacchimā**ti ettāvatā sabbā disā vidisāpi vātā dassitā honti. **Thūlā** **siṅghāṭakā**ti mahantā siṅghāṭakā ca. **Saṃsādiyā**ti sayaṃ jātasālī, sukasālītipi vuccanti. **Pasādiyā**ti teyeva bhūmiyaṃ patitā. **Byāviddhā**ti pasanne udake byāviddhā paṭipāṭiyā gacchantā dissanti. **Mupayānakā**ti kakkaṭakā. **Madha**unti bhisakoṭiyā bhinnāya paggharaṇaraso madhusadiso hoti. **Khīrasappi muḷālibhī**ti muḷālehi paggharaṇaraso khīramissakanavanītasappi viya hoti.

**Sammaddatevā**ti sampattajanaṃ madayati viya. **Samantā mabhināditā**ti samantā abhinadantā vicaranti. **‘‘Nandikā’’**tiādīni tesaṃ nāmāni. Tesu hi paṭhamā ‘‘sāmi vessantara, imasmiṃ vane vasanto nandā’’ti vadanti. Dutiyā ‘‘tvañca sukhena jīva, puttā ca te’’ti vadanti. Tatiyā ‘‘tvañca jīva, piyā puttā ca te’’ti vadanti. Catutthā ‘‘tvañca nanda, piyā puttā ca te’’ti vadanti. Tena tesaṃ etāneva nāmāni ahesuṃ. **Pokkharaṇīgharā**ti pokkharaṇivāsino.

Evaṃ cetaputtena vessantarassa vasanaṭṭhāne akkhāte jūjako tussitvā paṭisanthāraṃ karonto imaṃ gāthamāha –

::hangnum
2002\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idañca me sattubhattaṃ, madhunā paṭisaṃyutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Madhupiṇḍikā ca sukatāyo, sattubhattaṃ dadāmi te’’ti.
::

Tattha **sattubhatta**nti pakkamadhusannibhaṃ sattusaṅkhātaṃ bhattaṃ. Idaṃ vuttaṃ hoti – idaṃ mama atthi, taṃ te dammi, gaṇhāhi nanti.

Taṃ sutvā cetaputto āha –

::hangnum
2003\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tuyheva sambalaṃ hotu, nāhaṃ icchāmi sambalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Itopi brahme gaṇhāhi, gaccha brahme yathāsukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2004\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayaṃ {pb:V:7.0297}{pb:P:6.0532}{pb:M:7.0307} ekapadī eti, ujuṃ gacchati assamaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Isīpi accuto tattha, paṅkadanto rajassiro;
::

::gathalast
Dhārento brāhmaṇavaṇṇaṃ, āsadañca masaṃ jaṭaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2005\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cammavāsī chamā seti, jātavedaṃ namassati;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ tvaṃ gantvāna pucchassu, so te maggaṃ pavakkhatī’’ti.
::

Tattha **sambala**nti pātheyyaṃ. **Etī**ti yo ekapadikamaggo amhākaṃ abhimukho eti, esa assamaṃ ujuṃ gacchati. **Accuto**ti evaṃnāmako isi tattha vasati.

::hangnum
2006\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ sutvā brahmabandhu, cetaṃ katvā padakkhiṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Udaggacitto pakkāmi, yenāsi accuto isī’’ti.
::

Tattha **yenāsī**ti yasmiṃ ṭhāne accuto isi ahosi, tattha gatoti.

::centre
Cūḷavanavaṇṇanā niṭṭhitā.
::

#### Mahāvanavaṇṇanā

::hangnum
2007\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gacchanto so bhāradvājo, addassa accutaṃ isiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Disvāna taṃ bhāradvājo, sammodi isinā saha.
::

::hangnum
2008\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci nu bhoto kusalaṃ, kacci bhoto anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kacci uñchena yāpesi, kacci mūlaphalā bahū.
::

::hangnum
2009\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci ḍaṃsā makasā ca, appameva sarīsapā;
::

::gathalast
Vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe, kacci hiṃsā na vijjatī’’ti.
::

Tattha **bhāradvājo**ti jūjako. **Appamevā**ti appāyeva. **Hiṃsā**ti tesaṃ vasena tumhākaṃ vihiṃsā.

Tāpaso {pb:V:7.0298} āha –

::hangnum
2010\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kusalañceva me brahme, atho brahme anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atho uñchena yāpemi, atho mūlaphalā bahū.
::

::hangnum
2011\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atho {pb:M:7.0308} ḍaṃsā makasā ca, appameva sarīsapā;
::

::gathalast
Vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe, hiṃsā mayhaṃ na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
2012\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahūni vassapūgāni, assame vasato mama;
::

::gathalast
Nābhijānāmi uppannaṃ, ābādhaṃ amanoramaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2013\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ te mahābrahme, atho te adurāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anto pavisa bhaddante, pāde pakkhālayassu te.
::

::hangnum
2014\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tindukāni piyālāni, madhuke kāsumāriyo;
::

::gathalast
Phalāni khuddakappāni, bhuñja brahme varaṃ varaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2015\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idampi pānīyaṃ sītaṃ, ābhataṃ girigabbharā;
::

::gathalast
Tato piva mahābrahme, sace tvaṃ abhikaṅkhasī’’ti.
::

Jūjako āha –

::hangnum
2016\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭiggahitaṃ {pb:P:6.0533} yaṃ dinnaṃ, sabbassa agghiyaṃ kataṃ;
::

::gatha2
Sañjayassa sakaṃ puttaṃ, sivīhi vippavāsitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ dassanamāgato, yadi jānāsi saṃsa me’’ti.
::

Tattha **tamahaṃ dassanamāgato**ti taṃ ahaṃ dassanāya āgato. Tāpaso āha –

::hangnum
2017\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:7.0299} bhavaṃ eti puññatthaṃ, sivirājassa dassanaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Maññe bhavaṃ patthayati, rañño bhariyaṃ patibbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maññe kaṇhājinaṃ dāsiṃ, jāliṃ dāsañca icchasi.
::

::hangnum
2018\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha vā tayo mātāputte, araññā netumāgato;
::

::gathalast
Na tassa bhogā vijjanti, dhanaṃ dhaññañca brāhmaṇā’’ti.
::

Tattha **na tassa bhogā**ti bho brāhmaṇa, tassa vessantarassa araññe viharantassa neva bhogā vijjanti, dhanadhaññañca na vijjati, duggato hutvā vasati, tassa santikaṃ gantvā kiṃ karissasīti?

Taṃ sutvā jūjako āha –

::hangnum
2019\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akuddharūpohaṃ bhoto, nāhaṃ yācitumāgato;
::

::gathalast
Sādhu dassanamariyānaṃ, sannivāso sadā sukho.
::

::hangnum
2020\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adiṭṭhapubbo {pb:M:7.0309} sivirājā, sivīhi vippavāsito;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ dassanamāgato, yadi jānāsi saṃsa me’’ti.
::

Tassattho – ahaṃ, bho tāpasa, akuddharūpo, alaṃ ettāvatā, ahaṃ pana na kiñci vessantaraṃ yācitumāgato, ariyānaṃ pana dassanaṃ sādhu, sannivāso ca tehi saddhiṃ sukho. Ahaṃ tassa ācariyabrāhmaṇo, mayā ca so yato sivīhi vippavāsito, tato paṭṭhāya adiṭṭhapubbo, tenāhaṃ taṃ dassanatthāya āgato. Yadi tassa vasanaṭṭhānaṃ jānāsi, saṃsa meti.

So tassa vacanaṃ sutvā saddahitvā ‘‘hotu sve saṃsissāmi te, ajja tāva idheva vasāhī’’ti taṃ phalāphalehi santappetvā punadivase maggaṃ dassento dakkhiṇahatthaṃ pasāretvā āha –

::hangnum
2021\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Esa selo mahābrahme, pabbato gandhamādano;
::

::gathalast
Yattha vessantaro rājā, saha puttehi sammati.
::

::hangnum
2022\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhārento {pb:V:7.0300} brāhmaṇavaṇṇaṃ, āsadañca masaṃ jaṭaṃ;

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
2029\.

::gatha1
‘‘Mayūragīvasaṅkāsā, tūlaphassasamūpamā;
::

::gathalast
Tiṇāni nātivattanti, samantā caturaṅgulā.

::hangnum
2030\.

::gatha1
‘‘Ambā jambū kapitthā ca, nīce pakkā cudumbarā;
::

::gathalast
Paribhogehi rukkhehi, vanaṃ taṃ rativaḍḍhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2031\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Veḷuriyavaṇṇasannibhaṃ, macchagumbanisevitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Suciṃ sugandhaṃ salilaṃ, āpo tatthapi sandati.
::

::hangnum
2032\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassāvidūre {pb:V:7.0301} pokkharaṇī, bhūmibhāge manorame;
::

::gathalast
Padumuppalasañchannā, devānamiva nandane.
::

::hangnum
2033\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tīṇi uppalajātāni, tasmiṃ sarasi brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Vicittaṃ nīlānekāni, setā lohitakāni cā’’ti.
::

Tassattho heṭṭhā vuttasadisoyeva. **Karerimālā vitatā**ti kareripupphehi vitatā. **Saddalāharitā**ti dhuvasaddalena haritā. **Na tatthuddhaṃsate rajo**ti tasmiṃ vane appamattakopi rajo na uddhaṃsate. **Tūlaphassasamūpamā**ti mudusamphassatāya tūlaphassasadisā. **Tiṇāni nātivattantī**ti tāni tassā bhūmiyā mayūragīvavaṇṇāni tiṇāni samantato caturaṅgulappamāṇāneva vattanti, tato pana uttari na vaḍḍhanti. **Ambā jambū kapitthā cā**ti ambā ca jambū ca kapitthā ca. **Paribhogehī**ti nānāvidhehi pupphūpagaphalūpagehi paribhogarukkhehi. **Sandatī**ti tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe vaṅkapabbate kunnadīhi otarantaṃ udakaṃ sandati, pavattatīti attho. **Vicittaṃ nīlānekāni, setā lohitakāni cā**ti ekāni nīlāni, ekāni setāni, ekāni lohitakānīti imehi tīhi uppalajātehi taṃ saraṃ vicittaṃ. Susajjitapupphacaṅkoṭakaṃ viya sobhatīti dasseti.

Evaṃ caturassapokkharaṇiṃ vaṇṇetvā puna mucalindasaraṃ vaṇṇento āha –

::hangnum
2034\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khomāva {pb:M:7.0311} tattha padumā, setasogandhikehi ca;
::

::gathalast
Kalambakehi sañchanno, mucalindo nāma so saro.
::

::hangnum
2035\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athettha padumā phullā, apariyantāva dissare;
::

::gathalast
Gimhā hemantikā phullā, jaṇṇutagghā upattharā.
::

::hangnum
2036\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Surabhī sampavāyanti, vicittapupphasanthatā;
::

::gathalast
Bhamarā pupphagandhena, samantā mabhināditā’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:P:6.0535} **khomāvā**ti khomamayā viya paṇḍarā. **Setasogandhikehi cā**ti setuppalehi ca sogandhikehi ca kalambakehi ca so saro sañchanno. **Apariyantāva dissare**ti aparimāṇā viya dissanti. **Gimhā hemantikā**ti gimhe ca hemantike ca pupphitapadumā. **Jaṇṇutagghā upattharā**ti jaṇṇupamāṇe {pb:V:7.0302} udake upattharā phullā honti, santhatā viya khāyanti. **Vicittapupphasanthatā**ti vicittā hutvā pupphehi santhatā sadā surabhī sampavāyanti.

::hangnum
2037\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athettha udakantasmiṃ, rukkhā tiṭṭhanti brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Kadambā pāṭalī phullā, koviḷārā ca pupphitā.
::

::hangnum
2038\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aṅkolā kacchikārā ca, pārijaññā ca pupphitā;
::

::gathalast
Vāraṇā vayanā rukkhā, mucalindamubhato saraṃ.

::hangnum
2039\.

::gatha1
‘‘Sirīsā setapārisā, sādhu vāyanti paddhakā;
::

::gathalast
Nigguṇḍī sirīnigguṇḍī, asanā cettha pupphitā.

::hangnum
2040\.

::gatha1
‘‘Paṅgurā bahulā selā, sobhañjanā ca pupphitā;
::

::gathalast
Ketakā kaṇikārā ca, kaṇaverā ca pupphitā.

::hangnum
2041\.

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjunā ajjukaṇṇā ca, mahānāmā ca pupphitā;
::

::gathalast
Supupphitaggā tiṭṭhanti, pajjalanteva kiṃsukā.
::

::hangnum
2042\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Setapaṇṇī sattapaṇṇā, kadaliyo kusumbharā;
::

::gathalast
Dhanutakkārī pupphehi, sīsapāvaraṇāni ca.
::

::hangnum
2043\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Acchivā {pb:M:7.0312} sallavā rukkhā, sallakiyo ca pupphitā;
::

::gathalast
Setageru ca tagarā, maṃsikuṭṭhā kulāvarā.
::

::hangnum
2044\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Daharā rukkhā ca vuddhā ca, akuṭilā cettha pupphitā;
::

::gathalast
Assamaṃ ubhato ṭhanti, agyāgāraṃ samantato’’ti.
::

Tattha **tiṭṭhantī**ti saraṃ parikkhipitvā tiṭṭhanti. **Kadambā**ti kadambarukkhā. **Kacchikārā cā**ti evaṃnāmakā rukkhā. **Pārijaññā**ti rattamālā. **Vāraṇā vayanā**ti vāraṇarukkhā ca vayanarukkhā ca. **Mucalindamubhato sara**nti mucalindassa sarassa ubhayapassesu. **Setapārisā**ti setagaccharukkhā{pb:V:7.0303}. Te kira setakkhandhā mahāpaṇṇā kaṇikārasadisapupphā honti. **Nigguṇḍī sirīnigguṇḍī**ti pakatinigguṇḍī ceva kāḷanigguṇḍī ca. **Paṅgurā**ti paṅgurarukkhā. **Kusumbharā**ti ekagacchā. **Dhanutakkārī pupphehī**ti dhanūnañca takkārīnañca pupphehi sobhitā. **Sīsapāvaraṇāni cā**ti sīsapehi ca varaṇehi ca sobhitā. **Acchivā**tiādayopi rukkhāyeva. **Setageru ca tagarā**ti setageru ca tagarā ca. **Maṃsikuṭṭhā kulāvarā**ti maṃsigacchā ca kuṭṭhagacchā ca kulāvarā ca. **Akuṭilā**ti ujukā. **Agyāgāraṃ samantato**ti agyāgāraṃ parikkhipitvā ṭhitāti attho.

::hangnum
2045\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athettha {pb:P:6.0536} udakantasmiṃ, bahujāto phaṇijjako;
::

::gathalast
Muggatiyo karatiyo, sevālasīsakā bahū.
::

::hangnum
2046\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uddāpavattaṃ ulluḷitaṃ, makkhikā hiṅgujālikā;
::

::gathalast
Dāsimakañjako cettha, bahū nīcekalambakā.
::

::hangnum
2047\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Elamphurakasañchannā, rukkhā tiṭṭhanti brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
2048\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Indīvarehi sañchannaṃ, vanaṃ taṃ upasobhati.
::

::hangnum
2049\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aḍḍhamāsaṃ {pb:M:7.0313} dhāriyamānānaṃ, gandho tesaṃ na chijjati;
::

::gatha2
Nīlapupphī setavārī, pupphitā girikaṇṇikā;
::

::gathalast
Kalerukkhehi sañchannaṃ, vanaṃ taṃ tulasīhi ca.
::

::hangnum
2050\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sammaddateva gandhena, pupphasākhāhi taṃ vanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhamarā pupphagandhena, samantā mabhināditā.
::

::hangnum
2051\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tīṇi kakkārujātāni, tasmiṃ sarasi brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Kumbhamattāni cekāni, murajamattāni tā ubho’’ti.
::

Tattha **phaṇijjako**ti bhūtanako. **Muggatiyo**ti ekā muggajāti. **Karatiyo**ti rājamāso. **Sevālasīsakā**ti {pb:V:7.0304} imepi gacchāyeva, api ca **sīsakā**ti rattacandanaṃ vuttaṃ. **Uddāpavattaṃ ulluḷita**nti taṃ udakaṃ tīramariyādabandhaṃ vātāpahataṃ ulluḷitaṃ hutvā tiṭṭhati. **Makkhikā hiṅgujālikā**ti hiṅgujālasaṅkhāte vikasitapupphagacche pañcavaṇṇā madhumakkhikā madhurassarena viravantiyo tattha vicarantīti attho. **Dāsimakañjako cetthā**ti imāni dve rukkhajātiyo ca ettha. **Nīcekalambakā**ti nīcakalambakā. **Elamphurakasañchannā**ti evaṃnāmikāya valliyā sañchannā. **Tesa**nti tesaṃ tassā valliyā pupphānaṃ sabbesampi vā etesaṃ dāsimakañjakādīnaṃ pupphānaṃ sattāhaṃ gandho na chijjati. Evaṃ gandhasampannāni pupphāni, rajatapaṭṭasadisavālukapuṇṇā bhūmibhāgā. **Gandho tesa**nti tesaṃ indīvarapupphādīnaṃ gandho aḍḍhamāsaṃ na chijjati. **Nīlapupphī**tiādikā pupphavalliyo. **Tulasīhi cā**ti tulasigacchehi ca. **Kakkārujātānī**ti valliphalāni. Tattha ekissā valliyā phalāni mahāghaṭamattāni, dvinnaṃ mudiṅgamattāni. Tena vuttaṃ ‘‘murajamattāni tā ubho’’ti.

::hangnum
2052\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athettha sāsapo bahuko, nādiyo haritāyuto;
::

::gathalast
Asī tālāva tiṭṭhanti, chejjā indīvarā bahū.
::

::hangnum
2053\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Apphoṭā sūriyavallī ca, kāḷīyā madhugandhiyā;
::

::gathalast
Asokā mudayantī ca, vallibho khuddapupphiyo.
::

::hangnum
2054\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Koraṇḍakā anojā ca, pupphitā nāgamallikā;
::

::gathalast
Rukkhamāruyha tiṭṭhanti, phullā kiṃsukavalliyo.
::

::hangnum
2055\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṭeruhā {pb:P:6.0537}{pb:M:7.0314} ca vāsantī, yūthikā madhugandhiyā;
::

::gathalast
Niliyā sumanā bhaṇḍī, sobhati padumuttaro.
::

::hangnum
2056\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṭalī samuddakappāsī, kaṇikārā ca pupphitā;
::

::gathalast
Hemajālāva dissanti, ruciraggi sikhūpamā.
::

::hangnum
2057\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāni tāni ca pupphāni, thalajānudakāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāni tattha dissanti, evaṃ rammo mahodadhī’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:V:7.0305} **sāsapo**ti siddhatthako. **Bahuko**ti bahu. **Nādiyo haritāyuto**ti haritena āyuto nādiyo. Imā dvepi lasuṇajātiyo, sopi lasuṇo tattha bahukoti attho. **Asī tālāva tiṭṭhantī**ti **asī**ti evaṃnāmakā rukkhā siniddhāya bhūmiyā ṭhitā tālā viya tiṭṭhanti. **Chejjā indīvarā bahū**ti udakapariyante bahū suvaṇṇaindīvarā muṭṭhinā chinditabbā hutvā ṭhitā. **Apphoṭā**ti apphoṭavalliyo. **Vallibho khuddapupphiyo**ti vallibho ca khuddapupphiyo ca. **Nāgamallikā**ti vallināgā ca mallikā ca. **Kiṃsukavalliyo**ti sugandhapattā vallijātī. **Kaṭeruhā ca vāsantī**ti ime ca dve pupphagacchā. **Madhugandhiyā**ti madhusamānagandhā. **Niliyā sumanā bhaṇḍī**ti nīlavallisumanā ca pakatisumanā ca bhaṇḍī ca. **Padumuttaro**ti evaṃnāmako rukkho. **Kaṇikārā**ti vallikaṇikārā rukkhakaṇikārā. **Hemajālāvā**ti pasāritahemajālā viya dissanti. **Mahodadhī**ti mahato udakakkhandhassa ādhārabhūto mucalindasaroti.

::hangnum
2058\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athassā pokkharaṇiyā, bahukā vārigocarā;
::

::gathalast
Rohitā naḷapī siṅgū, kumbhilā makarā susū.
::

::hangnum
2059\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Madhu ca madhulaṭṭhi ca, tālisā ca piyaṅgukā;
::

::gathalast
Kuṭandajā bhaddamuttā, setapupphā ca lolupā.
::

::hangnum
2060\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Surabhī ca rukkhā tagarā, bahukā tuṅgavaṇṭakā;
::

::gathalast
Paddhakā naradā kuṭṭhā, jhāmakā ca hareṇukā.
::

::hangnum
2061\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Haliddakā {pb:M:7.0315} gandhasilā, hiriverā ca guggulā;
::

::gathalast
Vibhedikā corakā kuṭṭhā, kappūrā ca kaliṅgukā’’ti.
::

Tattha **athassā pokkharaṇiyā**ti idha pokkharaṇisadisatāya sarameva pokkharaṇīti vadati. **Rohitā**tiādīni tesaṃ vārigocarānaṃ nāmāni. **Madhu cā**ti nimmakkhikamadhu ca. **Madhulaṭṭhi cā**ti laṭṭhimadhukañca. **Tālisā cā**tiādikā sabbā gandhajātiyo.

::gatha1

::gathalast
Eṇeyyā pasadā ceva, rohiccā sarabhā migā.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::

::gathalast
Khaggā varāhā nakulā, kāḷakettha bahūtaso.
::

::hangnum
2065\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahiṃsā soṇasiṅgālā, pampakā ca samantato;
::

::gathalast
Ākucchā pacalākā ca, citrakā cāpi dīpiyo.
::

::hangnum
2066\.

::gatha1
‘‘Pelakā ca vighāsādā, sīhā gogaṇisādakā;
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭhapādā ca morā ca, bhassarā ca kukutthakā.

::hangnum

::gatha1
‘‘Caṅkorā kukkuṭā nāgā, aññamaññaṃ pakūjino;
::

::gathalast
Bakā balākā najjuhā, dindibhā kuñjavājitā.

::hangnum
2068\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Byagghinasā lohapiṭṭhā, pampakā jīvajīvakā;
::

::gathalast
Kapiñjarā tittirāyo, kulā ca paṭikutthakā.
::

::hangnum
2069\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mandālakā celakeṭu, bhaṇḍutittiranāmakā;
::

::gathalast
Celāvakā piṅgalāyo, goṭakā aṅgahetukā.
::

::hangnum
2070\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Karaviyā ca saggā ca, uhuṅkārā ca kukkuhā;
::

::gathalast
Nānādijagaṇākiṇṇaṃ, nānāsaranikūjita’’nti.
::

Tattha **purisālū**ti vaḷavāmukhayakkhiniyo. **Rohiccā sarabhā migā**ti rohitā ceva sarabhā migā ca. **Koṭṭhasukā**ti siṅgālasunakhā. ‘‘Kotthusuṇā’’tipi {pb:M:7.0316} pāṭho. **Suṇopi cā**ti esāpekā khuddakamigajāti. **Tuliyā**ti pakkhibiḷārā. **Naḷasannibhā**ti naḷapupphavaṇṇā rukkhasunakhā. **Cāmarī calanī laṅghī**ti cāmarīmigā ca calanīmigā ca laṅghīmigā ca. **Jhāpitā makkaṭā**ti dve makkaṭajātiyova. **Picū**ti sarapariyante gocaraggāhī eko makkaṭo. **Kakkaṭā kaṭamāyā cā**ti dve mahāmigā. **Ikkā**ti acchā. **Goṇasirā**ti araññagoṇā. **Kāḷakettha bahūtaso**ti kāḷamigā {pb:V:7.0307} nāmettha bahūtaso. **Soṇasiṅgālā**ti rukkhasunakhā ca siṅgālā ca. **Pampakā**ti assamapadaṃ parikkhipitvā ṭhitā mahāveḷupampakā. **Ākucchā**ti godhā. **Pacalākā cā**ti gajakumbhamigā. **Citrakā cāpi dīpiyo**ti citrakamigā ca dīpimigā ca.

**Pelakā cā**ti sasā. **Vighāsādā**ti ete gijjhā sakuṇā. **Sīhā**ti kesarasīhā. **Gogaṇisādakā**ti gogaṇe gahetvā khādanasīlā duṭṭhamigā. **Aṭṭhapādā**ti sarabhā migā. **Bhassarā**ti setahaṃsā. **Kukutthakā**ti kukutthakasakuṇā. **Caṅkorā**ti caṅkorasakuṇā. **Kukkuṭā**ti vanakukkuṭā. **Dindibhā kuñjavājitā**ti ime tayopi sakuṇāyeva. **Byagghinasā**ti senā. **Lohapiṭṭhā**ti lohitavaṇṇasakuṇā. **Pampakā**ti pampaṭakā. **Kapiñjarā tittirāyo**ti kapiñjarā ca tittirā ca. **Kulā ca paṭikutthakā**ti imepi dve sakuṇā. **Mandālakā celakeṭū**ti mandālakā ceva celakeṭu ca. **Bhaṇḍutittiranāmakā**ti bhaṇḍū ca tittirā ca nāmakā ca. **Celāvakā** {pb:P:6.0539} **piṅgalāyo**ti dve sakuṇajātiyo ca, tathā **goṭakā aṅgahetukā. Saggā**ti cātakasakuṇā. **Uhuṅkārā**ti ulūkā.

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Sāli akaṭṭhapāko ca, ucchu tattha anappako.
