::gatha1
‘‘Yassu sāyanhasamayaṃ, puttakā paṃsukuṇṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Ucchaṅge me vivattanti, te na passāmi dārake.
::

::hangnum
2214\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ayaṃ so assamo pubbe, samajjo paṭibhāti maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tyajja putte apassantyā, bhamate viya assamo.
::

::hangnum
2215\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kimidaṃ {pb:P:6.0560} appasaddova, assamo paṭibhāti maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kākolāpi na vassanti, matā me nūna dārakā.
::

::hangnum
2216\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kimidaṃ appasaddova, assamo paṭibhāti maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakuṇāpi na vassanti, matā me nūna dārakā’’ti.
::

Tattha **na**nti nipātamattaṃ. **Paṃsukuṇṭhitā**ti paṃsumakkhitā. **Paccuggatā ma**nti maṃ paccuggatā hutvā. ‘‘Paccuggantunā’’tipi pāṭho, paccuggantvāicceva attho. **Ukkaṇṇā**ti yathā migapotakā mātaraṃ disvā kaṇṇe ukkhipitvā gīvaṃ pasāretvā mātaraṃ upagantvā haṭṭhatuṭṭhā samantā abhidhāvino. **Vaggamānāva** {pb:M:7.0343} **kampare**tivajjamānāyeva mātu hadayamaṃsaṃ kampenti viya evaṃ pubbe mama puttā. **Tyajjā**ti te ajja na passāmi. **Chakalīva migī chāpa**nti yathā chakalī ca migī ca pañjarasaṅkhātā kulāvakā muttā pakkhī ca āmisagiddhinī sīhī ca attano chāpaṃ ohāya {pb:V:7.0335} gocarāya pakkamanti, tathāhampi ohāya putte gocarāya nikkhaminti vadati. **Idaṃ nesaṃ padakkanta**nti vassāratte sānupabbate nāgānaṃ padavalañjaṃ viya idaṃ nesaṃ kīḷanaṭṭhāne ādhāvanaparidhāvanapadakkantaṃ paññāyati. **Citakā**ti sañcitanicitā kavālukapuñjā. **Parikiṇṇāyo**ti vippakiṇṇāyo. **Samantā mabhidhāvantī**ti aññesu divasesu samantā abhidhāvanti.

**Paccuṭṭhentī**ti paccuggacchanti. **Dūramāyati**nti dūrato āgacchantiṃ. **Chakaliṃva migiṃ chāpā**ti attano mātaraṃ chakaliṃ viya migiṃ viya ca chāpā. **Idaṃ nesaṃ kīḷanaka**nti hatthirūpakādīhi kīḷantānaṃ idañca tesaṃ hatthato suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ kīḷanabeluvaṃ parigaḷitvā patitaṃ. **Mayhime**ti mayhaṃ ime thanā ca khīrassa pūrā. **Uro ca sampadālatī**ti hadayañca phalati. **Ucchaṅge me vivattantī**ti mama ucchaṅge āvattanti vivattanti. **Samajjo paṭibhāti ma**nti samajjaṭṭhānaṃ viya mayhaṃ upaṭṭhāti. **Tyajjā**ti te ajja. **Apassantyā**ti apassantiyā mama. **Bhamate viyā**ti kulālacakkaṃ viya bhamati. **Kākolā**ti vanakākā. **Matā nūnā**ti addhā matā vā kenaci nītā vā bhavissanti. **Sakuṇā**ti avasesasakuṇā.

Iti sā vilapantī mahāsattassa santikaṃ gantvā phalapacchiṃ otāretvā mahāsattaṃ tuṇhimāsīnaṃ disvā dārake cassa santike apassantī āha –

::hangnum
2217\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kimidaṃ tuṇhibhūtosi, api ratteva me mano;
::

::gathalast
Kākolāpi na vassanti, matā me nūna dārakā.
::

::hangnum
2218\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kimidaṃ tuṇhibhūtosi, api ratteva me mano;
::

::gathalast
Sakuṇāpi na vassanti, matā me nūna dārakā.
::

::hangnum
2219\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci nu me ayyaputta, migā khādiṃsu dārake;
::

::gathalast
Araññe iriṇe vivane, kena nītā me dārakā.
::

::hangnum
2220\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Adu {pb:P:6.0561}{pb:M:7.0344} te pahitā dūtā, adu suttā piyaṃvadā;
::

::gathalast
Adu bahi no nikkhantā, khiḍḍāsu pasutā nu te.
::

::hangnum
2221\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nevāsaṃ {pb:V:7.0336} kesā dissanti, hatthapādā ca jālino;
::

::gathalast
Sakuṇānañca opāto, kena nītā me dārakā’’ti.
::

Tattha **api ratteva me mano**ti api balavapaccūse supinaṃ passantiyā viya me mano. **Migā**ti sīhādayo vāḷamigā. **Iriṇe**ti niroje. **Vivane**ti vivitte. **Dūtā**ti adu jetuttaranagare sivirañño santikaṃ tayā dūtā katvā pesitā. **Suttā**ti antopaṇṇasālaṃ pavisitvā sayitā. **Adu bahi no**ti adu te dārakā khiḍḍāpasutā hutvā bahi nikkhantāti pucchati. **Nevāsaṃ kesā dissantī**ti sāmi vessantara, neva tesaṃ kāḷañjanavaṇṇā kesā dissanti. **Jālino**ti kañcanajālavicittā hatthapādā. **Sakuṇānañca opāto**ti himavantapadese hatthiliṅgasakuṇā nāma atthi, te opatitvā ādāya ākāseneva gacchanti. Tena taṃ pucchāmi ‘‘kiṃ tehi sakuṇehi nītā, ito aññesampi kesañci tesaṃ sakuṇānaṃ viya opāto jāto, akkhāhi, kena nītā me dārakā’’ti?

Evaṃ vuttepi mahāsatto na kiñci āha. Atha naṃ sā ‘‘deva, kasmā mayā saddhiṃ na kathesi, ko mama doso’’ti vatvā āha –

::hangnum
2222\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ tato dukkhataraṃ, sallaviddho yathā vaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Tyajja putte na passāmi, jāliṃ kaṇhājinaṃ cubho.
::

::hangnum
2223\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idampi dutiyaṃ sallaṃ, kampeti hadayaṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Yañca putte na passāmi, tvañca maṃ nābhibhāsasi.
::

::hangnum
2224\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjeva me imaṃ rattiṃ, rājaputta na saṃsati;
::

::gathalast
Maññe okkantasantaṃ maṃ, pāto dakkhisi no mata’’nti.
::

Tattha **idaṃ tato dukkhatara**nti sāmi vessantara, yaṃ mama raṭṭhā pabbājitāya araññe vasantiyā putte ca apassantiyā dukkhaṃ, idaṃ tava mayā saddhiṃ akathanaṃ mayhaṃ tato dukkhataraṃ. Tvañhi maṃ aggidaḍḍhaṃ paṭidahanto viya {pb:M:7.0345} papātā patitaṃ daṇḍena pothento viya sallena vaṇaṃ vijjhanto viya tuṇhībhāvena kilamesi. Idañhi me hadayaṃ sallaviddho yathā vaṇo tatheva kampati ceva rujati ca. ‘‘Sampaviddho’’tipi pāṭho, sampatividdhoti attho. **Okkantasantaṃ** {pb:V:7.0337} **ma**nti apagatajīvitaṃ maṃ. **Dakkhisi no mata**nti ettha **no**-kāro nipātamatto, mataṃ maṃ kālasseva tvaṃ passissasīti attho.

Atha mahāsatto ‘‘kakkhaḷakathāya naṃ puttasokaṃ jahāpessāmī’’ti cintetvā imaṃ gāthamāha –

::hangnum
2225\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nūna {pb:P:6.0562} maddī varārohā, rājaputtī yasassinī;
::

::gathalast
Pāto gatāsi uñchāya, kimidaṃ sāyamāgatā’’ti.
::

Tattha **kimidaṃ sāyamāgatā**ti ‘‘maddi, tvaṃ abhirūpā pāsādikā, himavante ca nāma bahū vanacarakā tāpasavijjādharādayo vicaranti. Ko jānāti, kiṃ bhavissati, kiñci tayā kataṃ, tvaṃ pātova gantvā kimidaṃ sāyamāgacchasi, daharakumārake ohāya araññagatitthiyo nāma sasāmikitthiyo evarūpā na honti, ‘kā nu kho me dārakānaṃ pavatti, kiṃ vā me sāmiko cintessatī’ti ettakampi te nāhosi. Tvaṃ pātova gantvā candālokena āgacchasi, mama duggatabhāvassevesa doso’’ti tajjetvā vañcetvā kathesi.

Sā tassa kathaṃ sutvā āha –

::hangnum
2226\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nanu tvaṃ saddamassosi, ye saraṃ pātumāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Sīhassapi nadantassa, byagghassa ca nikujjitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2227\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahu pubbanimittaṃ me, vicarantyā brahāvane;
::

::gathalast
Khaṇitto me hatthā patito, uggīvañcāpi aṃsato.
::

::hangnum
2228\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāhaṃ byathitā bhītā, puthu katvāna añjaliṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbadisā namassissaṃ, api sotthi ito siyā.
::

::hangnum
2229\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā {pb:M:7.0346} heva no rājaputto, hato sīhena dīpinā;
::

::gathalast
Dārakā vā parāmaṭṭhā, acchakokataracchihi.
::

::hangnum
2230\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīho {pb:V:7.0338} byaggho ca dīpi ca, tayo vāḷā vane migā;
::

::gathalast
Te maṃ pariyāvaruṃ maggaṃ, tena sāyamhi āgatā’’ti.
::

Tattha **ye saraṃ pātumāgatā**ti ye pānīyaṃ pātuṃ imaṃ saraṃ āgatā. **Byagghassa cā**ti byagghassa ca aññesaṃ hatthiādīnaṃ catuppadānañceva sakuṇasaṅghassa ca nikūjitaṃ ekaninnādasaddaṃ kiṃ tvaṃ na assosīti pucchati. So pana mahāsattena puttānaṃ dinnavelāya saddo ahosi. **Ahu pubbanimittaṃ me**ti deva, imassa me dukkhassa anubhavanatthāya pubbanimittaṃ ahosi. **Uggīva**nti aṃsakūṭe pacchilagganakaṃ. **Puthū**ti visuṃ visuṃ. **Sabbadisā namassissa**nti sabbā dasa disā namassiṃ. **Mā heva no**ti amhākaṃ rājaputto sīhādīhi hato mā hotu, dārakāpi acchādīhi parāmaṭṭhā mā hontūti patthayantī namassissaṃ. **Te maṃ pariyāvaruṃ magga**nti sāmi vessantara, ahaṃ ‘‘imāni ca bhīsanakāni mahantāni, dussupino ca me diṭṭho, ajja sakālasseva gamissāmī’’ti kampamānā mūlaphalāphalāni upadhāresiṃ, atha me phalitarukkhāpi aphalā viya aphalā ca phalino viya dissanti, kicchena phalāphalāni gahetvā giridvāraṃ sampāpuṇiṃ. Atha te sīhādayo maṃ disvā maggaṃ paṭipāṭiyā rumbhitvā aṭṭhaṃsu. Tena sāyaṃ āgatāmhi, khamāhi me, sāmīti.

Mahāsatto tāya saddhiṃ ettakameva kathaṃ vatvā yāva aruṇuggamanā na kiñci kathesi. Tato paṭṭhāya maddī nānappakārakaṃ vilapantī āha –

::hangnum
2231\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ {pb:P:6.0563} patiñca putte ca, āceramiva māṇavo;
::

::gathalast
Anuṭṭhitā divārattiṃ, jaṭinī brahmacārinī.
::

::hangnum
2232\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ajināni paridahitvā, vanamūlaphalahāriyā;
::

::gathalast
Vicarāmi divārattiṃ, tumhaṃ kāmā hi puttakā.
::

::hangnum
2233\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahaṃ suvaṇṇahaliddiṃ, ābhataṃ paṇḍubeluvaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rukkhapakkāni cāhāsiṃ, ime vo putta kīḷanā.
::

::hangnum
2234\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imaṃ {pb:M:7.0347} mūḷālivattakaṃ, sālukaṃ ciñcabhedakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhuñja khuddehi saṃyuttaṃ, saha puttehi khattiya.
::

::hangnum
2235\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Padumaṃ {pb:V:7.0339} jālino dehi, kumudañca kumāriyā;
::

::gathalast
Māline passa naccante, sivi puttāni avhaya.
::

::hangnum
2236\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato kaṇhājināyapi, nisāmehi rathesabha;
::

::gathalast
Mañjussarāya vagguyā, assamaṃ upayantiyā.
::

::hangnum
2237\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samānasukhadukkhamhā, raṭṭhā pabbājitā ubho;
::

::gathalast
Api sivi putte passesi, jāliṃ kaṇhājinaṃ cubho.
::

::hangnum
2238\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samaṇe brāhmaṇe nūna, brahmacariyaparāyaṇe;
::

::gatha2
Ahaṃ loke abhissapiṃ, sīlavante bahussute;
::

::gathalast
Tyajja putte na passāmi, jāliṃ kaṇhājinaṃ cubho’’ti.
::

Tattha **āceramiva māṇavo**ti vattasampanno antevāsiko ācariyaṃ viya paṭijaggati. **Anuṭṭhitā**ti pāricariyānuṭṭhānena anuṭṭhitā appamattā hutvā paṭijaggāmi. **Tumhaṃ kāmā**ti tumhākaṃ kāmena tumhe patthayantī. **Puttakā**ti kumāre ālapantī paridevati. **Suvaṇṇahaliddi**nti puttakā ahaṃ tumhākaṃ nhāpanatthāya suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ haliddiṃ ghaṃsitvā ādāya āgatā. **Paṇḍubeluva**nti kīḷanatthāya ca vo idaṃ suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ beluvapakkaṃ mayā ābhataṃ. **Rukkhapakkānī**ti tumhākaṃ kīḷanatthāya aññānipi manāpāni rukkhaphalāni āhāsiṃ. **Ime vo**ti puttakā ime vo kīḷanāti vadati. **Mūḷālivattaka**nti mūḷālakuṇḍalakaṃ. **Sāluka**nti idaṃ uppalādisālukampi me bahu ābhataṃ. **Ciñcabhedaka**nti siṅghāṭakaṃ. **Bhuñjā**ti idaṃ sabbaṃ khuddamadhunā saṃyuttaṃ puttehi saddhiṃ bhuñjāhīti paridevati. **Sivi puttāni avhayā**ti sāmi sivirāja, paṇṇasālāya sayāpitaṭṭhānato sīghaṃ puttake pakkosāhi. **Api sivi putte passesī**ti sāmi sivirāja, api putte passasi, sace passasi, mama dassehi, kiṃ maṃ ativiya kilamesi. **Abhissapi**nti tumhākaṃ puttadhītaro mā passitthāti evaṃ nūna akkosinti.

Evaṃ {pb:P:6.0564}{pb:M:7.0348} vilapamānāyapi tāya saddhiṃ mahāsatto na kiñci kathesi. Sā tasmiṃ akathente kampamānā candālokena putte vicinantī yesu yesu jamburukkhādīsu pubbe kīḷiṃsu, tāni tāni patvā paridevantī āha –

::hangnum
2239\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ime {pb:V:7.0340} te jambukā rukkhā, vedisā sinduvārakā;
::

::gathalast
Vividhāni rukkhajātāni, te kumārā na dissare.
::

::hangnum
2240\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assatthā panasā ceme, nigrodhā ca kapitthanā;
::

::gathalast
Vividhāni phalajātāni, te kumārā na dissare.
::

::hangnum
2241\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ime tiṭṭhanti ārāmā, ayaṃ sītūdakā nadī;
::

::gathalast
Yatthassu pubbe kīḷiṃsu, te kumārā na dissare.
::

::hangnum
2242\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vividhāni pupphajātāni, asmiṃ uparipabbate;
::

::gathalast
Yānassu pubbe dhāriṃsu, te kumārā na dissare.
::

::hangnum
2243\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vividhāni phalajātāni, asmiṃ uparipabbate;
::

::gathalast
Yānassu pubbe bhuñjiṃsu, te kumārā na dissare.
::

::hangnum
2244\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ime te hatthikā assā, balibaddā ca te ime;
::

::gathalast
Yehissu pubbe kīḷiṃsu, te kumārā na dissare’’ti.
::

Tattha **ime te hatthikā**ti sā pabbatūpari dārake adisvā paridevamānā tato oruyha puna assamapadaṃ āgantvā tattha te upadhārentī tesaṃ kīḷanabhaṇḍakāni disvā evamāha.

Athassā paridevanasaddena ceva padasaddena ca migapakkhino caliṃsu. Sā te disvā āha –

::hangnum
2245\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ime sāmā sasolūkā, bahukā kadalīmigā;
::

::gathalast
Yehissu pubbe kīḷiṃsu, te kumārā na dissare.
::

::hangnum
2246\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ime haṃsā ca koñcā ca, mayūrā citrapekhuṇā;
::

::gathalast
Yehissu pubbe kīḷiṃsu, te kumārā na dissare’’ti.
::

Tattha **sāmā**ti khuddakā sāmā suvaṇṇamigā. **Sasolūkā**ti sasā ca ulūkā ca.

Sā {pb:V:7.0341}{pb:M:7.0349} assamapade piyaputte adisvā nikkhamitvā pupphitavanaghaṭaṃ pavisitvā taṃ taṃ ṭhānaṃ olokentī āha –

::hangnum
2247\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imā tā vanagumbāyo, pupphitā sabbakālikā;
::

::gathalast
Yatthassu pubbe kīḷiṃsu, te kumārā na dissare.
::

::hangnum
2248\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imā tā pokkharaṇī rammā, cakkavākūpakūjitā;
::

::gatha2
Mandālakehi sañchannā, padumuppalakehi ca;
::

::gathalast
Yatthassu pubbe kīḷiṃsu, te kumārā na dissare’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:P:6.0565} **vanagumbāyo**ti vanaghaṭāyo.

Sā katthaci piyaputte adisvā puna mahāsattassa santikaṃ āgantvā taṃ dummukhaṃ nisinnaṃ disvā āha –

::hangnum
2249\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na te kaṭṭhāni bhinnāni, na te udakamāhaṭaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aggipi te na hāpito, kiṃ nu mandova jhāyasi.
::

::hangnum
2250\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piyo piyena saṅgamma, samo me byapahaññati;
::

::gathalast
Tyajja putte na passāmi, jāliṃ kaṇhājinaṃ cubho’’ti.
::

Tattha **na hāpito**ti na jalito. Idaṃ vuttaṃ hoti – sāmi, tvaṃ pubbe kaṭṭhāni bhindasi, udakaṃ āharitvā ṭhapesi, aṅgārakapalle aggiṃ karosi, ajja tesu ekampi akatvā kiṃ nu mandova jhāyasi, tava kiriyā mayhaṃ na ruccatīti. **Piyo piyenā**ti vessantaro mayhaṃ piyo, ito me piyataro natthi, iminā me piyena saṅgamma samāgantvā pubbe samo me byapahaññati dukkhaṃ vigacchati, ajja pana me imaṃ passantiyāpi soko na vigacchati, kiṃ nu kho kāraṇanti. **Tyajjā**ti hotu, diṭṭhaṃ me kāraṇaṃ, te ajja putte na passāmi, tena me imaṃ passantiyāpi soko na vigacchatīti.

Tāya evaṃ vuttepi mahāsatto tuṇhībhūtova nisīdi. Sā tasmiṃ akathente sokasamappitā {pb:V:7.0342} pahaṭakukkuṭī viya kampamānā puna paṭhamaṃ vicaritaṭṭhānāni vicaritvā mahāsattassa santikaṃ paccāgantvā āha –

::hangnum
2251\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:7.0350} kho no deva passāmi, yena te nīhatā matā;
::

::gathalast
Kākolāpi na vassanti, matā me nūna dārakā.
::

::hangnum
2252\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na kho no deva passāmi, yena te nīhatā matā;
::

::gathalast
Sakuṇāpi na vassanti, matā me nūna dārakā’’ti.
::

Tattha **na kho no**ti deva, na kho amhākaṃ putte passāmi. **Yena te nīhatā**ti kenaci tesaṃ nīhatabhāvampi na jānāmīti adhippāyenevamāha.

Evaṃ vuttepi mahāsatto na kiñci kathesiyeva. Sā puttasokena phuṭṭhā putte upadhārentī tatiyampi tāni tāni ṭhānāni vātavegena vicari. Tāya ekarattiṃ vicaritaṭṭhānaṃ pariggayhamānaṃ pannarasayojanamattaṃ ahosi. Atha ratti vibhāsi, aruṇodayo jāto. Sā puna gantvā mahāsattassa santike ṭhitā paridevi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2253\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sā tattha paridevitvā, pabbatāni vanāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Punadevassamaṃ gantvā, rodi sāmikasantike.
::

::hangnum
2254\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:P:6.0566} kho no deva passāmi, yena te nīhatā matā;
::

::gathalast
Kākolāpi na vassanti, matā me nūna dārakā.
::

::hangnum
2255\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na kho no deva passāmi, yena te nīhatā matā;
::

::gathalast
Sakuṇāpi na vassanti, matā me nūna dārakā.
::

::hangnum
2256\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nu kho no deva passāmi, yena te nīhatā matā;
::

::gathalast
Vicarantī rukkhamūlesu, pabbatesu guhāsu ca.
::

::hangnum
2257\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iti {pb:V:7.0343} maddī varārohā, rājaputtī yasassinī;
::

::gathalast
Bāhā paggayha kanditvā, tattheva patitā chamā’’ti.
::

Tattha **sāmikasantike**ti bhikkhave, sā maddī tattha vaṅkapabbatakucchiyaṃ sānupabbatāni vanāni ca vicarantī paridevitvā puna gantvā sāmikaṃ nissāya tassa santike ṭhitā puttānaṃ atthāya rodi, ‘‘na kho no’’tiādīni vadantī {pb:M:7.0351} paridevīti attho. **Iti maddī varārohā**ti bhikkhave, evaṃ sā uttamarūpadharā varārohā maddī rukkhamūlādīsu vicarantī dārake adisvā ‘‘nissaṃsayaṃ matā bhavissantī’’ti bāhā paggayha kanditvā tattheva vessantarassa pādamūle chinnasuvaṇṇakadalī viya chamāyaṃ pati.

Atha mahāsatto ‘‘matā maddī’’ti saññāya kampamāno ‘‘aṭṭhāne padese matā maddī. Sace hissā jetuttaranagare kālakiriyā abhavissa, mahanto parivāro abhavissa, dve raṭṭhāni caleyyuṃ. Ahaṃ pana araññe ekakova, kiṃ nu kho karissāmī’’ti uppannabalavasokopi satiṃ paccupaṭṭhāpetvā ‘‘jānissāmi tāvā’’ti uṭṭhāya tassā hadaye hatthaṃ ṭhapetvā santāpapavattiṃ ñatvā kamaṇḍalunā udakaṃ āharitvā satta māse kāyasaṃsaggaṃ anāpannapubbopi balavasokena pabbajitabhāvaṃ sallakkhetuṃ asakkonto assupuṇṇehi nettehi tassā sīsaṃ ukkhipitvā ūrūsu ṭhapetvā udakena paripphositvā mukhañca hadayañca parimajjanto nisīdi. Maddīpi kho thokaṃ vītināmetvā satiṃ paṭilabhitvā hirottappaṃ paccupaṭṭhāpetvā uṭṭhāya mahāsattaṃ vanditvā ‘‘sāmi vessantara, dārakā te kuhiṃ gatā’’ti āha. ‘‘Devi, ekassa brāhmaṇassa dāsatthāya dinnā’’ti. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2258\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tamajjhapattaṃ rājaputtiṃ, udakenābhisiñcatha;
::

::gathalast
Assatthaṃ naṃ viditvāna, atha naṃ etadabravī’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:P:6.0567} **ajjhapatta**nti attano santikaṃ pattaṃ, pādamūle patitvā visaññibhūtanti attho. **Etadabravī**ti etaṃ ‘‘ekassa me brāhmaṇassa dāsatthāya dinnā’’ti vacanaṃ abravi.

Tato tāya ‘‘deva, putte brāhmaṇassa datvā mama sabbarattiṃ paridevitvā vicarantiyā kiṃ nācikkhasī’’ti vutte mahāsatto āha –

::hangnum
2259\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ādiyeneva {pb:V:7.0344} te maddi, dukkhaṃ nakkhātumicchisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Daliddo yācako vuḍḍho, brāhmaṇo gharamāgato.
::

::hangnum
2260\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa {pb:M:7.0352} dinnā mayā puttā, maddi mā bhāyi assasa;
::

::gatha2
Maṃ passa maddi mā putte, mā bāḷhaṃ paridevasi;
::

::gathalast
Lacchāma putte jīvantā, arogā ca bhavāmase.
::

::hangnum
2261\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Putte pasuñca dhaññañca, yañca aññaṃ ghare dhanaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Dajjā sappuriso dānaṃ, disvā yācakamāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anumodāhi me maddi, puttake dānamuttama’’nti.
::

Tattha **ādiyenevā**ti ādikeneva. Idaṃ vuttaṃ hoti – sace te ahaṃ āditova tamatthaṃ ācikkhissaṃ, tato tava sokaṃ sandhāretuṃ asakkontiyā hadayaṃ phaleyya, tasmā ādikeneva te maddi dukkhaṃ na akkhātuṃ icchissanti. **Gharamāgato**ti imaṃ amhākaṃ vasanaṭṭhānaṃ āgato. **Arogā ca bhavāmase**ti yathā tathā mayaṃ arogā homa, jīvamānā avassaṃ putte brāhmaṇena nītepi passissāma. **Yañca añña**nti yañca aññaṃ ghare saviññāṇakaṃ dhanaṃ. **Dajjā sappuriso dāna**nti sappuriso uttamatthaṃ patthento uraṃ bhinditvā hadayamaṃsampi gahetvā dānaṃ dadeyyāti.

Maddī āha –

::hangnum
2262\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anumodāmi te deva, puttake dānamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Datvā cittaṃ pasādehi, bhiyyo dānaṃ dado bhava.
::

::hangnum
2263\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo tvaṃ maccherabhūtesu, manussesu janādhipa;
::

::gathalast
Brāhmaṇassa adā dānaṃ, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano’’ti.
::

Tattha **anumodāmi te**ti dasa māse kucchiyā dhāretvā divasassa dvattikkhattuṃ nhāpetvā pāyetvā bhojetvā ure nipajjāpetvā paṭijaggitaputtakesu bodhisattena dinnesu sayaṃ puttadānaṃ anumodantī evamāha. Iminā kāraṇena jānitabbaṃ ‘‘pitāva puttānaṃ sāmiko’’ti. **Bhiyyo dānaṃ** {pb:V:7.0345} **dado bhavā**ti mahārāja, uttaripi punappunaṃ dānaṃ dāyakova hohi, ‘‘sudinnaṃ me dāna’’nti cittaṃ pasādehi, yo tvaṃ maccherabhūtesu sattesu piyaputte adāsīti.

Evaṃ {pb:M:7.0353} vutte mahāsatto ‘‘maddi, kinnāmetaṃ kathesi, sace hi mayā putte datvā cittaṃ pasādetuṃ nābhavissa, imāni pana me acchariyāni na pavatteyyu’’nti vatvā sabbāni pathavininnādādīni {pb:P:6.0568} kathesi. Tato maddī tāni acchariyāni kittetvā dānaṃ anumodantī āha –

::hangnum
2264\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ninnāditā te pathavī, saddo te tidivaṅgato;
::

::gathalast
Samantā vijjutā āguṃ, girīnaṃva patissutā’’ti.
::

Tattha **vijjutā āgu**nti akālavijjulatā himavantapadese samantā nicchariṃsu. **Girīnaṃva patissutā**ti girīnaṃ patissutasaddā viya viravā uṭṭhahiṃsu.

::hangnum
2265\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa te anumodanti, ubho nāradapabbatā;
::

::gatha2
Indo ca brahmā pajāpati, somo yamo vessavaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe devānumodanti, tāvatiṃsā saindakā.
::

::hangnum
2266\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iti maddī varārohā, rājaputtī yasassinī;
::

::gathalast
Vessantarassa anumodi, puttake dānamuttama’’nti.
::

Tattha **ubho nāradapabbatā**ti imepi dve devanikāyā attano vimānadvāre ṭhitāva ‘‘sudinnaṃ te dāna’’nti anumodanti. **Tāvatiṃsā saindakā**ti indajeṭṭhakā tāvatiṃsāpi devā te dānaṃ anumodantīti.

Evaṃ mahāsattena attano dāne vaṇṇite tamevatthaṃ parivattetvā ‘‘mahārāja vessantara, sudinnaṃ nāma te dāna’’nti maddīpi tatheva dānaṃ vaṇṇayitvā anumodamānā nisīdi. Tena satthā ‘‘iti maddī varārohā’’ti gāthamāha.

::centre
Maddīpabbavaṇṇanā niṭṭhitā.
::

#### Sakkapabbavaṇṇanā

Evaṃ {pb:V:7.0346}{pb:M:7.0354} tesu aññamaññaṃ sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ kathentesu sakko cintesi ‘‘ayaṃ vessantaro rājā hiyyo jūjakassa pathaviṃ unnādetvā dārake adāsi, idāni taṃ koci hīnapuriso upasaṅkamitvā sabbalakkhaṇasampannaṃ maddiṃ yācitvā rājānaṃ ekakaṃ katvā maddiṃ gahetvā gaccheyya, tato esa anātho nippaccayo bhaveyya. Ahaṃ brāhmaṇavaṇṇena naṃ upasaṅkamitvā maddiṃ yācitvā pāramikūṭaṃ gāhāpetvā kassaci avissajjiyaṃ katvā puna naṃ tasseva datvā āgamissāmī’’ti. So sūriyuggamanavelāya tassa santikaṃ agamāsi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2267\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato ratyā vivasāne, sūriyassuggamanaṃ pati;
::

::gathalast
Sakko brāhmaṇavaṇṇena, pāto tesaṃ adissathā’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:P:6.0569} **pāto tesaṃ adissathā**ti pātova nesaṃ dvinnampi janānaṃ paññāyamānarūpo purato aṭṭhāsi, ṭhatvā ca pana paṭisanthāraṃ karonto āha –

::hangnum
2268\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci nu bhoto kusalaṃ, kacci bhoto anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kacci uñchena yāpetha, kacci mūlaphalā bahū.
::

::hangnum
2269\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci ḍaṃsā makasā ca, appameva sarīsapā;
::

::gathalast
Vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe, kacci hiṃsā na vijjatī’’ti.
::

Mahāsatto āha –

::hangnum
2270\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kusalañceva no brahme, atho brahme anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atho uñchena yāpema, atho mūlaphalā bahū.
::

::hangnum
2271\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atho ḍaṃsā makasā ca, appameva sarīsapā;
::

::gathalast
Vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe, hiṃsā mayhaṃ na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
2272\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satta {pb:V:7.0347} no māse vasataṃ, araññe jīvasokinaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Idaṃ dutiyaṃ passāma, brāhmaṇaṃ devavaṇṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ādāya veḷuvaṃ daṇḍaṃ, dhārentaṃ ajinakkhipaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2273\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ {pb:M:7.0355} te mahābrahme, atho te adurāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anto pavisa bhaddante, pāde pakkhālayassu te.
::

::hangnum
2274\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tindukāni piyālāni, madhuke kāsumāriyo;
::

::gathalast
Phalāni khuddakappāni, bhuñja brahme varaṃ varaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2275\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idampi pānīyaṃ sītaṃ, ābhataṃ girigabbharā;
::

::gathalast
Tato piva mahābrahme, sace tvaṃ abhikaṅkhasī’’ti.
::

Evaṃ tena saddhiṃ paṭisanthāraṃ katvā mahāsatto –

::hangnum
2276\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha tvaṃ kena vaṇṇena, kena vā pana hetunā;
::

::gathalast
Anuppatto brahāraññaṃ, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito’’ti. –
::

::unindented
Āgamanakāraṇaṃ pucchi. Atha naṃ sakko ‘‘mahārāja, ahaṃ mahallako, idhāgacchanto tava bhariyaṃ maddiṃ yācituṃ āgato, taṃ me dehī’’ti vatvā imaṃ gāthamāha –
::

::hangnum
2277\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā vārivaho pūro, sabbakālaṃ na khīyati;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ taṃ yācitāgacchiṃ, bhariyaṃ me dehi yācito’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte mahāsatto ‘‘hiyyo me brāhmaṇassa dārakā dinnā, araññe ekako hutvā kathaṃ te maddiṃ dassāmī’’ti avatvā pasāritahatthe sahassatthavikaṃ ṭhapento viya asajjitvā abajjhitvā anolīnamānaso hutvā giriṃ unnādento imaṃ gāthamāha –

::hangnum
2278\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dadāmi {pb:P:6.0570} na vikampāmi, yaṃ maṃ yācasi brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Santaṃ nappaṭiguyhāmi, dāne me ramatī mano’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:V:7.0348} **santaṃ nappaṭiguyhāmī**ti saṃvijjamānaṃ na guyhāmi.

Evañca pana vatvā sīghameva kamaṇḍalunā udakaṃ āharitvā udakaṃ hatthe pātetvā piyabhariyaṃ brāhmaṇassa adāsi. Taṅkhaṇeyeva heṭṭhā vuttappakārāni sabbāni acchariyāni pāturahesuṃ. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2279\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maddiṃ {pb:M:7.0356} hatthe gahetvāna, udakassa kamaṇḍaluṃ;
::

::gathalast
Brāhmaṇassa adā dānaṃ, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano.
::

::hangnum
2280\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāsi yaṃ bhiṃsanakaṃ, tadāsi lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maddiṃ pariccajantassa, medanī sampakampatha.
::

::hangnum
2281\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nevassa maddī bhākuṭi, na sandhīyati na rodati;
::

::gathalast
Pekkhatevassa tuṇhī sā, eso jānāti yaṃ vara’’nti.
::

Tattha **adā dāna**nti ‘‘ambho brāhmaṇa, maddito me sataguṇena sahassaguṇena satasahassaguṇena sabbaññutaññāṇameva piyataraṃ, idaṃ me dānaṃ sabbaññutaññāṇappaṭivedhassa paccayo hotū’’ti vatvā dānaṃ adāsi vuttampi cetaṃ –

::gatha1
‘‘Jāliṃ kaṇhājinaṃ dhītaṃ, maddiṃ deviṃ patibbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cajamāno na cintesiṃ, bodhiyāyeva kāraṇā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na me dessā ubho puttā, maddī devī na dessiyā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaññutaṃ piyaṃ mayhaṃ, tasmā piye adāsaha’’nti. (cariyā. 1.118-119);
::

Tattha **sampakampathā**ti pathavī udakapariyantaṃ katvā kampittha. **Nevassa maddī bhākuṭī**ti bhikkhave, tasmiṃ khaṇe maddī ‘‘maṃ mahallakassa brāhmaṇassa rājā detī’’ti kodhavasena bhākuṭipi nāhosi. **Na sandhīyati na rodatī**ti neva maṅku ahosi, na akkhīni pūretvā rodati, atha kho tuṇhī sā hutvā ‘‘mādisaṃ itthiratanaṃ dadamāno na nikkāraṇā dassati, eso {pb:V:7.0349} yaṃ varaṃ, taṃ jānātī’’ti phullapadumavaṇṇaṃ assa mukhaṃ **pekkhateva,** olokayamānāva ṭhitāti attho.

Atha mahāsatto ‘‘kīdisā maddī’’ti tassā mukhaṃ olokesi. Sāpi ‘‘sāmi kiṃ maṃ olokesī’’ti vatvā sīhanādaṃ nadantī imaṃ gāthamāha –

::hangnum
2282\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Komārī yassāhaṃ bhariyā, sāmiko mama issaro;
::

::gathalast
Yassicche tassa maṃ dajjā, vikkiṇeyya haneyya vā’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:P:6.0571}{pb:M:7.0357} **komārī yassāhaṃ bhariyā**ti ahaṃ yassa tava daharikā bhariyā, so tvaññeva mama issaro sāmiko. **Yassicche tassā**ti issaro ca nāma dāsiṃ maṃ yassa dātuṃ iccheyya, tassa dadeyya. **Vikkiṇeyya vā**ti dhanena vā atthe sati vikkiṇeyya, maṃsena vā atthe sati haneyya, tasmā yaṃ vo ruccati, taṃ karotha, nāhaṃ kujjhāmīti.

Sakko tesaṃ paṇītajjhāsayataṃ viditvā thutiṃ akāsi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2283\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesaṃ saṅkappamaññāya, devindo etadabravi;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe jitā te paccūhā, ye dibbā ye ca mānusā.
::

::hangnum
2284\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ninnāditā te pathavī, saddo te tidivaṅgato;
::

::gathalast
Samantā vijjutā āguṃ, girīnaṃva patissutā.
::

::hangnum
2285\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa te anumodanti, ubho nāradapabbatā;
::

::gatha2
Indo ca brahmā pajāpati, somo yamo vessavaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe devānumodanti, dukkarañhi karoti so.
::

::hangnum
2286\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duddadaṃ dadamānānaṃ, dukkaraṃ kamma kubbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asanto nānukubbanti, sataṃ dhammo durannayo.
::

::hangnum
2287\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā {pb:V:7.0350} satañca asataṃ, nānā hoti ito gati;
::

::gathalast
Asanto nirayaṃ yanti, santo saggaparāyaṇā.
::

::hangnum
2288\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yametaṃ kumāre adā, bhariyaṃ adā vane vasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Brahmayānamanokkamma, sagge te taṃ vipaccatū’’ti.
::

Tattha **paccūhā**ti paccatthikā. **Dibbā**ti dibbasampattipaṭibāhakā. **Mānusā**ti manussasampattipaṭibāhakā. Ke pana teti? Macchariyadhammā. Te sabbe puttadāraṃ dentena mahāsattena jitā. Tenāha ‘‘sabbe jitā te paccūhā’’ti. **Dukkarañhi karoti so**ti so vessantaro rājā ekakova araññe vasanto bhariyaṃ brāhmaṇassa dento dukkaraṃ {pb:M:7.0358} karotīti evaṃ sabbe devā anumodantīti vadati. **‘‘Yameta’’**nti gāthaṃ anumodanaṃ karonto āha. **Vane vasa**nti vane vasanto. **Brahmayāna**nti seṭṭhayānaṃ. Tividho hi sucaritadhammo evarūpo ca dānadhammo ariyamaggassa paccayo hotīti ‘‘brahmayāna’’nti vuccati. Tasmā yaṃ taṃ idaṃ ajja dānaṃ dadatopi nipphannaṃ brahmayānaṃ apāyabhūmiṃ anokkamitvā sagge te taṃ vipaccatu, vipākapariyosāne ca sabbaññutaññāṇadāyakaṃ hotūti.

Evamassa sakko anumodanaṃ katvā ‘‘idāni mayā idha papañcaṃ akatvā imaṃ imasseva datvā gantuṃ vaṭṭatī’’ti cintetvā āha –

::hangnum
2289\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dadāmi {pb:P:6.0572} bhoto bhariyaṃ, maddiṃ sabbaṅgasobhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tvañceva maddiyā channo, maddī ca patinā saha.
::

::hangnum
2290\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā payo ca saṅkho ca, ubho samānavaṇṇino;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ tuvañca maddī ca, samānamanacetasā.
::

::hangnum
2291\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avaruddhettha araññasmiṃ, ubho sammatha assame;
::

::gatha2
Khattiyā gottasampannā, sujātā mātupettito;
::

::gathalast
Yathā puññāni kayirātha, dadantā aparāpara’’nti.
::



Tattha {pb:V:7.0351} **channo**ti anurūpo. **Ubho samānavaṇṇino**ti samānavaṇṇā ubhopi parisuddhāyeva. **Samānamanacetasā**ti ācārādīhi kammehi samānena manasaṅkhātena cetasā samannāgatā. **Avaruddhetthā**ti raṭṭhato pabbājitā hutvā ettha araññe vasatha. **Yathā puññānī**ti yathā jetuttaranagare vo bahūni puññāni katāni, hiyyo puttānaṃ ajja bhariyāya dānavasenapi katānīti ettakeneva paritosaṃ akatvā ito uttaripi aparāparaṃ dadantā yathānurūpāni puññāni kareyyāthāti.

Evañca pana vatvā sakko mahāsattassa maddiṃ paṭicchāpetvā varaṃ dātuṃ attānaṃ ācikkhanto āha –

::hangnum
2292\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakkohamasmi devindo, āgatosmi tavantike;
::

::gathalast
Varaṃ varassu rājisi, vare aṭṭha dadāmi te’’ti.
::

Kathentoyeva {pb:M:7.0359} ca dibbattabhāvena jalanto taruṇasūriyo viya ākāse aṭṭhāsi. Tato bodhisatto varaṃ gaṇhanto āha –

::hangnum
2293\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Varaṃ ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
::

::gatha2
Pitā maṃ anumodeyya, ito pattaṃ sakaṃ gharaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āsanena nimanteyya, paṭhametaṃ varaṃ vare.
::

::hangnum
2294\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Purisassa vadhaṃ na roceyyaṃ, api kibbisakārakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vajjhaṃ vadhamhā moceyyaṃ, dutiyetaṃ varaṃ vare.
::

::hangnum
2295\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye vuḍḍhā ye ca daharā, ye ca majjhimaporisā;
::

::gathalast
Mameva upajīveyyuṃ, tatiyetaṃ varaṃ vare.
::

::hangnum
2296\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paradāraṃ na gaccheyyaṃ, sadārapasuto siyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Thīnaṃ vasaṃ na gaccheyyaṃ, catutthetaṃ varaṃ vare.
::

::hangnum
2297\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Putto {pb:V:7.0352} me sakka jāyetha, so ca dīghāyuko siyā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammena jine pathaviṃ, pañcametaṃ varaṃ vare.
::

::hangnum
2298\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato ratyā vivasāne, sūriyassuggamanaṃ pati;
::

::gathalast
Dibbā bhakkhā pātubhaveyyuṃ, chaṭṭhametaṃ varaṃ vare.
::

::hangnum
2299\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dadato me na khīyetha, datvā nānutapeyyahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dadaṃ cittaṃ pasādeyyaṃ, sattametaṃ varaṃ vare.
::

::hangnum
2300\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito {pb:P:6.0573} vimuccamānāhaṃ, saggagāmī visesagū;
::

::gathalast
Anivatti tato assaṃ, aṭṭhametaṃ varaṃ vare’’ti.
::

Tattha **anumodeyyā**ti sampaṭiccheyya na kujjheyya. **Ito patta**nti imamhā araññā sakaṃ gharaṃ anuppattaṃ. **Āsanenā**ti rājāsanena. Rajjaṃ me detūti vadati. **Api kibbisakāraka**nti rājā hutvā rājāparādhikampi vajjhaṃ vadhamhā moceyyaṃ, evarūpassapi me vadho nāma na ruccatu. **Mameva upajīveyyu**nti sabbete maññeva nissāya upajīveyyuṃ. **Dhammena jine**ti dhammena jinātu, dhammena rajjaṃ kāretūti attho. **Visesagū**ti visesagamano hutvā tusitapure nibbatto homīti vadati. **Anivatti** {pb:M:7.0360} **tato assa**nti tusitabhavanato cavitvā manussattaṃ āgato punabhave anivatti assaṃ, sabbaññutaṃ sampāpuṇeyyanti vadati.

::hangnum
2301\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, devindo etadabravi;
::

::gathalast
‘Aciraṃ vata te tato, pitā taṃ daṭṭhumessatī’’’ti.
::

Tattha **daṭṭhumessatī**ti mahārāja, tava mātā ca pitā ca acireneva taṃ passitukāmo hutvā idhāgamissati, āgantvā ca pana setacchattaṃ datvā rajjaṃ niyyādetvā jetuttaranagarameva nessati, sabbe te manorathā matthakaṃ pāpuṇissanti, mā cintayi, appamatto hohi, mahārājāti.

Evaṃ mahāsattassa ovādaṃ datvā sakko sakaṭṭhānameva gato. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2302\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ {pb:V:7.0353} vatvāna maghavā, devarājā sujampati;
::

::gathalast
Vessantare varaṃ datvā, saggakāyaṃ apakkamī’’ti.
::

Tattha **vessantare**ti vessantarassa. **Apakkamī**ti gato anuppattoyevāti.

::centre
Sakkapabbavaṇṇanā niṭṭhitā.
::

#### Mahārājapabbavaṇṇanā

Bodhisatto ca maddī ca sammodamānā sakkadattiye assame vasiṃsu. Jūjakopi kumāre gahetvā saṭṭhiyojanamaggaṃ paṭipajji. Devatā kumārānaṃ ārakkhamakaṃsu. Jūjakopi sūriye atthaṅgate kumāre gacche bandhitvā bhūmiyaṃ nipajjāpetvā sayaṃ caṇḍavāḷamigabhayena rukkhaṃ āruyha viṭapantare sayati. Tasmiṃ khaṇe eko devaputto vessantaravaṇṇena, ekā devadhītā maddivaṇṇena āgantvā kumāre mocetvā hatthapāde sambāhitvā nhāpetvā maṇḍetvā dibbabhojanaṃ bhojetvā dibbasayane sayāpetvā {pb:M:7.0361} aruṇuggamanakāle {pb:P:6.0574} baddhākāreneva nipajjāpetvā antaradhāyi. Evaṃ te devatāsaṅgahena arogā hutvā gacchanti. Jūjakopi devatādhiggahito hutvā ‘‘kāliṅgaraṭṭhaṃ gacchāmī’’ti gacchanto aḍḍhamāsena jetuttaranagaraṃ patto. Taṃ divasaṃ paccūsakāle sañjayo mahārājā supinaṃ passi. Evarūpo supino ahosi – rañño mahāvinicchaye nisinnassa eko puriso kaṇho dve padumāni āharitvā rañño hatthe ṭhapesi. Rājā tāni dvīsu kaṇṇesu piḷandhi. Tesaṃ reṇu bhassitvā rañño ure patati. So pabujjhitvā pātova brāhmaṇe pucchi. Te ‘‘cirapavutthā vo, deva, bandhavā āgamissantī’’ti byākariṃsu. So pātova sīsaṃ nhāyitvā nānaggarasabhojanaṃ bhuñjitvā alaṅkaritvā vinicchaye nisīdi. Devatā brāhmaṇaṃ dvīhi kumārehi saddhiṃ ānetvā rājaṅgaṇe ṭhapayiṃsu. Tasmiṃ khaṇe rājā maggaṃ olokento kumāre disvā āha –

::hangnum
2303\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kassetaṃ mukhamābhāti, hemaṃ-vuttattamagginā;
::

::gathalast
Nikkhaṃva jātarūpassa, ukkāmukhapahaṃsitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2304\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubho {pb:V:7.0354} sadisapaccaṅgā, ubho sadisalakkhaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Jālissa sadiso eko, ekā kaṇhājinā yathā.
::

::hangnum
2305\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīhā bilāva nikkhantā, ubho sampatirūpakā;
::

::gathalast
Jātarūpamayāyeva, ime dissanti dārakā’’ti.
::

Tattha **hemaṃvuttattamagginā**ti hemaṃ iva uttattaṃ agginā. **Sī**hā bilāva nikkhantāti kañcanaguhato nikkhantā sīhā viya.

Evaṃ rājā tīhi gāthāhi kumāre vaṇṇetvā ekaṃ amaccaṃ āṇāpesi ‘‘gacchetaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ dārakehi saddhiṃ ānehī’’ti. So vegena gantvā brāhmaṇaṃ ānesi. Atha rājā brāhmaṇaṃ āha –

::hangnum
2306\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuto nu bhavaṃ bhāradvāja, ime ānesi dārake;
::

::gathalast
Ajja raṭṭhaṃ anuppatto, kuhiṃ gacchasi brāhmaṇā’’ti.
::

Jūjako {pb:M:7.0362} āha –

::hangnum
2307\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mayhaṃ te dārakā deva, dinnā vittena sañjaya;
::

::gathalast
Ajja pannarasā ratti, yato laddhā me dārakā’’ti.
::

Tattha **vittenā**ti tuṭṭhena pasannena. **Ajja pannarasā rattī**ti imesaṃ laddhadivasato paṭṭhāya ajja pannarasā rattīti vadati.

Rājā {pb:P:6.0575} āha –

::hangnum
2308\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kena vā vācapeyyena, sammāñāyena saddahe;
::

::gathalast
Ko tetaṃ dānamadadā, puttake dānamuttama’’nti.
::

Tattha **kena vā vācapeyyenā**ti brāhmaṇa, kena piyavacanena te tayā laddhā. **Sammāñāyena saddahe**ti {pb:V:7.0355} musāvādaṃ akatvā sammāñāyena kāraṇena amhe saddahāpeyyāsi. **Puttake**ti attano piyaputtake uttamaṃ dānaṃ katvā ko te etaṃ dānaṃ adadāti.

Jūjako āha –

::hangnum
2309\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo yācataṃ patiṭṭhāsi, bhūtānaṃ dharaṇīriva;
::

::gathalast
So me vessantaro rājā, puttedāsi vane vasaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2310\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo yācataṃ gatī āsi, savantīnaṃva sāgaro;
::

::gathalast
So me vessantaro rājā, puttedāsi vane vasa’’nti.
::

Tattha **patiṭṭhāsī**ti patiṭṭhā āsi.

Taṃ sutvā amaccā vessantaraṃ garahamānā āhaṃsu –

::hangnum
2311\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dukkaṭaṃ vata bho raññā, saddhena gharamesinā;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ nu puttake dajjā, araññe avaruddhako.
::

::hangnum
2312\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Imaṃ bhonto nisāmetha, yāvantettha samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ vessantaro rājā, puttedāsi vane vasaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2313\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dāsiṃ dāsañca so dajjā, assaṃ cassatarīrathaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hatthiñca kuñjaraṃ dajjā, kathaṃ so dajja dārake’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:M:7.0363} **saddhenā**ti saddhāya sampannenapi satā gharaṃ āvasantena raññā idaṃ dukkaṭaṃ vata, ayuttaṃ vata kataṃ. **Avaruddhako**ti raṭṭhā pabbājito araññe vasanto. **Imaṃ bhonto**ti bhonto nagaravāsino yāvanto ettha samāgatā, sabbe imaṃ nisāmetha upadhāretha, kathaṃ nāmeso puttake dāse katvā adāsi, kena nāma evarūpaṃ katapubbanti adhippāyenevamāhaṃsu. **Dajjā**ti dāsādīsu yaṃ kiñci dhanaṃ detu. **Kathaṃ so dajja dārake**ti ime pana dārake kena kāraṇena adāsīti.

Taṃ {pb:V:7.0356} sutvā kumāro pitu garahaṃ asahanto vātābhihatassa sineruno bāhaṃ oḍḍento viya imaṃ gāthamāha –

::hangnum
2314\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa nassa ghare dāso, asso cassatarīratho;
::

::gathalast
Hatthī ca kuñjaro nāgo, kiṃ so dajjā pitāmahā’’ti.
::

Rājā āha –

::hangnum
2315\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dānamassa {pb:P:6.0576} pasaṃsāma, na ca nindāma puttakā;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ nu hadayaṃ āsi, tumhe datvā vanibbake’’ti.
::

Tattha **dānamassa pasaṃsāmā**ti puttakā mayaṃ tava pitu dānaṃ pasaṃsāma na nindāma.

Taṃ sutvā kumāro āha –

::hangnum
2316\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dukkhassa hadayaṃ āsi, atho uṇhampi passasi;
::

::gathalast
Rohinīheva tambakkhī, pitā assūni vattayī’’ti.
::

Tattha **dukkhassa hadayaṃ āsī**ti pitāmaha kaṇhājināya vuttaṃ etaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā tassa hadayaṃ dukkhaṃ āsi. **Rohinīheva tambakkhī**ti tambavaṇṇehi viya rattaakkhīhi mama pitā tasmiṃ khaṇe assūni pavattayi.

Idānissā taṃ vacanaṃ dassento āha –

::hangnum
2317\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ taṃ kaṇhājināvoca, ayaṃ maṃ tāta brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Laṭṭhiyā paṭikoṭeti, ghare jātaṃva dāsiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2318\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:7.0364} cāyaṃ brāhmaṇo tāta, dhammikā honti brāhmaṇā;
::

::gatha2
Yakkho brāhmaṇavaṇṇena, khādituṃ tāta neti no;
::

::gathalast
Nīyamāne pisācena, kiṃ nu tāta udikkhasī’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:V:7.0357} ne kumāre brāhmaṇaṃ amuñcante disvā rājā gāthamāha –

::hangnum
2319\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājaputtī ca vo mātā, rājaputto ca vo pitā;
::

::gathalast
Pubbe me aṅkamāruyha, kiṃ nu tiṭṭhatha ārakā’’ti.
::

Tattha **pubbe me**ti tumhe ito pubbe maṃ disvā vegenāgantvā mama aṅkamāruyha, idāni kiṃ nu ārakā tiṭṭhathāti?

Kumāro āha –

::hangnum
2320\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rājaputtī ca no mātā, rājaputto ca no pitā;
::

::gathalast
Dāsā mayaṃ brāhmaṇassa, tasmā tiṭṭhāma ārakā’’ti.
::

Tattha **dāsā maya**nti idāni pana mayaṃ brāhmaṇassa dāsā bhavāma.

Rājā āha –

::hangnum
2321\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā sammevaṃ avacuttha, ḍayhate hadayaṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Citakāyaṃva me kāyo, āsane na sukhaṃ labhe.
::

::hangnum
2322\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā sammevaṃ avacuttha, bhiyyo sokaṃ janetha maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nikkiṇissāmi dabbena, na vo dāsā bhavissatha.
::

::hangnum
2323\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kimagghiyañhi {pb:P:6.0577} vo tāta, brāhmaṇassa pitā adā;
::

::gathalast
Yathābhūtaṃ me akkhātha, paṭipādentu brāhmaṇa’’nti.
::

Tattha **sammā**ti piyavacanaṃ. **Citakāyaṃva me kāyo**ti idāni mama kāyo aṅgāracitakāyaṃ āropito viya jāto. **Janetha ma**nti janetha me, ayameva vā pāṭho. **Nikkiṇissāmi dabbenā**ti dhanaṃ datvā mocessāmi. **Kimagghiya**nti kiṃ agghaṃ katvā. **Paṭipādentū**ti dhanaṃ paṭicchāpentu.

Kumāro {pb:V:7.0358}{pb:M:7.0365} āha –

::hangnum
2324\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sahassagghañhi maṃ tāta, brāhmaṇassa pitā adā;
::

::gathalast
Atha kaṇhājinaṃ kaññaṃ, hatthinā ca satena cā’’ti.
::

Tattha **sahassagghaṃ hī**ti deva, maṃ pitā tadā nikkhasahassaṃ agghāpetvā adāsi. **Atha kaṇhājina**nti kaniṭṭhaṃ pana me kaṇhājinaṃ. **Hatthinā ca satena cā**ti hatthīnañca assānañca usabhānañca nikkhānañcāti sabbesaṃ etesaṃ satena antamaso mañcapīṭhapāduke upādāya sabbasatena agghāpesīti.

Rājā kumārānaṃ nikkayaṃ dāpento āha –

::hangnum
2325\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uṭṭhehi katte taramāno, brāhmaṇassa avākara;
::

::gatha2
Dāsisataṃ dāsasataṃ, gavaṃ hatthusabhaṃ sataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jātarūpasahassañca, puttānaṃ dehi nikkaya’’nti.
::

Tattha **avākarā**ti dehi.

::hangnum
2326\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato kattā taramāno, brāhmaṇassa avākari;
::

::gatha2
Dāsisataṃ dāsasataṃ, gavaṃ hatthusabhaṃ sataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jātarūpasahassañca, puttānaṃdāsi nikkaya’’nti.
::

Tattha **avākarī**ti adāsi. **Nikkaya**nti agghassa mūlaṃ.

Evaṃ brāhmaṇassa sabbasatañca nikkhasahassañca kumārānaṃ nikkayaṃ adāsi, sattabhūmikañca pāsādaṃ, brāhmaṇassa parivāro mahā ahosi. So dhanaṃ paṭisāmetvā pāsādaṃ abhiruyha sādurasabhojanaṃ bhuñjitvā mahāsayane nipajji. Kumāre sīsaṃ nahāpetvā bhojetvā alaṅkaritvā ekaṃ ayyako, ekaṃ ayyikāti dvepi ucchaṅge upavesesuṃ. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2327\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nikkiṇitvā nahāpetvā, bhojayitvāna dārake;
::

::gathalast
Samalaṅkaritvā bhaṇḍena, ucchaṅge upavesayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
2328\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīsaṃ {pb:V:7.0359}{pb:M:7.0366} nhāte {pb:P:6.0578} sucivatthe, sabbābharaṇabhūsite;
::

::gathalast
Rājā aṅke karitvāna, ayyako paripucchatha.
::

::hangnum
2329\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuṇḍale ghusite māle, sabbābharaṇabhūsite;
::

::gathalast
Rājā aṅke karitvāna, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
::

::hangnum
2330\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci ubho arogā te, jāli mātāpitā tava;
::

::gathalast
Kacci uñchena yāpenti, kacci mūlaphalā bahū.
::

::hangnum
2331\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci ḍaṃsā makasā ca, appameva sarīsapā;
::

::gathalast
Vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe, kacci hiṃsā na vijjatī’’ti.
::

Tattha **kuṇḍale**ti kuṇḍalāni pilandhāpetvā. **Ghusite**ti ugghosite manoramaṃ ravaṃ ravante. **Māle**ti pupphāni pilandhāpetvā. **Aṅke karitvānā**ti jālikumāraṃ aṅke nisīdāpetvā.

Kumāro āha –

::hangnum
2332\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atho ubho arogā me, deva mātāpitā mama;
::

::gathalast
Atho uñchena yāpenti, atho mūlaphalā bahū.
::

::hangnum
2333\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atho ḍaṃsā makasā ca, appameva sarīsapā;
::

::gathalast
Vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe, hiṃsā nesaṃ na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
2334\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khaṇantālukalambāni, bilāni takkalāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Kolaṃ bhallātakaṃ bellaṃ, sā no āhatva posati.
::

::hangnum
2335\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yañceva sā āharati, vanamūlaphalahāriyā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ no sabbe samāgantvā, rattiṃ bhuñjāma no divā.
::

::hangnum
2336\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ammāva {pb:V:7.0360} no kisā paṇḍu, āharantī dumapphalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vātātapena sukhumālī, padumaṃ hatthagatāmiva.
::

::hangnum
2337\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ammāya patanū kesā, vicarantyā brahāvane;
::

::gathalast
Vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe, khaggadīpinisevite.
::

::hangnum
2338\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kesesu {pb:M:7.0367} jaṭaṃ bandhitvā, kacche jallamadhārayi;
::

::gathalast
Cammavāsī chamā seti, jātavedaṃ namassatī’’ti.
::

Tattha **khaṇantālukalambānī**ti khaṇantī ālūni ca kalambāni ca. Iminā mātāpitūnaṃ kicchajīvikaṃ vaṇṇeti. **Taṃ no**ti ettha **no**ti nipātamattaṃ. **Padumaṃ hatthagatāmivā**ti hatthena parimadditaṃ padumaṃ viya jātā. **Patanū kesā**ti deva, ammāya me mahāvane vicarantiyā te bhamarapattavaṇṇā kāḷakesā rukkhasākhādīhi viluttā patanū jātā. **Jallamadhārayī**ti ubhohi kacchehi jallaṃ dhāreti, kiliṭṭhavesena vicaratīti.

So evaṃ mātu dukkhitabhāvaṃ kathetvā ayyakaṃ codento imaṃ gāthamāha –

::hangnum
2339\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puttā piyā manussānaṃ, lokasmiṃ udapajjisuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na hi nūnamhākaṃ ayyassa, putte sneho ajāyathā’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:P:6.0579} **udapajjisu**nti uppajjiṃsu.

Tato rājā attano dosaṃ āvikaronto āha –

::hangnum
2340\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dukkaṭañca hi no putta, bhūnahaccaṃ kataṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Yohaṃ sivīnaṃ vacanā, pabbājesimadūsakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2341\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ me kiñci idha atthi, dhanaṃ dhaññañca vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Etu vessantaro rājā, siviraṭṭhe pasāsatū’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:V:7.0361} **puttā**ti putta jāli etaṃ amhākaṃ dukkaṭaṃ. **Bhūnahacca**nti vuḍḍhighātakammaṃ. **Yaṃ me kiñcī**ti tāta, yaṃ me kiñci idha atthi, sabbaṃ te pitu demi. **Siviraṭṭhe pasāsatū**ti imasmiṃ nagare so rājā hutvā pasāsatūti.

Kumāro āha –

::hangnum
2342\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na deva mayhaṃ vacanā, ehiti sivisuttamo;
::

::gathalast
Sayameva devo gantvā, siñca bhogehi atraja’’nti.
::

Tattha **sivisuttamo**ti siviseṭṭho vessantaro. **Siñcā**ti mahāmegho viya vuṭṭhiyā bhogehi abhisiñca.

::hangnum
2343\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:M:7.0368} senāpatiṃ rājā, sañjayo ajjhabhāsatha;
::

::gatha2
Hatthī assā rathā pattī, senā sannāhayantu naṃ;
::

::gathalast
Negamā ca maṃ anventu, brāhmaṇā ca purohitā.
::

::hangnum
2344\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato saṭṭhisahassāni, yodhino cārudassanā;
::

::gathalast
Khippamāyantu sannaddhā, nānāvaṇṇehilaṅkatā.
::

::hangnum
2345\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nīlavatthadharā neke, pītāneke nivāsitā;
::

::gatha2
Aññe lohitauṇhīsā, suddhāneke nivāsitā;
::

::gathalast
Khippamāyantu sannaddhā, nānāvaṇṇehilaṅkatā.
::

::hangnum
2346\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Himavā yathā gandhadharo, pabbato gandhamādano;
::

::gathalast
Nānārukkhehi sañchanno, mahābhūtagaṇālayo.
::

::hangnum
2347\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Osadhehi ca dibbehi, disā bhāti pavāti ca;
::

::gathalast
Khippamāyantu sannaddhā, disā bhantu pavantu ca.
::

::hangnum
2348\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:V:7.0362} nāgasahassāni, yojayantu catuddasa;
::

::gathalast
Suvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā, hemakappanavāsasā.
::

::hangnum
2349\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ārūḷhā gāmaṇīyehi, tomaraṅkusapāṇibhi;
::

::gathalast
Khippamāyantu sannaddhā, hatthikkhandhehi dassitā.
::

::hangnum
2350\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato assasahassāni, yojayantu catuddasa;
::

::gathalast
Ājānīyāva jātiyā, sindhavā sīghavāhanā.
::

::hangnum
2351\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ārūḷhā gāmaṇīyehi, illiyācāpadhāribhi;
::

::gathalast
Khippamāyantu sannaddhā, assapiṭṭhehīlaṅkatā.
::

::hangnum
2352\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:P:6.0580} rathasahassāni, yojayantu catuddasa;
::

::gathalast
Ayosukatanemiyo, suvaṇṇacitapakkhare.
::

::hangnum
2353\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āropentu dhaje tattha, cammāni kavacāni ca;
::

::gatha2
Vippālentu ca cāpāni, daḷhadhammā pahārino;
::

::gathalast
Khippamāyantu sannaddhā, rathesu rathajīvino’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:M:7.0369} **sannāhayantuna**nti sannayhantu. **Saṭṭhisahassānī**ti mama puttena sahajātā saṭṭhisahassā amaccā. **Nīlavatthadharā neke**ti eke nīlavatthanivāsitā hutvā āyantu. **Mahābhūtagaṇālayo**ti bahuyakkhagaṇānaṃ ālayo. **Disā bhantu pavantu cā**ti vuttappakāro himavā viya ābharaṇavilepanādīhi obhāsentu ceva pavāyantu ca. **Hatthikkhandhehī**ti te hatthigāmaṇino hatthikkhandhehi khippamāyantu. **Dassitā**ti dassitavibhūsanā. **Ayosukatanemiyo**ti ayena suṭṭhu parikkhittanemiyo. **Suvaṇṇacitapakkhare**ti suvaṇṇena khacitapakkhare. Evarūpe cuddasa sahasse rathe yojayantūti vadati. **Vippālentū**ti āropentu.

Evaṃ rājā senaṅgaṃ vicāretvā ‘‘puttassa me jetuttaranagarato yāva vaṅkapabbatā aṭṭhusabhavitthāraṃ āgamanamaggaṃ samatalaṃ katvā maggālaṅkāratthāya idañcidañca karothā’’ti āṇāpento āha –

::hangnum
2354\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lājā {pb:V:7.0363} olopiyā pupphā, mālāgandhavilepanā;
::

::gathalast
Agghiyāni ca tiṭṭhantu, yena maggena ehiti.
::

::hangnum
2355\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gāme gāme sataṃ kumbhā, merayassa surāya ca;
::

::gathalast
Maggamhi patitiṭṭhantu, yena maggena ehiti.
::

::hangnum
2356\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maṃsā pūvā saṅkuliyo, kummāsā macchasaṃyutā;
::

::gathalast
Maggamhi patitiṭṭhantu, yena maggena ehiti.
::

::hangnum
2357\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sappi telaṃ dadhi khīraṃ, kaṅgubījā bahū surā;
::

::gathalast
Maggamhi patitiṭṭhantu, yena maggena ehiti.
::

::hangnum
2358\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āḷārikā ca sūdā ca, naṭanaṭṭakagāyino;
::

::gathalast
Pāṇissarā kumbhathūṇiyo, mandakā sokajjhāyikā.
::

::hangnum
2359\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āhaññantu sabbavīṇā, bheriyo dindimāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Kharamukhāni dhamentu, nadantu ekapokkharā.
::

::hangnum
2360\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mudiṅgā paṇavā saṅkhā, godhā parivadentikā;
::

::gathalast
Dindimāni ca haññantu, kutumpadindimāni cā’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:M:7.0370} **lājā olopiyā pupphā**ti lājehi saddhiṃ lājapañcamakāni pupphāni okirantānaṃ okiraṇapupphāni paṭiyādethāti āṇāpeti. **Mālāgandhavilepanā**ti maggavitāne olambakamālā {pb:P:6.0581} ceva gandhavilepanāni ca. **Agghiyāni cā**ti pupphaagghiyāni ceva ratanaagghiyāni ca yena maggena mama putto ehiti, tattha tiṭṭhantu. **Gāme gāme**ti gāmadvāre gāmadvāre. **Patitiṭṭhantū**ti pipāsitānaṃ pivanatthāya paṭiyāditā hutvā surāmerayamajjakumbhā tiṭṭhantu. **Macchasaṃyutā**ti macchehi saṃyuttā. **Kaṅgubījā**ti kaṅgupiṭṭhamayā. **Mandakā**ti mandakagāyino. **Sokajjhāyikā**ti māyākārā, aññepi vā ye keci uppannasokaharaṇasamatthā sokajjhāyikāti vuccanti, socante jane attano vaṃsaghosaparamparānaṃ nacce kate nissoke katvā sayāpakāti attho. **Kharamukhānī**ti sāmuddikamahāmukhasaṅkhā. **Saṅkhā**ti dakkhiṇāvaṭṭā muṭṭhisaṅkhā{pb:V:7.0364}, nāḷisaṅkhāti dve saṅkhā. Godhā parivadentikā dindimāni kutumpadindimānīti imānipi cattāri tūriyāneva.

Evaṃ rājā maggālaṅkārāni vicāresi. Jūjakopi pamāṇātikkantaṃ bhuñjitvā jīrāpetuṃ asakkonto tattheva kālamakāsi. Rājā tassa sarīrakiccaṃ kārāpetvā ‘‘nagare koci brāhmaṇassa ñātako atthi, idaṃ gaṇhātū’’ti bheriṃ carāpesi. Na kañcissa ñātakaṃ passi, dhanaṃ puna raññoyeva ahosi. Atha sattame divase sabbā senā sannipati. Atha rājā mahantena parivārena jāliṃ magganāyakaṃ katvā nikkhami. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2361\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sā senā mahatī āsi, uyyuttā sivivāhinī;
::

::gathalast
Jālinā magganāyena, vaṅkaṃ pāyāsi pabbataṃ.
::

::hangnum
2362\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Koñcaṃ nadati mātaṅgo, kuñjaro saṭṭhihāyano;
::

::gathalast
Kacchāya baddhamānāya, koñcaṃ nadati vāraṇo.
::

::hangnum
2363\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ājānīyā {pb:M:7.0371} hasiyanti, nemighoso ajāyatha;
::

::gathalast
Abbhaṃ rajo acchādesi, uyyuttā sivivāhinī.
::

::hangnum
2364\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sā senā mahatī āsi, uyyuttā hārahārinī;
::

::gathalast
Jālinā magganāyena, vaṅkaṃ pāyāsi pabbataṃ.
::

::hangnum
2365\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te pāviṃsu brahāraññaṃ, bahusākhaṃ mahodakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Puppharukkhehi sañchannaṃ, phalarukkhehi cūbhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2366\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha bindussarā vaggū, nānāvaṇṇā bahū dijā;
::

::gathalast
Kūjantamupakūjanti, utusampupphite dume.
::

::hangnum
2367\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te gantvā dīghamaddhānaṃ, ahorattānamaccaye;
::

::gathalast
Padesaṃ taṃ upāgacchuṃ, yattha vessantaro ahū’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:V:7.0365} **mahatī**ti dvādasaakkhobhaṇisaṅkhātā senā. **Uyyuttā**ti payātā. **Koñcaṃ nadatī**ti tadā kāliṅgaraṭṭhavāsino brāhmaṇā attano raṭṭhe deve vuṭṭhe taṃ nāgaṃ āharitvā sañjayassa adaṃsu. So hatthī ‘‘sāmikaṃ vata passituṃ labhissāmī’’ti tuṭṭho koñcanādamakāsi. Taṃ sandhāyetaṃ vuttaṃ. **Kacchāyā**ti suvaṇṇakacchāya baddhamānāyapi tussitvā koñcaṃ nadati. **Hasiyantī**ti hasasaddamakaṃsu{pb:P:6.0582}. **Hārahārinī**ti haritabbaharaṇasamatthā. **Pāviṃsū**ti pavisiṃsu. **Bahusākha**nti bahurukkhasākhaṃ. **Dīghamaddhāna**nti saṭṭhiyojanamaggaṃ. **Upāgacchu**nti yattha vessantaro ahosi, taṃ padesaṃ upagatāti.

::centre
Mahārājapabbavaṇṇanā niṭṭhitā.
::

#### Chakhattiyakammavaṇṇanā

Jālikumāro mucalindasaratīre khandhāvāraṃ nivāsāpetvā cuddasa rathasahassāni āgatamaggābhimukhāneva ṭhapāpetvā tasmiṃ tasmiṃ padese sīhabyagghadīpiādīsu ārakkhaṃ saṃvidahi. Hatthiādīnaṃ saddo mahā ahosi. Atha mahāsatto taṃ saddaṃ sutvā ‘‘kiṃ nu kho me paccāmittā {pb:M:7.0372} mama pitaraṃ ghātetvā mamatthāya āgatā’’ti maraṇabhayabhīto maddiṃ ādāya pabbataṃ āruyha senaṃ olokesi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2368\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesaṃ sutvāna nigghosaṃ, bhīto vessantaro ahu;
::

::gathalast
Pabbataṃ abhiruhitvā, bhīto senaṃ udikkhati.
::

::hangnum
2369\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iṅgha maddi nisāmehi, nigghoso yādiso vane;
::

::gathalast
Ājānīyā hasiyanti, dhajaggāni ca dissare.
::

::hangnum
2370\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ime nūna araññasmiṃ, migasaṅghāni luddakā;
::

::gatha2
Vāgurāhi parikkhippa, sobbhaṃ pātetvā tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Vikkosamānā tibbāhi, hanti nesaṃ varaṃ varaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2371\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā mayaṃ adūsakā, araññe avaruddhakā;
::

::gathalast
Amittahatthattaṃ gatā, passa dubbalaghātaka’’nti.
::

Tattha {pb:V:7.0366} **iṅghā**ti codanatthe nipāto. **Nisāmehī**ti sakasenā vā parasenā vāti olokehi upadhārehi. ‘‘Ime nūna araññasmi’’ntiādīnaṃ aḍḍhateyyagāthānaṃ evamatthasambandho veditabbo ‘‘maddi yathā araññamhi migasaṅghāni luddakā vāgurāhi parikkhippa atha vā pana sobbhaṃ pātetvā tāvadeva ‘hanatha, are, duṭṭhamige’ti vikkosamānā tibbāhi migamāraṇasattīhi nesaṃ migānaṃ varaṃ varaṃ thūlaṃ thūlaṃ hananti, ime ca nūna tatheva amhe asabbhāhi vācāhi vikkosamānā tibbāti sattīhi hanissanti, mayañca adūsakā araññe avaruddhakā raṭṭhā pabbājitā vane vasāma, evaṃ santepi amittānaṃ hatthattaṃ gatā, passa dubbalaghātaka’’nti. Evaṃ so maraṇabhayena paridevi.

Sā tassa vacanaṃ sutvā senaṃ oloketvā ‘‘sakasenāya bhavitabba’’nti mahāsattaṃ assāsentī imaṃ gāthamāha –

::hangnum
2372\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amittā {pb:P:6.0583} nappasāheyyuṃ, aggīva udakaṇṇave;
::

::gathalast
Tadeva tvaṃ vicintehi, api sotthi ito siyā’’ti.
::

Tattha **aggīva udakaṇṇave**ti yathā tiṇukkādīnaṃ vasena upanīto aggi aṇṇavasaṅkhātāni puthulagambhīrāni udakāni nappasahati, tāpetuṃ na sakkoti{pb:M:7.0373}, tathā taṃ amittā nappasaheyyuṃ nābhibhavissanti. **Tadevā**ti yaṃ sakkena tuyhaṃ varaṃ datvā ‘‘mahārāja, na cirasseva te pitā ehitī’’ti vuttaṃ, tadeva tvaṃ vicintehi, api nāma ito balakāyato amhākaṃ sotthi siyāti mahāsattaṃ assāsesi.

Atha mahāsatto sokaṃ tanukaṃ katvā tāya saddhiṃ pabbatā oruyha paṇṇasālādvāre nisīdi, itarāpi attano paṇṇasālādvāre nisīdi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2373\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato vessantaro rājā, orohitvāna pabbatā;
::

::gathalast
Nisīdi paṇṇasālāyaṃ, daḷhaṃ katvāna mānasa’’nti.
::

Tattha **daḷhaṃ katvāna mānasa**nti mayaṃ pabbajitā nāma, amhākaṃ ko kiṃ karissatīti thiraṃ hadayaṃ katvā nisīdi.

Tasmiṃ {pb:V:7.0367} khaṇe sañjayo rājā deviṃ āmantetvā – ‘‘bhadde, phussati amhesu sabbesu ekato gatesu soko mahā bhavissati, paṭhamaṃ tāva ahaṃ gacchāmi, tato ‘idāni sokaṃ vinodetvā nisinnā bhavissantī’ti sallakkhetvā tvaṃ mahantena parivārena āgaccheyyāsi. Atha thokaṃ kālaṃ vītināmetvā jālikaṇhājinā pacchato āgacchantū’’ti vatvā rathaṃ nivattāpetvā āgatamaggābhimukhaṃ katvā tattha tattha ārakkhaṃ saṃvidahitvā alaṅkatahatthikkhandhato oruyha puttassa santikaṃ agamāsi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2374\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nivattayitvāna rathaṃ, vuṭṭhapetvāna seniyo;
::

::gathalast
Ekaṃ araññe viharantaṃ, pitā puttaṃ upāgami.
::

::hangnum
2375\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthikkhandhato oruyha, ekaṃso pañjalīkato;
::

::gathalast
Parikiṇṇo amaccehi, puttaṃ siñcitumāgami.
::

::hangnum
2376\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatthaddasa kumāraṃ so, rammarūpaṃ samāhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nisinnaṃ paṇṇasālāyaṃ, jhāyantaṃ akutobhaya’’nti.
::

Tattha {pb:M:7.0374} **vuṭṭhapetvāna seniyo**ti ārakkhatthāya balakāye ṭhapetvā. **Ekaṃso**ti ekaṃsakatauttarāsaṅgo. **Siñcitumāgamī**ti rajje abhisiñcituṃ upāgami. **Rammarūpa**nti anañjitaṃ amaṇḍitaṃ.

::hangnum
2377\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañca {pb:P:6.0584} disvāna āyantaṃ, pitaraṃ puttagiddhinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vessantaro ca maddī ca, paccuggantvā avandisuṃ.
::

::hangnum
2378\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maddī ca sirasā pāde, sasurassābhivādayi;
::

::gatha2
Maddī ahañhi te deva, pāde vandāmi te suṇhā;
::

::gathalast
Te su tattha palissajja, pāṇinā parimajjathā’’ti.
::

Tattha **pāde vandāmi te suṇhā**ti ahaṃ, deva, tava suṇhā pāde vandāmīti evaṃ vatvā vandi. **Te su tatthā**ti te ubhopi jane tasmiṃ sakkadattiye assame palissajitvā hadaye nipajjāpetvā sīse paricumbitvā mudukena pāṇinā parimajjatha, piṭṭhiyo nesaṃ parimajji.

Tato {pb:V:7.0368} roditvā paridevitvā rājā soke parinibbute tehi saddhiṃ paṭisanthāraṃ karonto āha –

::hangnum
2379\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci vo kusalaṃ putta, kacci putta anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kacci uñchena yāpetha, kacci mūlaphalā bahū.
::

::hangnum
2380\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci ḍaṃsā makasā ca, appameva sarīsapā;
::

::gathalast
Vane vāḷamigākiṇṇe, kacci hiṃsā na vijjatī’’ti.
::

Pitu vacanaṃ sutvā mahāsatto āha –

::hangnum
2381\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthi no jīvikā deva, sā ca yādisakīdisā;
::

::gathalast
Kasirā jīvikā homa, uñchācariyāya jīvitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2382\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aniddhinaṃ mahārāja, dametassaṃva sārathi;
::

::gathalast
Tyamhā aniddhikā dantā, asamiddhi dameti no.
::

::hangnum
2383\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Api no kisāni maṃsāni, pitu mātu adassanā;
::

::gathalast
Avaruddhānaṃ mahārāja, araññe jīvasokina’’nti.
::

Tattha {pb:M:7.0375} **yādisakīdisā**ti yā vā sā vā, lāmakāti attho. **Kasirā jīvikā homā**ti tāta, amhākaṃ uñchācariyāya jīvitaṃ nāma kicchaṃ, dukkhā no jīvikā ahosi. **Aniddhina**nti mahārāja, aniddhiṃ asamiddhiṃ daliddapurisaṃ nāma sāva aniddhi cheko sārathi assaṃ viya dameti, nibbisevanaṃ karoti, te mayaṃ idha vasantā aniddhikā dantā nibbisevanā katā, asamiddhiyeva no dametīti. ‘‘Dametha no’’tipi pāṭho, damayittha noti attho. **Jīvasokina**nti avigatasokānaṃ araññe vasantānaṃ kiṃ nāma amhākaṃ sukhanti vadati.

Evañca pana vatvā puna puttānaṃ pavattiṃ pucchanto āha –

::hangnum
2384\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yepi {pb:V:7.0369} te siviseṭṭhassa, dāyādāpattamānasā;
::

::gatha2
Jālī kaṇhājinā cubho, brāhmaṇassa vasānugā;
::

::gathalast
Accāyikassa luddassa, yo ne gāvova sumbhati.
::

::hangnum
2385\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te {pb:P:6.0585} rājaputtiyā putte, yadi jānātha saṃsatha;
::

::gathalast
Pariyāpuṇātha no khippaṃ, sappadaṭṭhaṃva māṇava’’nti.
::

Tattha **dāyādāpattamānasā**ti mahārāja, yepi te tava siviseṭṭhassa dāyādā apattamānasā asampuṇṇamanorathā hutvā brāhmaṇassa vasānugā jātā, te dve kumāre yo brāhmaṇo gāvova sumbhati paharati, te rājaputtiyā putte yadi diṭṭhavasena vā sutavasena vā jānātha saṃsatha. **Sappadaṭṭhaṃva māṇava**nti visanimmadanatthāya sappadaṭṭhaṃ māṇavaṃ tikicchantā viya khippaṃ no pariyāpuṇātha kathethāti vadati.

Rājā āha –

::hangnum
2386\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubho kumārā nikkītā, jālī kaṇhājinā cubho;
::

::gathalast
Brāhmaṇassa dhanaṃ datvā, putta mā bhāyi assasā’’ti.
::

Tattha **nikkītā**ti nikkayaṃ datvā gahitā.

Taṃ sutvā mahāsatto paṭiladdhassāso pitarā saddhiṃ paṭisanthāramakāsi –

::hangnum
2387\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci {pb:M:7.0376} nu tāta kusalaṃ, kacci tāta anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kacci nu tāta me mātu, cakkhu na parihāyatī’’ti.
::

Tattha **cakkhu na parihāyatī**ti puttasokena rodantiyā cakkhu na parihāyatīti.

Rājā āha –

::hangnum
2388\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kusalañceva {pb:V:7.0370} me putta, atho putta anāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atho ca putta te mātu, cakkhu na parihāyatī’’ti.
::

Bodhisatto āha –

::hangnum
2389\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci arogaṃ yoggaṃ te, kacci vahati vāhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kacci phīto janapado, kacci vuṭṭhi na chijjatī’’ti.
::

Tattha **vuṭṭhī**ti vuṭṭhidhārā.

Rājā āha –

::hangnum
2390\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atho arogaṃ yoggaṃ me, atho vahati vāhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atho phīto janapado, atho vuṭṭhi na chijjatī’’ti.
::

Evaṃ tesaṃ sallapantānaññeva phussatī devī ‘‘idāni sokaṃ tanukaṃ katvā nisinnā bhavissantī’’ti sallakkhetvā mahāparivārena saddhiṃ puttassa santikaṃ agamāsi. Tamatthaṃ {pb:P:6.0586} pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2391\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iccevaṃ mantayantānaṃ, mātā nesaṃ adissatha;
::

::gathalast
Rājaputtī giridvāre, pattikā anupāhanā.
::

::hangnum
2392\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañca disvāna āyantiṃ, mātaraṃ puttagiddhiniṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vessantaro ca maddī ca, paccuggantvā avandisuṃ.
::

::hangnum
2393\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maddī ca sirasā pāde, sassuyā abhivādayi;
::

::gathalast
Maddī ahañhi te ayye, pāde vandāmi te suṇhā’’ti.
::

Tesaṃ phussatideviṃ vanditvā ṭhitakāle puttakā kumārakumārikāhi parivutā āgamiṃsu. Maddī ca tesaṃ āgamanamaggaṃ olokentīyeva aṭṭhāsi. Sā te sotthinā āgacchante disvā sakabhāvena {pb:V:7.0371} saṇṭhātuṃ {pb:M:7.0377} asakkontī taruṇavacchā viya gāvī paridevamānā tato pāyāsi. Tepi taṃ disvā paridevantā mātarābhimukhāva padhāviṃsu. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2394\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maddiñca puttakā disvā, dūrato sotthimāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Kandantā mabhidhāviṃsu, vacchabālāva mātaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
2395\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maddī ca puttake disvā, dūrato sotthimāgate;
::

::gathalast
Vāruṇīva pavedhentī, thanadhārābhisiñcathā’’ti.
::

Tattha **kandantā mabhidhāviṃsū**ti kandantā abhidhāviṃsu. **Vāruṇīvā**ti yakkhāviṭṭhā ikkhaṇikā viya pavedhamānā thanadhārā abhisiñcathāti.

Sā kira mahāsaddena paridevitvā kampamānā visaññī hutvā dīghato pathaviyaṃ pati. Kumārāpi vegenāgantvā visaññino hutvā mātu upariyeva patiṃsu. Tasmiṃ khaṇe tassā dvīhi thanehi dve khīradhārā nikkhamitvā tesaṃ mukheyeva pavisiṃsu. Sace kira ettako assāso nābhavissa, dve kumārā sukkhahadayā hutvā addhā nassissanti. Vessantaropi piyaputte disvā sokaṃ sandhāretuṃ asakkonto visaññī hutvā tattheva pati. Mātāpitaropissa visaññino hutvā tattheva patiṃsu, tathā sahajātā saṭṭhisahassā amaccā. Taṃ kāruññaṃ passantesu ekopi sakabhāvena saṇṭhātuṃ nāsakkhi. Sakalaṃ assamapadaṃ yugantavātena pamadditaṃ viya sālavanaṃ ahosi. Tasmiṃ khaṇe pabbatā nadiṃsu, mahāpathavī kampi, mahāsamuddo saṅkhubhi, sineru girirājā onami. Cha kāmāvacaradevalokā ekakolāhalā ahesuṃ.

Sakko devarājā ‘‘cha khattiyā saparisā visaññino jātā, tesu ekopi uṭṭhāya kassaci sarīre udakaṃ siñcituṃ samattho nāma natthi, ahaṃ dāni imesaṃ pokkharavassaṃ vassāpessāmī’’ti cintetvā chakhattiyasamāgame pokkharavassaṃ vassāpesi. Tattha ye temitukāmā, te tementi, atemitukāmānaṃ upari ekabindumattampi na patati, padumapattato udakaṃ viya nivattitvā gacchati. Iti pokkharavane patitaṃ {pb:M:7.0378} vassaṃ viya taṃ vassaṃ ahosi. Cha khattiyā {pb:P:6.0587} assāsaṃ paṭilabhiṃsu. Mahājano tampi disvā ‘‘aho acchariyaṃ, aho abbhutaṃ evarūpe ñātisamāgame pokkharavassaṃ vassi, mahāpathavī kampī’’ti acchariyaṃ pavedesi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2396\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samāgatānaṃ {pb:V:7.0372} ñātīnaṃ, mahāghoso ajāyatha;
::

::gathalast
Pabbatā samanādiṃsu, mahī pakampitā ahu.
::

::hangnum
2397\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vuṭṭhidhāraṃ pavattento, devo pāvassi tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Atha vessantaro rājā, ñātīhi samagacchatha.
::

::hangnum
2398\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nattāro suṇisā putto, rājā devī ca ekato;
::

::gathalast
Yadā samāgatā āsuṃ, tadāsi lomahaṃsanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2399\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañjalikā tassa yācanti, rodantā bherave vane;
::

::gatha2
Vessantarañca maddiñca, sabbe raṭṭhā samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Tvaṃ nosi issaro rājā, rajjaṃ kāretha no ubho’’ti.
::

Tattha **ghoso**ti kāruññaghoso. **Pañjalikā**ti sabbe nāgarā ceva negamā ca jānapadā ca paggahitañjalikā hutvā. **Tassa yācantī**ti tassa pādesu patitvā roditvā kanditvā ‘‘deva, tvaṃ no sāmi issaro, pitā te idheva abhisiñcitvā nagaraṃ netukāmo, kulasantakaṃ setacchattaṃ paṭicchathā’’ti yāciṃsu.

::centre
Chakhattiyakammavaṇṇanā niṭṭhitā.
::

#### Nagarakaṇḍavaṇṇanā

Taṃ sutvā mahāsatto pitarā saddhiṃ sallapanto imaṃ gāthamāha –

::hangnum
2400\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammena rajjaṃ kārentaṃ, raṭṭhā pabbājayittha maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tvañca jānapadā ceva, negamā ca samāgatā’’ti.
::

Tato {pb:M:7.0379} rājā puttaṃ attano dosaṃ khamāpento āha –

::hangnum
2401\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dukkaṭañca {pb:V:7.0373} hi no putta, bhūnahaccaṃ kataṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Yohaṃ sivīnaṃ vacanā, pabbājesimadūsaka’’nti.
::

Imaṃ gāthaṃ vatvā attano dukkhaharaṇatthaṃ puttaṃ yācanto itaraṃ gāthamāha –

::hangnum
2402\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yena kenaci vaṇṇena, pitu dukkhaṃ udabbahe;
::

::gathalast
Mātu bhaginiyā cāpi, api pāṇehi attano’’ti.
::

Tattha **udabbahe**ti hareyya. **Api pāṇehī**ti tāta puttena nāma jīvitaṃ pariccajitvāpi mātāpitūnaṃ sokadukkhaṃ haritabbaṃ, tasmā mama dosaṃ hadaye akatvā mama vacanaṃ karohi, imaṃ isiliṅgaṃ hāretvā rājavesaṃ gaṇha tātāti iminā kira naṃ adhippāyenevamāha.

Bodhisatto {pb:P:6.0588} rajjaṃ kāretukāmopi ‘‘ettake pana akathite garukaṃ nāma na hotī’’ti kathesi. Mahāsatto ‘‘sādhū’’ti sampaṭicchi. Athassa adhivāsanaṃ viditvā sahajātā saṭṭhisahassā amaccā ‘‘nahānakālo mahārāja, rajojallaṃ pavāhayā’’ti vadiṃsu. Atha ne mahāsatto ‘‘thokaṃ adhivāsethā’’ti vatvā paṇṇasālaṃ pavisitvā isibhaṇḍaṃ omuñcitvā paṭisāmetvā saṅkhavaṇṇasāṭakaṃ nivāsetvā paṇṇasālato nikkhamitvā ‘‘idaṃ mayā nava māse aḍḍhamāsañca vasantena samaṇadhammassa kataṭṭhānaṃ, pāramīkūṭaṃ gaṇhantena mayā dānaṃ datvā mahāpathaviyā kampāpitaṭṭhāna’’nti paṇṇasālaṃ tikkhattuṃ padakkhiṇaṃ katvā pañcapatiṭṭhitena vanditvā aṭṭhāsi. Athassa kappakādayo kesamassukammādīni kariṃsu. Tamenaṃ sabbābharaṇabhūsitaṃ devarājānamiva virocamānaṃ rajje abhisiñciṃsu. Tena vuttaṃ –

::hangnum
2403\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato vessantaro rājā, rajojallaṃ pavāhayi;
::

::gathalast
Rajojallaṃ pavāhetvā, saṅkhavaṇṇaṃ adhārayī’’ti.
::

Tattha **pavāhayī**ti hāresi, hāretvā ca pana rājavesaṃ gaṇhīti attho.

Athassa yaso mahā ahosi. Olokitaolokitaṭṭhānaṃ kampati, mukhamaṅgalikā mukhamaṅgalāni ghosayiṃsu, sabbatūriyāni paggaṇhiṃsu, mahāsamuddakucchiyaṃ {pb:M:7.0380} meghagajjitaghoso viya tūriyaghoso ahosi. Hatthiratanaṃ alaṅkaritvā upānayiṃsu. So khaggaratanaṃ bandhitvā hatthiratanaṃ {pb:V:7.0374} abhiruhi. Tāvadeva naṃ sahajātā saṭṭhisahassā amaccā sabbālaṅkārappaṭimaṇḍitā parivārayiṃsu, sabbakaññāyo maddidevimpi nahāpetvā alaṅkaritvā abhisiñciṃsu. Sīse ca panassā abhisekaudakaṃ abhisiñcamānā ‘‘vessantaro taṃ pāletū’’tiādīni maṅgalāni vadiṃsu. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2404\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīsaṃ nhāto sucivattho, sabbābharaṇabhūsito;
::

Paccayaṃ nāgamāruyha, khaggaṃ bandhi parantapaṃ.

::hangnum
2405\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato saṭṭhisahassāni, yodhino cārudassanā;
::

::gathalast
Sahajātā pakiriṃsu, nandayantā rathesabhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2406\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:P:6.0589} maddimpi nhāpesuṃ, sivikaññā samāgatā;
::

::gatha2
Vessantaro taṃ pāletu, jālī kaṇhājinā cubho;
::

::gathalast
Athopi taṃ mahārājā, sañjayo abhirakkhatū’’ti.
::

Tattha **paccayaṃ nāgamāruyhā**ti taṃ attano jātadivase uppannaṃ hatthināgaṃ. **Parantapa**nti amittatāpanaṃ. **Pakiriṃsū**ti parivārayiṃsu. **Nandayantā**ti tosentā. **Sivikaññā**ti sivirañño pajāpatiyo sannipatitvā gandhodakena nhāpesuṃ. **Jālī kaṇhājinā cubho**ti ime te puttāpi mātaraṃ rakkhantūti.

::hangnum
2407\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idañca paccayaṃ laddhā, pubbe saṃklesamattano;
::

::gathalast
Ānandiyaṃ ācariṃsu, ramaṇīye giribbaje.
::

::hangnum
2408\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idañca paccayaṃ laddhā, pubbe saṃklesamattano;
::

::gathalast
Ānandi vittā sumanā, putte saṅgamma lakkhaṇā.
::

::hangnum
2409\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idañca paccayaṃ laddhā, pubbe saṃklesamattano;
::

::gathalast
Ānandi vittā patītā, saha puttehi lakkhaṇā’’ti.
::

Tattha **idañca paccayaṃ laddhā**ti bhikkhave, vessantaro maddī ca idañca paccayaṃ laddhā imaṃ patiṭṭhaṃ {pb:V:7.0375} labhitvā, rajje patiṭṭhahitvāti attho. **Pubbe**ti ito {pb:M:7.0381} pubbe attano vanavāsasaṃklesañca anussaritvā. **Ānandiyaṃ ācariṃsu, ramaṇīye giribbaje**ti ramaṇīye vaṅkagirikucchimhi ‘‘vessantarassa rañño āṇā’’ti kañcanalatāvinaddhaṃ ānandabheriṃ carāpetvā ānandachaṇaṃ ācariṃsu. **Ānandi vittā sumanā**ti lakkhaṇasampannā maddī putte saṅgamma sampāpuṇitvā vittā sumanā hutvā ativiya nandīti attho. **Patītā**ti somanassā hutvā.

Evaṃ patītā hutvā ca pana putte āha –

::hangnum
2410\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekabhattā pure āsiṃ, niccaṃ thaṇḍilasāyinī;
::

::gathalast
Iti metaṃ vataṃ āsi, tumhaṃ kāmā hi puttakā.
::

::hangnum
2411\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ me vataṃ samiddhajja, tumhe saṅgamma puttakā;
::

::gatha2
Mātujampi taṃ pāletu, pitujampi ca puttaka;
::

::gathalast
Athopi taṃ mahārājā, sañjayo abhirakkhatu.
::

::hangnum
2412\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kiñcitthi kataṃ puññaṃ, mayhañceva pitucca te;
::

::gathalast
Sabbena tena kusalena, ajaro amaro bhavā’’ti.
::

Tattha **tumhaṃ kāmā hi puttakā**ti puttakā ahaṃ tumhākaṃ kāmā tumhe patthayamānā pure tumhesu brāhmaṇena nītesu ekabhattaṃ bhuñjitvā bhūmiyaṃ sayiṃ, iti me tumhākaṃ kāmā etaṃ vataṃ āsīti vadati. **Samiddhajjā**ti taṃ me vataṃ ajja samiddhaṃ. **Mātujampi taṃ pāletu, pitujampi ca puttakā**ti puttajāli taṃ mātujātaṃ somanassampi pitujātaṃ somanassampi pāletu, mātāpitūnaṃ santakaṃ puññaṃ taṃ pāletūti attho. Tenevāha **‘‘yaṃ kiñcitthi kataṃ puñña’’**nti.

Phussatīpi {pb:P:6.0590} devī ‘‘ito paṭṭhāya mama suṇhā imāneva vatthāni nivāsetu, imāni ābharaṇāni dhāretū’’ti suvaṇṇasamugge pūretvā pahiṇi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2413\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kappāsikañca koseyyaṃ, khomakoṭumbarāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Sassu suṇhāya pāhesi, yehi maddī asobhatha.
::

::hangnum
2414\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:V:7.0376}{pb:M:7.0382} hemañca kāyūraṃ, gīveyyaṃ ratanāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sassu suṇhāya pāhesi, yehi maddī asobhatha.
::

::hangnum
2415\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato hemañca kāyūraṃ, aṅgadaṃ maṇimekhalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sassu suṇhāya pāhesi, yehi maddī asobhatha.
::

::hangnum
2416\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uṇṇataṃ mukhaphullañca, nānāratte ca māṇike;
::

::gathalast
Sassu suṇhāya pāhesi, yehi maddī asobhatha.
::

::hangnum
2417\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uggatthanaṃ giṅgamakaṃ, mekhalaṃ pāṭipādakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sassu suṇhāya pāhesi, yehi maddī asobhatha.
::

::hangnum
2418\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suttañca suttavajjañca, upanijjhāya seyyasi;
::

::gathalast
Asobhatha rājaputtī, devakaññāva nandane.
::

::hangnum
2419\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīsaṃ nhātā sucivatthā, sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā;
::

::gathalast
Asobhatha rājaputtī, tāvatiṃseva accharā.
::

::hangnum
2420\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kadalīva vātacchupitā, jātā cittalatāvane;
::

::gathalast
Antāvaraṇasampannā, rājaputtī asobhatha.
::

::hangnum
2421\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakuṇī mānusinīva, jātā cittapattā patī;
::

::gathalast
Nigrodhapakkabimboṭṭhī, rājaputtī asobhathā’’ti.
::

Tattha **hemañca kāyūra**nti suvaṇṇamayaṃ vanakhajjūriphalasaṇṭhānaṃ gīvāpasādhanameva. **Ratanamaya**nti aparampi ratanamayaṃ gīveyyaṃ. **Aṅgadaṃ maṇimekhala**nti aṅgadābharaṇañca maṇimayamekhalañca. **Uṇṇata**nti ekaṃ nalāṭapasādhanaṃ. **Mukhaphulla**nti nalāṭante tilakamālābharaṇaṃ. **Nānāratte**ti nānāvaṇṇe. **Māṇike**ti maṇimaye. **Uggatthanaṃ giṅgamaka**nti etānipi dve ābharaṇāni. **Mekhala**nti suvaṇṇarajatamayaṃ mekhalaṃ. **Pāṭipādaka**nti pādapasādhanaṃ. **Suttañca suttavajjaṃ cā**ti suttārūḷhañca asuttārūḷhañca pasādhanaṃ. Pāḷiyaṃ pana ‘‘suppañca suppavajjañcā’’ti {pb:V:7.0377} likhitaṃ. **Upanijjhāya seyyasī**ti etaṃ suttārūḷhañca asuttārūḷhañca ābharaṇaṃ taṃ taṃ ūnaṭṭhānaṃ oloketvā alaṅkaritvā ṭhitā seyyasī uttamarūpadharā maddī devakaññāva nandane asobhatha. **Vātacchupitā**ti cittalatāvane jātā vātasamphuṭṭhā suvaṇṇakadalī viya taṃ divasaṃ sā vijambhamānā asobhatha{pb:M:7.0383}. **Dantāvaraṇasampannā**ti bimbaphalasadisehi rattadantāvaraṇehi samannāgatā. **Sakuṇī mānusinīva, jātā cittapattā patī**ti yathā mānusiyā sarīrena {pb:P:6.0591} jātā mānusinī nāma sakuṇī cittapattā ākāse uppatamānā pakkhe pasāretvā gacchantī sobhati, evaṃ sā rattoṭṭhatāya nigrodhapakkabimbaphalasadisaoṭṭhehi asobhatha.

Saṭṭhisahassā amaccā maddiṃ abhiruhanatthāya sabbālaṅkārappaṭimaṇḍitaṃ nātivaddhaṃ sattisarapahārakkhamaṃ ekaṃ taruṇahatthiṃ upanāmesuṃ. Tena vuttaṃ –

::hangnum
2422\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassā ca nāgamānesuṃ, nātivaddhaṃva kuñjaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sattikkhamaṃ sarakkhamaṃ, īsādantaṃ urūḷhavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2423\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sā maddī nāgamāruhi, nātivaddhaṃva kuñjaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sattikkhamaṃ sarakkhamaṃ, īsādantaṃ urūḷhava’’nti.
::

Tattha **tassā cā**ti bhikkhave, tassāpi maddiyā sabbālaṅkārappaṭimaṇḍitaṃ katvā nātivaddhaṃ sattisarapahārakkhamaṃ ekaṃ taruṇahatthiṃ upanesuṃ. **Nāgamāruhī**ti varahatthipiṭṭhiṃ abhiruhi.

Iti te ubhopi mahantena yasena khandhāvāraṃ agamaṃsu. Sañjayarājā dvādasahi akkhobhiṇīhi saddhiṃ māsamattaṃ pabbatakīḷaṃ vanakīḷaṃ kīḷi. Mahāsattassa tejena tāvamahante araññe koci vāḷamigo vā pakkhī vā kañci na viheṭhesi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2424\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbamhi taṃ araññamhi, yāvantettha migā ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vessantarassa tejena, naññamaññaṃ viheṭhayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
2425\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbamhi taṃ araññamhi, yāvantettha dijā ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vessantarassa tejena, naññamaññaṃ viheṭheyuṃ.
::

::hangnum
2426\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbamhi {pb:V:7.0378} taṃ araññamhi, yāvantettha migā ahuṃ;
::

::gatha2
Ekajjhaṃ sannipātiṃsu, vessantare payātamhi;
::

::gathalast
Sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane.
::

::hangnum
2427\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbamhi {pb:M:7.0384} taṃ araññamhi, yāvantettha dijā ahuṃ;
::

::gatha2
Ekajjhaṃ sannipātiṃsu, vessantare payātamhi;
::

::gathalast
Sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane.
::

::hangnum
2428\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbamhi taṃ araññamhi, yāvantettha migā ahuṃ;
::

::gatha2
Nāssu mañjū nikūjiṃsu, vessantare payātamhi;
::

::gathalast
Sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane.
::

::hangnum
2429\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbamhi taṃ araññamhi, yāvantettha dijā ahuṃ;
::

::gatha2
Nāssu mañjū nikūjiṃsu, vessantare payātamhi;
::

::gathalast
Sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane’’ti.
::

Tattha **yāvantetthā**ti yāvanto ettha. **Ekajjhaṃ sannipātiṃsū**ti ekasmiṃ ṭhāne sannipatiṃsu, sannipatitvā ca pana ‘‘ito paṭṭhāya idāni amhākaṃ aññamaññaṃ lajjā vā hirottappaṃ vā saṃvaro vā na bhavissatī’’ti domanassapattā ahesuṃ. **Nāssu mañjū nikūjiṃsū**ti mahāsattassa viyogadukkhitā madhuraṃ ravaṃ pubbe viya na raviṃsu.

Sañjayanarindo {pb:P:6.0592} māsamattaṃ pabbatakīḷaṃ, vanakīḷaṃ kīḷitvā senāpatiṃ pakkosāpetvā ‘‘tāta, ciraṃ no araññe vuttaṃ, kiṃ te mama puttassa gamanamaggo alaṅkato’’ti pucchitvā ‘‘āma, deva, kālo vo gamanāyā’’ti vutte vessantarassa ārocāpetvā senaṃ ādāya nikkhami. Vaṅkagirikucchito yāva jetuttaranagarā saṭṭhiyojanaṃ alaṅkatamaggaṃ mahāsatto mahantena parivārena saddhiṃ paṭipajji. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2430\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭiyatto rājamaggo, vicitto pupphasanthato;
::

::gathalast
Vasi vessantaro yattha, yāvatāva jetuttarā.
::

::hangnum
2431\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato {pb:V:7.0379} saṭṭhisahassāni, yodhino cārudassanā;
::

::gatha2
Samantā parikiriṃsu, vessantare payātamhi;
::

::gathalast
Sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane.
::

::hangnum
2432\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Orodhā {pb:M:7.0385} ca kumārā ca, vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā;
::

::gatha2
Samantā parikiriṃsu, vessantare payātamhi;
::

::gathalast
Sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane.
::

::hangnum
2433\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthārohā anīkaṭṭhā, rathikā pattikārakā;
::

::gatha2
Samantā parikiriṃsu, vessantare payātamhi;
::

::gathalast
Sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane.
::

::hangnum
2434\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samāgatā jānapadā, negamā ca samāgatā;
::

::gatha2
Samantā parikiriṃsu, vessantare payātamhi;
::

::gathalast
Sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane.
::

::hangnum
2435\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Karoṭiyā cammadharā, illīhatthā suvammino;
::

::gatha2
Purato paṭipajjiṃsu, vessantare payātamhi;
::

::gathalast
Sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane’’ti.
::

Tattha **paṭiyatto**ti visākhāpuṇṇamapūjākāle viya alaṅkato. **Vicitto**ti kadalipuṇṇaghaṭadhajapaṭākādīhi vicitto. **Pupphasanthato**ti lājāpañcamakehi pupphehi santhato. **Yatthā**ti yasmiṃ vaṅkapabbate vessantaro vasati, tato paṭṭhāya yāva jetuttaranagarā nirantaraṃ alaṅkatappaṭiyattova. **Karoṭiyā**ti sīsakaroṭīti laddhanāmāya sīse paṭimukkakaroṭikā yodhā. **Cammadharā**ti kaṇḍavāraṇacammadharā. **Suvammino**ti vicitrāhi jālikāhi suṭṭhu vammikā. **Purato paṭipajjiṃsū**ti mattahatthīsupi āgacchantesu anivattino sūrayodhā rañño vessantarassa purato paṭipajjiṃsu.

Rājā saṭṭhiyojanamaggaṃ dvīhi māsehi atikkamma jetuttaranagaraṃ patto alaṅkatappaṭiyattanagaraṃ pavisitvā pāsādaṃ abhiruhi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2436\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te {pb:V:7.0380} pāvisuṃ puraṃ rammaṃ, mahāpākāratoraṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upetaṃ annapānehi, naccagītehi cūbhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
2437\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vittā {pb:M:7.0386} jānapadā āsuṃ, negamā ca samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Anuppatte kumāramhi, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane.
::

::hangnum
2438\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Celukkhepo avattittha, āgate dhanadāyake;
::

::gathalast
Nandiṃ pavesi nagare, bandhanā mokkho aghosathā’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:P:6.0593} **mahāpākāratoraṇa**nti mahantehi pākārehi ca toraṇehi ca samannāgataṃ. **Naccagītehi cūbhaya**nti naccehi ca gītehi ca ubhayehi samannāgataṃ. **Vittā**ti tuṭṭhā somanassappattā. **Āgate dhanadāyake**ti mahājanassa dhanadāyake mahāsatte āgate. **Nandiṃ pavesī**ti ‘‘vessantarassa mahārājassa āṇā’’ti nagare nandibherī cari. **Bandhanā mokkho aghosathā**ti sabbasattānaṃ bandhanā mokkho ghosito. Antamaso biḷāraṃ upādāya vessantaramahārājā sabbasatte bandhanā vissajjāpesi.

So nagaraṃ paviṭṭhadivaseyeva paccūsakāle cintesi ‘‘ye vibhātāya rattiyā mama āgatabhāvaṃ sutvā yācakā āgamissanti, tesāhaṃ kiṃ dassāmī’’ti? Tasmiṃ khaṇe sakkassa bhavanaṃ uṇhākāraṃ dassesi. So āvajjento taṃ kāraṇaṃ ñatvā tāvadeva rājanivesanassa purimavatthuñca pacchimavatthuñca kaṭippamāṇaṃ pūrento ghanamegho viya sattaratanavassaṃ vassāpesi, sakalanagare jāṇuppamāṇaṃ vassāpesi. Punadivase mahāsatto ‘‘tesaṃ tesaṃ kulānaṃ purimapacchimavatthūsu vuṭṭhadhanaṃ tesaṃ tesaññeva hotū’’ti dāpetvā avasesaṃ āharāpetvā attano gehavatthusmiṃ saddhiṃ dhanena koṭṭhāgāresu okirāpetvā dānamukhe ṭhapesi. Tamatthaṃ pakāsento satthā āha –

::hangnum
2439\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jātarūpamayaṃ vassaṃ, devo pāvassi tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Vessantare paviṭṭhamhi, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane.
::

::hangnum
2440\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tato vessantaro rājā, dānaṃ datvāna khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Kāyassa bhedā sappañño, saggaṃ so upapajjathā’’ti.
::

Tattha {pb:V:7.0381}{pb:M:7.0387} **saggaṃ so upapajjathā**ti tato cuto dutiyacittena tusitapure uppajjīti.

::centre
Nagarakaṇḍavaṇṇanā niṭṭhitā.
::

Satthā imaṃ gāthāsahassappaṭimaṇḍitaṃ mahāvessantaradhammadesanaṃ āharitvā jātakaṃ samodhānesi – ‘‘tadā jūjako devadatto ahosi, amittatāpanā ciñcamāṇavikā, cetaputto channo, accutatāpaso sāriputto, sakko anuruddho, sañcayanarindo suddhodanamahārājā, phussatī devī sirimahāmāyā, maddī devī rāhulamātā, jālikumāro rāhulo, kaṇhājinā uppalavaṇṇā, sesaparisā buddhaparisā, mahāvessantaro rājā pana ahameva sammāsambuddho ahosi’’nti.

::centre
Vessantarajātakavaṇṇanā dasamā.
::

::centre
Mahānipātavaṇṇanā niṭṭhitā.
::

::centre
Jātaka-aṭṭhakathā samattā.
::
